#### Murmur of What Was
*Divination cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 15.0 feet
**Components:** V
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You briefly attune your perception to faint residual impressions left upon a location.

You hear a single whispered sentence in a language you understand, originating from a creature that occupied your current space within the last 24 hours. The sentence is indistinct, fragmentary, and chosen by the GM. It may be relevant, trivial, misleading, or devoid of context.

If no creature has occupied the area within that time, you instead perceive a vague and meaningless murmur with no discernible content.

This spell does not reveal the identity, nature, or number of creatures that produced the impression.

You conjure a small, ancient mussel in your hand—enchanted, annoyed, and tightly sealed shut. If anyone tries to pry it open, it vanishes with a faint salty pop, leaving behind only a briny scent.

If spoken to gently and respectfully, the mussel may whisper a cryptic phrase in an ancient tongue or forgotten accent. These utterances are rarely useful and often nonsense, though occasionally they align with bizarre truths.

Once conjured, the mussel lasts for 1 minute or until it disappears. It may be placed on surfaces, used as a very passive familiar, or simply admired.

#### Oxidized Strike
*Necromancy cantrip*

You channel the corrosive forces of decay into your strike, touching a creature’s armor or weapon with a touch imbued with necrotic energy. **Components:** V, S

You create a faint, distorted trace of someone who recently handled an object. A ghostly outline of their hands or footprints lingers faintly, fading slowly over the duration. This effect does not reveal the person’s identity but may suggest their presence.

#### Poltergust
*Illusion cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 10.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You gesture subtly, and a phantasmal breeze whispers through an area you can see within range. Curtains billow, candles flicker, papers shift, and cold air brushes the skin. Though entirely illusory, the sensation feels real—enough to distract, unnerve, or suggest a presence unseen.- The wind cannot cause harm or move objects heavier than 5 lbs.- Creatures within the area instinctively glance around. If they are unaware of you or expecting stealth, you may gain advantage on your next Charisma (Deception or Performance) or Dexterity (Stealth) check against them before the end of your next turn.

This 0-Cantrip is often used to haunt, mislead, or emphasize one’s words, and is popular among illusionists, tricksters, and dramatists alike.

#### Psyblade
*Evocation cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 bonus action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You conjure a shimmering blade of psychic energy in your hand, forged from your focused will. Choose any melee weapon form you are proficient with (no ammunition or thrown weapons). The Psyblade takes that shape but is weightless, emits faint mental whispers, and deals force damage instead of its usual type.

You can use your Wisdom modifier instead of Strength or Dexterity for attack and damage rolls with this weapon.

The damage die starts at 1d4 and improves as you gain Psionic levels, following the Monk’s Martial Arts die:
Additional Properties:
- The blade vanishes if it leaves your hand, if you cast this spell again, or if you dismiss it (no action required).
- The Psyblade is magical, counts as a spellcasting focus, and can be used as the delivery method for Psionic Cantrips.
- When you take the Attack action, you may forgo one attack to cast a Psionic cantrip through the blade, targeting the same creature.
### Psyblade Damage Die Progression

| Psionic Level | Psyblade Damage Die |
|--------------- |---------------------- |
| 1–4 | 1d4 |
| 5–10 | 1d6 |
| 11–16 | 1d8 |
| 17+ | 1d10 |

#### Pummel Stone
*Conjuration cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You summon a chunk of stone or brick from the earth beneath you, hurling it toward a target with magical force. The rocky projectile strikes with an explosive impact.- Ranged spell attack: Make a ranged spell attack against a target. On a hit, the target takes 1d8 bludgeoning damage from the stone.- The target must make a Strength saving throw (DC equals your spellcasting ability modifier) or be knocked prone by the force of the impact.

- 5th level: The damage increases to 2d8 impact, and the range of the spell increases to 60 feet.- 11th level: The spell deals 3d8 bludgeoning damage, and the target is stunned until the end of their next turn on a failed saving throw.

#### Radiant Shine

**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You call upon divine radiance to flare from the gilded surface of the marble beneath you. #### Rail Arc
*Evocation cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You awaken the latent fury sleeping within worked metal, calling a violent spark along iron veins, rails, or bound steel nearby. The metal answers with a sudden crack of lightning, leaping outward to punish those too close.

Creatures near the charged metal suffer the bite of the spark, and those clad in steel or gripping iron draw the wrath more fiercely, as the metal itself conspires to betray them. The air snaps and hums in the aftermath, carrying the scent of scorched stone and ringing iron.

#### Resonant Clang
*Evocation cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 15.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You focus the sound of your steps and amplify the resonant clatter of metal beneath you, creating a sharp, ringing clang that reverberates through the environment. The disruptive noise causes nearby creatures to lose focus and become disoriented.- Creatures within a 15- foot radius of the source must make a Constitution saving throw or take 1d6 sound damage and have disadvantage on Perception checks for the next minute as they struggle to recover from the ringing.- The sound effects can be heard clearly through solid objects, and creatures within range must make a second saving throw if they are engaged in any concentration spells or abilities. On a failure, their concentration is broken.

#### Reverb Cloak
*Illusion cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You attune your presence to the resonating echoes of the surrounding environment, causing your form to distort and flicker like a ripple in sound. In places with reflective or hollow surfaces, such as concrete tunnels or other echoing terrains, your form becomes harder to focus on, creating confusion and uncertainty.- The first attack against you each round has disadvantage, as your form fluctuates within the echoes, making it difficult for enemies to track your exact location.- While the spell lasts, you gain advantage on Stealth checks to hide in areas with echoing acoustics, such as tunnels, caves, or large, noisy chambers.

#### Rhythmic Movement
*Conjuration cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 rounds

The natural flow of the parquet wood beneath you guides your movements as you flicker momentarily between positions, destabilizing your form and reappearing in a more advantageous stance.- You gain advantage on your next Dexterity (Acrobatics) check or melee attack roll made before the end of your next turn.- If you are within 5 feet of a surface or object (like a wall or ledge), you can use your bonus action to teleport up to 10 feet in any direction within range. This teleportation does not provoke opportunity attacks.

#### Runes of Inconsequence
*Illusion cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You inscribe a rune onto a piece of paper, document, or surface. The rune hums with unstable magical nonsense, waiting for the next creature to read or open the marked object. When triggered, the rune unleashes a harmless but dramatic effect that startles, annoys, or mildly entertains.

The effect is randomly determined by rolling a d6:

The rune fades after being triggered. A creature that succeeds a DC 13 Arcana check while inspecting the document can spot the rune before triggering it.
d6 | Harmless Effect
--- |---------------- 
1 | A burst of confetti and a trumpet fanfare plays.
2 | The reader hears a magical raspberry blown directly into their ear.
3 | A tiny banner pops out: “Gotcha!”
4 | The paper insults the reader in a refined accent.
5 | Glitter explodes everywhere. It sticks.
6 | A small illusory bird flaps out and poops ghost ink on them.

#### Sanguine Ink
*Necromancy cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You conjure a thin line of crimson ink, written in your own blood, onto a surface within reach. The writing is in a language you know and can be as fine or elaborate as desired. You can erase the writing at will, but others cannot remove it by mundane means. The ink dries immediately and cannot be smudged. If used on a creature’s skin, it fades naturally in 24 hours.

#### Scorned Mark
*Illusion cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You inscribe an invisible sigil onto a creature or surface—an anomalous imprint that flickers just outside visible light. The mark is imperceptible to normal senses but can be perceived by you, and by others under the effects of an attunement protocol (such as *Reveal Transmission*, *Trace Anomaly*, or *See the Unseen*). 

You may choose one of the following effects for the mark: 
- It emits a subtle warmth or chill to those who touch it. 
- It causes a sense of unease or dread when handled. 
- It makes the marked object feel subtly *wrong* to the attuned. 

If placed on a creature, the mark persists until the duration ends or the target takes fire damage (1 HP or more). The sigil has no impact on gameplay unless revealed, but its presence may trigger paranormal sensors, bureaucratic alarms, or ritual interactions.

#### Season
*Transmutation cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You subtly alter the taste, aroma, and temperature of a small amount of food or liquid within range. You can make bland food flavorful, warm or chill it, and remove minor unpleasant qualities, but this spell does not neutralize poison, disease, or magical effects.

#### Seduce Hollows
*Necromancy cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 10.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 24 hourss

A binding ritual forces one or more undead entities into total compliance with the caster’s physical or emotional desires.

- The undead must make a Charisma saving throw. On a failed save, they cannot resist the caster’s commands for the duration.
- If forced into pleasurable acts, they take 1d6 fire damage per instance of forced compliance.
- This spell is illegal under A.S.T.R.A.L. anomaly regulations and has severe ethical consequences.

#### Severed Whisper
*Enchantment cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You invoke the name of something lost to time, letting its voice slip through your own. A creature of your choice within range hears a whisper from the void. It must make a Wisdom saving throw or become momentarily overwhelmed, causing it to miss the next verbal component it attempts to use before the start of your next turn. If the target does not cast spells, it instead hesitates, reducing its speed by 10 feet for one round.

#### Shatter Step
*Evocation cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 5.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You focus a controlled vibration into the glass floor beneath you, causing a sudden concussive burst that shatters the surface. The shockwave ripples outward, damaging those within range.- Adjacent creatures (within 5 feet) must make a Constitution saving throw. On a failed save, they take 1d6 thunder damage and are deafened until the end of their next turn. On a successful save, they take half damage and are not deafened.- You suffer no ill effects from the glass beneath you, and you remain unharmed.

#### Shifting Hallway
*Illusion cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You subtly alter the perception of an indoor corridor or room, causing it to appear slightly longer, shorter, or misaligned. A creature attempting to navigate the affected area must make an Intelligence (Investigation) check against your spell save DC or briefly hesitate, treating the terrain as difficult for one round.

#### Sibilant Murmurs
*Divination cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V
**Duration:** 1 rounds

You whisper a fleeting phrase laced with unsettling intent, audible only to one creature within range. The target must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw or hear your voice echoing around them, causing mild disorientation. On a failed save, the creature has disadvantage on its next attack roll or ability check before the start of your next turn.

#### Silhouette Link
*Illusion cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

A nearly invisible strand of shadow stretches between you and a creature within range. For the duration, you always know the direction of the target as long as they remain within range. The thread vanishes if the target moves behind total cover or crosses a body of water wider than 5 feet.

#### Slitherword
*Enchantment cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 rounds

You speak with a voice that does not belong to you—layered, shifting, and wrong.
 
One creature of your choice within range must make a Wisdom saving throw. On a failed save:
- The creature flinches involuntarily, disrupting its focus.
- If it takes an action on its next turn, it must spend its bonus action first, if available.
- If it has no bonus action to use, its speed is reduced by 10 feet instead.

 A creature that succeeds on its saving throw is immune to this effect for 24 hours.

#### Solid Footing
*Abjuration cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 rounds

You draw strength from the stability of concrete beneath your feet, solidifying your posture and ensuring that you cannot be easily moved. Your connection to the earth gives you exceptional resistance to being pushed or knocked down.

You gain advantage on Strength and Dexterity saving throws made to resist knockback or any effects that would push, pull, or topple you. This effect lasts until the start of your next turn.

#### Soothing Pulse
*Abjuration cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

The soothing comfort of velvet carpet emanates from your being, gently reinforcing your body and spirit. The calming energy wraps around you, providing minor restorative benefits and a sense of calm resilience.

You gain 1d4 temporary hit points, which last until you take a short or long rest. This temporary hit points cannot stack and are replenished with each casting of the spell.

#### Spectral Utensil
*Conjuration cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You summon a spectral cooking utensil, such as a cast iron pan, a sturdy pot, or a well-balanced ladle. This summoned item can be wielded as a magical weapon. It bypasses resistance to nonmagical attacks. On a hit, the utensil deals 1d4 bludgeoning damage. The force damage increases as you gain levels: 1d4 force at 5th level, 2d4 force at 11th level, and 3d4 force at 17th level.

#### Spellgraft
*Enchantment cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 hours
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You weave a transient channel of arcane force into a willing creature you can see within range. Until the spell ends, the next time that creature makes a spell attack and hits, the attack deals one additional damage die of the same type as the spell (do not add ability modifiers twice). The effect then ends. If the attack misses, the spell persists until the end of the duration or until an empowered spell attack hits. This spell ends early if you cast another spell that requires concentration.

#### Splinter Dart
*Transmutation cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 20.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

Drawing upon the natural flow of the wooden environment around you, you call forth a sharpened splinter from the very floor or nearby wooden structures, launching it with precision and agility.

You make a ranged spell attack against one creature within 20 feet. On a hit, the target takes 1d6 slashing damage as a splinter of wood embeds itself in their body.

#### Splintered Reflection
*Illusion cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 rounds

You afflict a creature’s mind with a sudden deluge of irrelevant memories, false recollections, and intrusive ideas. Fragments of half-remembered lessons, imagined failures, and meaningless details flood their thoughts, crowding out focus and intent.

The target must make an Intelligence saving throw. On a failure, it is mentally overwhelmed for the duration. While affected, the creature rolls 1d6 and subtracts the result from all attack rolls, ability checks, and saving throws, as hesitation and confusion interfere with every decision.

The spell ends early if the target takes psychic damage, as sharp mental pain clears the cluttered thoughts through shock and forced clarity.

For the duration, the creature is visibly distracted, muttering, hesitating, or reacting a moment too late, as though trapped in its own spiraling inner monologue.

#### Stillness of the Grave
*Abjuration cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You slow your breathing and still your pulse, imitating the lifeless calm of a corpse. Until the spell ends, you appear dead to mundane inspection, such as touch or sight. A creature that physically examines you must succeed on a DC 15 Wisdom (Medicine) check to determine that you are still alive. This effect does not suppress your ability to move or speak, but any voluntary action ends the spell immediately.

#### Stonebound Boots
*Transmutation cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 rounds

You attune your footing to worked stone, causing your boots or feet to cling with unnatural tenacity.

For the spell’s duration, while you stand on a stone surface (such as masonry, carved stone, flagstones, or natural bedrock):

• You gain advantage on Strength saving throws and Strength (Athletics) checks made to resist being shoved, pushed, or knocked prone.
• You cannot be moved against your will by nonmagical physical force unless the creature attempting to move you succeeds on a Strength (Athletics) check contested by your Strength saving throw.
• This stability applies only while you remain in direct contact with stone.

The spell immediately ends if you leave a stone surface.

#### Sundersoul
*Evocation cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self (5.0-foot radius)
**Components:** V
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You release a concussive burst of internal instability — the psychic scream of a soul sundered by power.

Each creature of your choice within 5 feet of you must make a Constitution saving throw. On a failed save, they take 1d6 psychic damage and are pushed 5 feet away from you. On a success, they take half damage and are not moved.

The psychic burst has no visible light, but those affected feel an echo of broken memory.
The spell’s damage increases as you reach higher levels:
| Character Level | Damage |
|-----------------|--------|
| 1st             | 1d6    |
| 5th             | 2d6    |
| 11th            | 3d6    |
| 17th            | 4d6    |

#### Surefooted Leap
*Transmutation cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 rounds

You attune your balance and momentum to the structural rhythm of your surroundings—metal beams, concrete ledges, scaffolding, and rooftop catwalks. For the briefest moment, the world feels designed for your movement.

Until the start of your next turn, your long jump distance is doubled, and you do not need a 10- foot run- up to make a long jump.

This movement ignores difficult terrain caused by uneven platforms, narrow ledges, or slippery surfaces, as long as they are part of a constructed or elevated structure (e.g., catwalks, fire escapes, scaffolding, or city rooftop obstacles).

#### Tenderize
*Transmutation cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You deliver a spectral strike that softens defenses. Make a melee spell attack against a creature. On a hit, the target takes 1d4 bludgeoning damage and has disadvantage on the next Strength check or Strength saving throw it makes before the start of your next turn.

#### Thoughtseed
*Divination cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You plant a subtle psychic thread into the mind of a creature you can see within range. The target must succeed on an **Intelligence saving throw** or become **Seeded** for the duration.

While Seeded:
- You can hear **surface thoughts** (what they are actively thinking).
- You know the creature’s **emotional state** and any strong **intent** involving you or your allies.
- As a bonus action on your turn, you may:
- Ask the GM one **yes/no question** the creature knows the answer to.
- Whisper a **single word or phrase** into their mind, which they perceive as their own thought.

A creature that succeeds on the save is immune to your Thoughtseed for 24 hours. 
This spell has **no visual or audible effect** and cannot be detected by mundane means.

#### Tremor Sign
*Enchantment cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 10.0 feet
**Components:** S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You tap the ground, sending a ripple of energy through the surface. A creature standing on solid ground within range must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw or momentarily lose balance, forcing it to make its next attack roll or Dexterity check with disadvantage. If the terrain is loose or unstable, the effect is automatically successful.

#### Tweak/Goose
*Transmutation cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 10.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

A pulse of low- frequency nerve stimulation targets a muscle group or sensitive area, triggering a sharp jolt of sensation akin to a goosebump- inducing touch.

- The target must succeed on a Constitution saving throw or experience an involuntary twitch, shiver, or sharp intake of breath, losing their next reaction.

This spell is often misused in underground establishments, enhancing paid experiences or delivering unexpected sensations.

#### Veilborn Glimmer
*Transmutation cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

Your body shimmers with ethereal light, briefly phasing between reality and the unknown. For the duration, you can dim or brighten your own appearance at will, causing yourself to glow faintly (shedding dim light in a 5- foot radius) or become shadowed (light sources within 10 feet of you appear dimmer). This effect ends if you fall unconscious or dismiss it as a bonus action.

#### Verdant Renewal
*Abjuration cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You touch a patch of resilient green—be it moss growing through cracked pavement or ivy clinging to concrete—and draw strength from its quiet persistence.

Upon casting this spell, a subtle green glow briefly pulses around your feet and chest. For the next minute:- You gain resistance to poison damage.- You have advantage on Constitution saving throws made to resist or recover from exhaustion.

This effect represents the restorative essence of hardy flora—clinging life that thrives in adversity, even in forgotten corners of the city.

#### Wardrobe Malfunction
*Transmutation cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 bonus action
**Range:** 15.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You remotely manipulate the fastenings of a creature’s outfit—zippers slip, laces untie, clasps flick open or shut, or corsets snap with whispered precision.
- You may don or doff any simple clothing as a bonus action, including on a willing creature within range.
- If cast on an unwilling creature, they must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw or have part of their clothing shift, loosen, or fall apart (purely cosmetic, unless specified).
- Subtle castings require a Wisdom (Insight) check against your spell save DC to notice the alteration.

At Higher Tiers:
- If the caster is level 5 or higher, the spell can affect light armor.
- At level 10, it can affect medium or heavy armor, but doing so requires a Strength (Athletics) check (DC 15) to undo or resecure the armor manually.

#### Wisp of the Forgotten
*Necromancy cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You conjure a faint, ghostly whisper from beyond the veil, carrying an unintelligible but haunting message to a creature within range. The target must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw or become unnerved until the start of its next turn, giving it disadvantage on the next Wisdom (Perception) check or initiative roll it makes. If the creature is already frightened, it takes psychic damage equal to your spellcasting ability modifier.

#### Word Stricken from the Record
*Enchantment cantrip*
**Casting Time:** 1 reaction
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V
**Duration:** Instantaneous

When a creature within range attempts to speak, you erase a single spoken word from their sentence. The word is completely omitted, leaving a clear and unnatural gap in their speech.

This does not alter the meaning of the statement, but the omission is obvious to all listeners. If used against a spellcaster, the spell they cast is not disrupted, though they suffer a brief moment of mental dissonance.

#### Arouse
*1st-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 20.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 rounds

You stir the creature’s vital humors, kindling a sudden and involuntary warmth that courses through flesh and nerve alike. Breath shortens, the pulse quickens, and the body answers a stimulus it cannot name nor refuse. Sensation sharpens to an almost unbearable clarity as the target’s physical nature betrays its composure.

The target must succeed on a Constitution saving throw or become Aroused for the duration.

While Aroused, the creature’s body is gripped by restless excitation. Subtle control falters beneath heightened awareness, and every movement carries a faint, unsteady tension.

• The creature has disadvantage on Stealth checks, as its agitation resists stillness and quiet precision.
• The creature has advantage on Perception checks relying on hearing, touch, or taste, its senses keen yet distractible.
• The creature has disadvantage on Constitution saving throws made to maintain concentration, as intrusive sensations scatter disciplined thought.

This effect imposes no emotion, desire, or fear. The disturbance is purely of the body, though observers may misread the creature’s flushed state, quickened breath, or distracted gaze according to their own assumptions.

Creatures devoid of living instincts or immune to charm effects are unaffected.
Optional Roleplay Effects:

The response may resemble nervousness, excitement, or panic depending on context. Social misinterpretations are common and potentially useful (or disastrous).

Notes for Tables:
- Reflavor it for espionage, interrogation, or psychic interference if you want to avoid overtly sexual interpretation.
- Mechanically, it behaves like a stimulant- overload or magic caffeine shot — sensory boost, motor disruption.

#### Barriers of Officialism
*1st-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 reaction
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

A hovering writ of binding law manifests around you, forming an unseen but oppressive obstruction. For the duration, whenever a creature targets you with an attack, it must choose one of the following options:

• Submit a Petition: The creature forfeits its next action, doing nothing on its following turn.
• Endure the Queue: The creature’s movement speed is reduced by 10 feet for that turn.
• Defy the Writ: The creature makes the attack roll with disadvantage.

This effect persists for the spell’s full duration or until you are incapacitated.

#### Bogbolt
*1st-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You conjure and fling a dense glob of swamp muck at a creature within range. The bolt arcs with a disgusting squelch, trailing algae, peat, and mystery goo.

Make a ranged spell attack against a creature. On a hit, the target takes 1d8 blundgeoning damage and must succeed on a Charisma saving throw or be coated in stinking mire for 1 minute.

While affected:- The target has disadvantage on Charisma checks involving persuasion, performance, or decorum.- The effect ends early if the creature spends an action to scrape or wash off the muck.

#### Bonechant Bloom
*1st-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You provoke a violent bloom of pale, sinewy vines drawn from the hidden marrow of the earth.

Choose a point on the ground you can see within 30 feet. A writhing mass of parasitic growth erupts in a 10-foot-radius circle centered on that point. The area becomes difficult terrain for the duration.

When a creature enters the area for the first time on a turn or starts its turn there, it must make a Strength saving throw.

• Failure: The creature is Restrained until the end of its next turn as the vines coil and constrict with unnatural persistence.
• Success: The creature moves unhindered through the growth.

A creature restrained by the vines may use its action to make a Strength (Athletics) check against your spell save DC, ending the restrained condition on a success.

The vines remain animate for the duration, shifting, tightening, and recoiling in slow, unsettling motion, as though guided by half-formed instinct.

#### Borrowed Chance
*1st-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You twist the flow of possibility, briefly diverting fortune from your target’s immediate future.

Choose one creature you can see within range. Until the end of your next turn, you have advantage on the first attack roll you make against that creature.

After that attack roll is resolved, the distortion of fate reverses.

Until the end of the target’s next turn, the creature has advantage on the first attack roll it makes.

If you do not make an attack against the target before the spell’s initial effect expires, the target gains no benefit.

#### Borrowed Momentum
*1st-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You urge a creature beyond its natural cadence, drawing fleeting vigor from moments not yet lived. The target moves with uncanny immediacy, as though anticipation and motion have become indistinguishable.

For the duration, the creature’s body and perception flow in rare accord:

• The target’s speed increases by 20 feet.
• The target has advantage on Dexterity checks.
• The target has advantage on Dexterity saving throws.
• The target’s movement does not provoke opportunity attacks.

Their movements carry an unnatural continuity. Steps land without wasted effort, reactions precede conscious thought, and motion unfolds with effortless certainty.

When the spell ends, the stolen momentum is reclaimed. The creature’s vitality recoils under the strain of borrowed time, and it gains one level of exhaustion.

#### Cloak of the Mason’s Shadow
*1st-level Illusion*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 hours

You veil yourself in the muted hues and fractured geometry of worked stone, blending your presence into the visual rhythm of constructed spaces.

For the duration, your form subtly adopts the tones and textures of masonry, shadowed recesses, and weathered surfaces.

While you are within a settlement, ruin, or constructed environment:

• You have advantage on Dexterity (Stealth) checks.
• Creatures relying on casual observation do not automatically distinguish you from surrounding movement or structure.

This effect ends early if you:

• Make an attack
• Cast a spell that directly affects another creature
• Create a sudden loud noise (GM discretion)

The spell does not render you invisible, obscure your physical position, or prevent deliberate scrutiny.

#### Coitus Compulsum
*1st-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 reaction
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You flood a creature’s mind with intrusive passions, overwhelming it with disorienting impulses of longing, infatuation, and romantic fixation.

Choose one creature within range. The target must make a Charisma saving throw.

• Failure: The creature is Charmed by you for the duration and becomes mentally preoccupied by intense romantic and intimate ideation.
• Success: The creature is unaffected.

While Charmed by this spell, the creature is visibly distracted:

• The creature has disadvantage on Wisdom (Perception) checks.
• The creature has disadvantage on attack rolls against creatures other than you.
• The creature cannot willingly move farther away from you unless it succeeds on a Wisdom saving throw at the start of its turn.

Roll 1d6 immediately upon casting. The target suffers the additional effect for the duration:
d6
Random Effect
1
The target becomes irrationally enamored with the nearest inanimate object within 10 feet. For the duration, the creature is Charmed by the object, treats it as precious, and is unwilling to move more than 10 feet away from it. If the object is threatened or removed, the creature may repeat its saving throw at the end of each of its turns.
2
The target becomes socially disoriented for 1 hour. It has disadvantage on all Charisma checks and Charisma saving throws.
3
The target is overwhelmed by romantic fixation. For the duration, the creature is Charmed by you and regards you with exaggerated affection. This does not compel obedience but may influence behavior at the GM’s discretion.
4
Adrenaline surges through the target. For the duration, it gains a +2 bonus to AC, but it has disadvantage on attack rolls against creatures it finds attractive or emotionally compelling (GM discretion).
5
The target is struck by a cascade of mortifying recollections, taking 1d4 psychic damage and having disadvantage on its next attack roll or ability check before the end of its next turn.
6
A fleeting, illusory winged figure manifests near the target for 1 minute, visible only to creatures within 10 feet. The apparition offers distracting commentary. The target has disadvantage on Wisdom (Perception) checks for the duration. The figure has no mechanical presence and cannot be interacted with.

#### Drain Cognition
*1st-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You siphon fragments of clarity and structured thought from a creature within range.

The target must make an Intelligence saving throw.

• Failure: Roll 1d4. For the duration, the creature suffers a penalty equal to the result:

• Subtract the penalty from its spell save DC (if any).
• Subtract the penalty from Intelligence-based ability checks.

• Success: The creature is unaffected.

A creature affected by this spell cannot suffer additional penalties from multiple castings of Drain Cognition. Only the highest penalty applies.

#### Eternal Etching
*1st-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Permanent

You inscribe a declaration or mark into a nonliving object, anchoring the inscription with unnatural permanence.

Choose a nonmagical object you can touch. You create a visible inscription, symbol, signature, or brief message upon its surface.

For the duration of the object’s existence:

• The inscription cannot be removed, altered, or obscured by mundane means, including abrasion, burning, staining, or physical damage.
• The inscription persists even if the object is broken, provided its fragments remain identifiable as parts of the original object.

The inscription conveys no magical compulsion and produces no mechanical effects beyond its persistence.

The mark may be removed or altered only by magic capable of directly modifying magical effects or reality itself.

#### Fingerbang
*1st-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 bonus action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You snap your hand into a confident finger gun and unleash a crackling projectile of arcane force shaped like a bullet. Choose one creature within range. Make a ranged spell attack against the target.

- On a hit, the target takes 2d6 ballistic damage.
- The projectile leaves behind a faint trail of cigarette smoke and the smell of ozone.
- If cast while wearing sunglasses or leaning on something cool, you may deal an additional +1 damage (DM discretion, style points encouraged).

#### Giocrin's Nostalgia
*1st-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V
**Duration:** 30 minutess

You evoke a pale, memory-laden radiance that lingers with an unsettling stillness. When you cast this spell, choose one of the following manifestations:

⸻

Beacon

A soft, eerie light appears at a point you can see within 5 feet.

• The light sheds bright light in a 20-foot radius and dim light for an additional 20 feet
• The beacon remains stationary for 30 minutes
• The light is unaffected by wind, rain, or immersion in water

⸻

Flare

A sudden lance of colored light streaks upward from a point you choose within range.

• The flare rises vertically and briefly blooms overhead
• For 1 round, it sheds bright light in a 60-foot radius centered on its peak
• The light then fades instantly

Outdoors, the flare is visible at great distance, often mistaken for an omen or distant signal.

⸻

The light may be any color you choose. It is uncanny but gentle, causing no harm and imposing no visual impairment.

#### Glossolalia Error
*1st-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 reaction
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V
**Duration:** 1 rounds

You unleash a surge of disruptive interference that tangles speech, thought, and articulation.

Choose one creature within range. The target must make a Constitution saving throw.

• Failure: The creature is unable to produce intelligible speech until the end of its next turn. During this time, it cannot cast spells with verbal components.

• If the creature was in the process of casting a spell when targeted, it must succeed on a Constitution saving throw or the spell fails and the action is wasted.

• Success: The creature resists the disruption and suffers no effect.

For a brief moment, the target’s words fracture into meaningless syllables and broken sounds.

#### Gourds and Wharfs
*1st-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You conjure a curious arrangement of autumnal objects at a point you can see within range. Roll a d6 to determine what appears.

The conjured objects are nonmagical, fragile, and persist for the duration unless destroyed.
| d6 | Summon Result |
|---- |------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| 1 | A harmless pile of decorative gourds appears. |
| 2 | Gourds appear and burst into harmless, colorful sparks. |
| 3 | A small wooden dock appears precisely 10 feet away from the target point. |
| 4 | A small wooden dock appears with a tiny boat gently bobbing at its side. |
| 5 | A talking scarecrow briefly appears, makes an obscure remark, and vanishes. |
| 6 | A single, massive pumpkin (large enough to provide half- cover) appears. |

#### Greaseproof Grip
*1st-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

Choose a creature you can see within range. For the duration, the target’s grasp becomes unnaturally secure.

The target has advantage on Strength checks and Strength saving throws made to:

• Maintain hold of an object
• Resist being disarmed
• Prevent an item it is holding from being forcibly removed

If the target would drop an item due to an external effect, it may make a Strength saving throw. On a success, the item is not dropped.

#### Grubby Learn-Fists
*1st-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

Your hands are seized by an intrusive hunger for unfamiliar skill. Fingers twitch, probe, and fidget with restless curiosity, as if guided by instincts not entirely your own.

Choose one tool, weapon, or musical instrument. For the duration, you gain proficiency with the chosen item. If you are already proficient, you instead gain advantage on ability checks made using it.

At the start of each of your turns, you must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw (DC 10) or your hands behave erratically until the start of your next turn. While erratic, the DM may impose one of the following effects:

• You have disadvantage on attack rolls made with held weapons
• You have disadvantage on Dexterity-based ability checks
• You drop one held object of the DM’s choice
• Your hands perform involuntary gestures, preventing somatic components that turn

The hands’ movements are compulsive rather than intelligent, driven by restless experimentation rather than intent.

At Higher Levels. When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 2nd level or higher, you may choose one additional item per slot level above 1st. The saving throw DC increases by 1 for each additional item learned.

#### Gut Instinct
*1st-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 rounds

You surrender conscious thought to raw survival impulse, allowing reflex to outrun intention.

Until the start of your next turn:

• You gain a +2 bonus to AC
• You have advantage on the next Dexterity saving throw you make
• When a creature you can see targets you with an attack, you may use your reaction to move up to 10 feet

This movement occurs after the attack is declared but before the attack roll is made, and does not provoke opportunity attacks.

Moving in this way does not automatically cause the attack to miss, but may place you outside the attacker’s reach or line of effect as normal.

#### Halo Brand
*1st-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 bonus action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You inscribe a subtle metaphysical mark upon a creature you can see within range, manifesting as either a faint halo of sanctity or a dim corona of corruption (your choice). The mark may be visible or imperceptible at the time of casting.

For the duration, the branded creature interacts differently with consecrated terrain:

• On Sanctified Ground: The creature becomes unnaturally vulnerable to purifying force. The first time each turn it is hit by a melee attack, it takes an additional 1d4 fire damage.

• On Desecrated Ground: The creature’s resolve falters beneath hostile resonance. It suffers a –1 penalty to damage rolls and a –1 penalty to spell attack rolls.

If the creature is not within sanctified or desecrated terrain, the brand remains dormant and has no effect.

If terrain beneath the creature becomes sanctified or desecrated while the spell persists, the appropriate effect activates immediately.

The halo is a magical mark rather than a physical phenomenon and does not obstruct vision or movement.

#### Hunter’s Unerring Mark
*1st-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 bonus action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

When your projectile finds its prey, you bind the target to your awareness with an invisible hunter’s sigil.

When you hit a creature with a ranged weapon attack, you may mark it for the duration.

While the creature is marked:

• You know the creature’s direction and distance while it remains within 500 feet of you
• This awareness is not blocked by nonmagical obstacles, but is suppressed if the creature is behind total cover or on another plane
• Your ranged weapon attacks against the marked creature treat half cover as no cover

The mark ends early if you lose concentration or mark another creature with this spell.

Duration: Concentration, up to 1 hour.

#### Huruma’s Immediate Recall
*1st-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You seize a faltering life at the brink of dissolution, forcing its thread back into the body before it fully slips beyond reach.

Choose one creature within range that is at 0 hit points. The creature immediately stabilizes and regains 1d4 hit points + your spellcasting ability modifier.

If the creature was unconscious, it awakens in a state of violent disorientation. Until the end of its next turn:

• The creature is Stunned

The restoration is forceful rather than restorative. Breath returns in ragged convulsions, limbs tremble, and awareness lags behind sensation.

This spell has no effect on creatures that have died.

#### Inkbound Familiar
*1st-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 hours
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Permanent

You bind a minor familiar spirit into your flesh, where it persists as a living sigil of animated ink. The entity exists as a shifting tattoo upon your skin, its form fluid and expressive, yet incapable of separating from your body.

The familiar uses the statistics of a normal familiar but cannot manifest physically and cannot occupy a space outside your body.

While the familiar is inkbound:

• You may use an action to see and hear through the familiar’s senses. While doing so, you are blind and deaf to your own surroundings.
• You may communicate telepathically with the familiar while it remains conscious.
• When you cast a spell with a range of touch, the familiar may deliver the spell as though it were the contacting body part.
• The familiar cannot attack, manipulate objects, or move independently beyond shifting across your skin.
• The familiar must remain on an exposed portion of your body to use its senses.

The tattoo is magical and cannot be removed by mundane means. It persists through non-destructive transformations such as disguise or polymorph.

If the spell ends, or if the tattoo is suppressed by magic that negates conjuration effects, the familiar vanishes.

You may have only one inkbound familiar at a time. Casting this spell again causes any previous inkbound familiar to disappear.

Duration: Until dispelled.

#### Jealousy
*1st-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 minutes
**Range:** 6.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You disturb the emotional equilibrium of nearby minds, amplifying insecurity, possessiveness, and perceived slights.

Creatures of your choice within range must make a Wisdom saving throw.

On a failure, a creature becomes Agitated for the duration:

• The creature has disadvantage on Charisma checks made toward other affected creatures
• The creature has disadvantage on Insight checks
• If another affected creature takes a Help action or receives visible praise, the creature must succeed on a Charisma saving throw or use its reaction (if available) to voice irritation, suspicion, or accusation

While Agitated, creatures are predisposed toward rivalry and mistrust, though they retain full control of their actions.

The effect ends early for a creature if it takes damage.

Duration: Concentration, up to 1 minute.

Creatures immune to being charmed are unaffected.
In social or investigative scenarios, this spell may cause suspicion, false confessions, or betrayal.

#### Lantern of the Pale Path
*1st-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 bonus action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

A pallid, heatless flame blossoms in your palm, illuminating only what the world attempts to conceal. The flame sheds no normal light and is visible only to you.

For the duration, you perceive subtle pale glimmers that reveal:

• Invisible tracks and trails left within the past 24 hours
• Deliberately concealed objects within 30 feet
• Hidden doors, secret markings, and inscriptions, including those obscured by mundane or magical means

This perception does not penetrate total cover or solid barriers, but it ignores nonmagical camouflage, visual illusions, and mundane attempts at hiding.

Other creatures cannot see the flame or its revelations unless they are Under Surveillance, in which case they perceive the flame as a faint, ghostly glow without gaining its benefits.

The flame occupies your hand and moves with you.

#### Luhtin's Curious Footing
*1st-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You channel a wavering current of arcane force into a creature you touch, lifting it slightly out of step with the ground.

For the spell’s duration, the target gains a hovering movement equal to its walking speed. This allows the creature to remain suspended up to 3 feet above a surface.

While hovering:

• The creature is treated as not in physical contact with the ground.
• It may move across liquid surfaces, fragile terrain, and ground-based hazards without triggering effects that require direct contact (such as pressure plates, caltrops, or similar triggers).
• The spell does not grant flight. The creature cannot ascend beyond the 3-foot limit and cannot move vertically except as required to follow the contour of a surface.
• The creature cannot cross vertical barriers, gaps without underlying support, ceilings, or walls.

If the creature becomes incapacitated, restrained, or its speed becomes 0, the hovering effect immediately ends and it descends harmlessly to the nearest supporting surface.

#### Naxious Haze
*1st-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You summon choking fumes that blur vision.
- A 10- foot- radius sphere becomes heavily obscured.
- Creatures inside must succeed a Constitution save or have disadvantage on attacks and lose reactions for 1 round.
- The area smells faintly of burnt plastic and rust.

#### Orb of Let's Not
*1st-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You conjure a glowing, humming orb of soft pastel light that floats 5 feet off the ground and emits gentle music and phrases like:- “Let’s not do this.”- “Violence is exhausting.”- “Hugs not hits.”- “Come on, talk it out, champ.”

Each creature of your choice within a 10- foot radius of the sphere must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw or become non- hostile for as long as they remain within the sphere’s area.

They won’t initiate attacks, cast offensive spells, or shout mean things while inside—but they may still pout, sulk, or engage in passive aggression.

The Save DC is equal to: 10 + the creature’s Challenge Rating (rounded down)
This means tougher creatures are less likely to resist the sphere’s charm, because even ancient dragons want to be understood.

While active:- The sphere follows its original position and cannot be moved.- Creatures who exit and re- enter must re- roll their save.- Creatures who are damaged immediately shake off the effect.
| d6 | The Sphere says... |
|---- |--------------------------------------------- |
| 1 | "Let’s take a deep breath." |
| 2 | "I’m hearing a lot of anger right now." |
| 3 | "Let’s find common ground... maybe brunch?" |
| 4 | "It’s not about winning." |
| 5 | "I’m on your side. All of your sides." |
| 6 | *Plays gentle ukulele chords and sighs* |

#### Phase Step
*1st-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 bonus action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You momentarily shift into a liminal state, allowing you to step through solid objects no thicker than 5 feet. If you would end your movement inside an object, you are ejected to the nearest open space, taking 1d8 bludgeoning damage.

#### Revelation of the Flesh
*1st-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You place your hand on a willing creature and channel a diagnostic pulse of divinatory energy. For a brief moment, their body becomes transparent to your senses, revealing hidden disruptions or irregularities within.

You detect the presence of any internal affliction, including:
- Natural or magical diseases
- Poisons or chemical imbalances
- Curses with a biological or physiological component
- Arcane mutations or lingering experimental side effects

You immediately learn the type of affliction present (e.g., “necrotic infection,” “alchemical toxin,” or “soul- linked corruption”). You do not learn the exact name or nature of the condition unless you succeed on a DC 13 Intelligence (Medicine or Arcana) check.

Creatures without any detectable affliction feel nothing. Afflicted creatures may feel a brief sting, or other harmless somatic response depending on the nature of their condition.

#### Rodent of Frost
*1st-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You summon a single, spectral rat formed of condensed frost and arcane chill. It scurries off immediately, following an inexplicable instinct.- The rat automatically seeks the coldest location within a 200- foot radius, regardless of visibility or accessibility.- It can sense cold through barriers, insulation, or seals—even within a hermetically sealed container like a locked freezer.- As it moves, it leaves behind a trail of tiny frost- lined footprints, which last for 1 minute before sublimating.

The rat is entirely uninterested in combat and disappears instantly if initiative is rolled or hostilities begin nearby.

#### Splintered Howl
*1st-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You emit a fractured, unsteady howl that unsettles the minds of nearby creatures, echoing with something disturbingly inhuman.

Creatures of your choice within 10 feet must make a Wisdom saving throw.

• Failure: A creature is Frightened of you until the end of its next turn.
• Success: The creature is unaffected.

Creatures that are Undeads or Constructs suffer a −2 penalty to the saving throw.

You guarantee that your target contracts a non- lethal but incredibly annoying illness. The target must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw or become afflicted for the duration. While afflicted, the target suffers one randomly determined symptom.

#### Taunt the Fruit Boots
*1st-level Illusion*
**Casting Time:** 1 minutes
**Range:** 120.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You channel your arcane energy into pure style and physics- defying balance. As part of the spell, you perform an absolutely sick trick on a skateboard (or any similar celebrityl transport device). The trick defies gravity, logic, and taste. Everyone nearby feels its impact.

Roll a Performance (Charisma) check. Choose one of the following based on the result:- 15 or higher: A nearby crowd gathers. If 5 or more creatures visibly react with awe (DM’s discretion), you gain advantage on all Charisma checks and Charisma saving throws until your next long rest.- 10–14: The trick works, but only a few bystanders notice. You gain advantage on your next Charisma ability check.- Below 10: You still land it… barely. No benefit, but you avoid humiliation.

This spell grants no combat bonuses and immediately ends if cast in combat.
- NPC reactions can be determined by a group Insight check or DM fiat.- Impressing elite socialites, hardened criminals, or nobles may require a higher Performance DC.

#### Tether Hook
*1st-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You conjure an ethereal tether and anchor it to a visible ledge or wall.
- You may instantly pull yourself up to 20 feet toward the anchor as part of the casting.
- For the spell’s duration, you or an ally may use a bonus action to pull themselves to the same anchor.
- If the anchor is removed or broken, the tether snaps.

#### The Mourner's Kiss
*1st-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You infuse the Veins of Lament into a kiss, channeling raw pain through the moment of contact. When you touch a creature with your lips (or simulate the act with a somatic gesture), your magic delivers a pulse of internal anguish.

The target must make a Dexterity saving throw. On a failed save, it takes 1d3 fire damage plus 3 damage per caster level (maximum 1d3 + 20). On a successful save, the creature takes half damage.

This kiss leaves no visible wound, but the target feels as if something delicate within them cracked.

#### Truth Between the Sheets
*1st-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You exhale a slow, intoxicating breath, sending whispers of carnal truth and romantic echoes drifting into the target’s aura. The magic doesn’t extract facts—it invites revelation.

A silken mirage unfolds, where the subject’s soul steps forward, cloaked in glimmering honesty. Faces, forms, emotions, and gestures emerge from the haze—some familiar, some unknown—each representing a truth they’ve always carried.

The spell may reveal one or more of the following aspects, depending on your focus:

Gender Identity: The target's inner identity manifests briefly as a mirage, affirming their true self. This may reveal identities such as Male, Female, Nonbinary, Transgender, Cisgender, Two- Spirit, Genderfluid, Agender, or something uniquely celebrityl and beyond typical categories.

Romantic Inclination: You awaken a subtle echo within the target’s spirit, reflecting their romantic nature. This might indicate whether they identify as Hyper- Romantic, Romantic, Demi- Romantic, Grayromantic, Aromantic, or something entirely undefined.

Sexual Orientation: A fleeting, sensory dreamscape gently unfolds around the target, reflecting their deepest attractions. They may acknowledge, embrace, or gently dismiss these visions. The spell doesn't impose new desires; it simply illuminates those already present.

Position Preference: A subtle sensation reveals the subject's preferred intimacy position, such as Top, Bottom, Versatile, Vers- Top, Vers- Bottom, Side, or an unclassified, uniquely celebrityl preference.

Fetish Affinity: A delicate hum pulses into the subject’s subconscious, drawing forth hidden motifs of pleasure—those they cherish, those they deny, and those that whisper only in dreams. This may reveal affinities such as Bondage, Impact Play, Sensory Deprivation, Exhibitionism, Voyeurism, Power Exchange, Pet Play, or something undocumented by common texts.

Kink Role Alignment: A soft whisper coils through the subject’s awareness, coaxing insight into their innate position within dominance- submission dynamics. They may momentarily experience themselves in a state of control, surrender, or fluidity. Whether they resist, acknowledge, or embrace this vision, the spell merely opens a door—it does not push them through it.

The experience is not invasive—it is affirming, deeply celebrityl, and laced with quiet reverence. The subject may resist this unveiling with a Wisdom saving throw; on a success, the vision remains fragmented, and only a vague sense of their essence slips through.

This spell does not coerce. It does not judge. It simply illuminates what was already burning softly beneath the surface.
This spell respects the target's autonomy and does not alter or coerce identities or preferences; it merely reveals truths already held.

Always ensure sensitive handling of these revelations at your table, prioritizing player comfort and respectful roleplay.

#### Veiled Word of Imperative Thought
*1st-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 rounds

You utter a single word carried directly through telepathic channels, comprehensible only to the intended target. To all others, the sound fractures into meaningless distortion or incomprehensible murmuring. The target must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw or obey the command on its next turn, as though compelled by a direct imperative of thought.

If the saving throw succeeds, the target senses that its will was briefly tested, though it gains no knowledge of the source. Observers may recognize that magic was invoked, but cannot discern the content or intent of the command. When cast at greater power, the utterance leaves no sound, sign, or lingering trace beyond the shared thought itself.

#### Wall of Farce
*1st-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You conjure an illusory wall up to 5 feet wide, 10 feet tall, and 1 inch thick made entirely of bad visual gags and slapstick nonsense. Rubber chickens, cream pies, banana peels, and invisible panes of glass loop endlessly in magical animation. The wall occasionally emits groan- worthy puns, honking horns, or laugh tracks from nowhere.

The wall is not solid and can be walked through—but creatures who approach it often don’t realize it’s fake.

When a creature comes within 5 feet of the wall for the first time on a turn or starts its turn near it, it must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw or become incapacitated with uncontrollable laughter until the start of its next turn.

A creature that investigates the wall (as an action) may make another Wisdom saving throw. On a success, it sees through the illusion—the wall disappears for that creature only.

The spell ends early if you lose concentration or dismiss it.

#### Wanton Assessment
*1st-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You brush your fingers gently across the target’s skin, and for a moment, their body opens itself to your senses—like a lover whispering its deepest discomforts.

You detect any sexual or intimacy- related ailments currently affecting the creature, whether physical, psychological, emotional, or arcane. This includes but is not limited to:
- Venereal diseases, mundane or magical
- Hormonal imbalances, arousal anomalies, arcane sterility
- Psychological blocks, trauma- induced aversions, or compulsions
- Magically- induced attractions, false bonds, or enchantments
- Anomalous intimacy curses (e.g., “can’t touch anyone,” “always fall in love,” etc.)

Each issue is revealed in poetic, metaphorical terms, such as:

“The heart is sealed with wax,” or “There is a hunger with no source.”

With a DC 12 Wisdom (Medicine or Insight) check, you may interpret one affliction literally.

An afflicted creature feels a brief sensation of heat or shiver, depending on the nature of the ailment. Some report hearing a whisper from within themselves.

#### Whispering Wine
*1st-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You conjure a bottle of smooth, dark wine that whispers strange, cryptic advice to anyone who drinks from it. The murmurs are soft, slurred, and often incoherent—but they always sound meaningful… even when they aren’t.

Each time a creature takes a sip (a free object interaction), they must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw or accidentally reveal a celebrityl secret aloud. The secret is chosen by the DM or the player, depending on tone.

The wine’s advice is usually:- Just slightly off- topic- Half- true at best- Or deeply unsettling with no context (“Beware the third fork…”)

#### Aegis of Rebounding Force
*2nd-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 reaction
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 rounds

You draw a momentary aegis of compressed force tight against your body, condensing the surrounding air into an invisible, resistant shell. Until the start of your next turn, ranged weapon attacks made against you are partially deflected by the distortion.

When a creature makes a ranged weapon attack targeting you before the spell ends:

- The attack is made with disadvantage.
- On a hit, the attack’s damage is reduced by 2d8 as the impact is dulled by the force sheath.

The rebounding energy punishes reckless aggression. If the attacker is within the weapon’s normal range and the attack roll fails to hit, the creature takes force damage equal to your spellcasting ability modifier (minimum 1) as the disrupted momentum snaps back along the attack’s path, bruising flesh and rattling bone.

Missiles, bolts, and hurled weapons strike as though the air itself resists them, their violence blunted before reaching you. Those who attempt to wound you from afar feel the backlash of their own momentum, a sharp and unforgiving reminder that distance offers no safety from consequence.

#### Amphibious Downpour
*2nd-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 hours

You summon a localized, magical downpour of harmless frogs in a 10-foot-radius area within range. The amphibians fall in a soft, chaotic cascade, immediately covering the ground in a dense, shifting layer of damp bodies.

The area becomes difficult terrain for the duration as footing turns unstable and movement requires exaggerated care. The frogs persistently croak in gentle but relentless harmony, their overlapping calls filling the space with a strangely soothing yet impossible-to-ignore chorus.

Creatures within the area experience constant sensory interference:

• Creatures have disadvantage on Perception checks that rely on hearing.
• Any creature maintaining concentration while inside the area has disadvantage on Constitution saving throws made to maintain that concentration.

The frogs themselves are harmless, though creatures moving at speed through the area must contend with the unsteady surface. When a creature first enters the area on a turn or starts its turn there, it must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw or have its movement speed reduced to 0 until the start of its next turn as it struggles for footing.

When the spell ends, the frogs disperse naturally, hopping away, slipping into cracks, or vanishing into nearby undergrowth. No trace of their presence remains beyond lingering moisture and memory.
Clarifications:- The frogs are non- hostile and cannot be used for damage.- The difficult terrain affects all creatures equally, allies and enemies alike.
| Spell Slot Level | Radius of Effect |
|----------------------- |-------------------- |
| 1st-level | 10- foot radius |
| 2nd-level | 20- foot radius |
| 3rd-level | 30- foot radius |
| 4th-level | 40- foot radius |
| 5th-level or higher | 50- foot radius |

#### Artisan's Crucible
*2nd-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 1.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 hours

You attune a forge, workshop, or crafting station to a state long recognized by artisans yet poorly understood. A steady, disciplined warmth suffuses the workspace, replacing the need for open flame. The heat is even, controlled, and curiously responsive to deliberate effort.

Those experienced in craft sometimes speak of such conditions in reverent or superstitious terms, though no consensus exists as to their origin.

While working within the crucible’s influence:

• Refined Conditions: Crafting checks involving metal, bone, ceramic, or composite materials are made with advantage.
• Material Responsiveness: Nonmagical metal objects handled within the workspace may be bent, joined, or adjusted in minor ways consistent with their physical limits. Attempts to exceed structural plausibility fail without effect.
• Unusual Cohesion: Simple material joins or assemblies performed during the duration exhibit exceptional stability at the GM’s discretion.
• Residual Warmth: Items completed within the crucible retain faint warmth for 72 hours, a cosmetic effect.

The crucible does not generate materials, accelerate crafting time, or enable transformations beyond conventional technical possibility.

If a manipulation strains the material beyond tolerance, the attempt fails. The GM may apply minor consequences such as wasted effort, cosmetic flaws, or harmless backlash.

Repeated use upon the same workspace may produce subtle irregularities. Tools settle into comfortable balance, surfaces appear unusually well-aligned, and completed items may display curious but nonmechanical peculiarities. Interpretations vary.

#### Battle-Fury Ascension
*2nd-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You lift the target into a state of dreadful martial exaltation, as though their spirit has briefly crossed the threshold walked only by the honored dead. Hesitation falls away. Fear dissolves. Motion becomes inevitable.

For the duration, the creature moves with the cold, flawless certainty of one who no longer doubts survival nor death:

• The target’s speed doubles.
• The target gains a +2 bonus to AC.
• The target has advantage on Dexterity saving throws.
• On each of its turns, the target gains one additional action, usable only for Attack (one weapon attack only), Dash, Disengage, Hide, or Use an Object.

Their movements carry an eerie finality. Blows are placed with silent precision. Missiles pass by as though unwilling to interfere. Every step lands with the weight of fate already accepted.

When the spell ends, the ascension is revoked.

The warrior’s body, suddenly burdened once more by the frailty of living flesh, falters beneath the loss of that terrible clarity. Until the end of its next turn, the target cannot move or take actions, its limbs heavy and unresponsive, as though awakening from a place where struggle was no longer required.

#### Bliss on the Lips
*2nd-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You deliver a kiss infused with phantasmal delirium, flooding the target’s mind with euphoric distortions and treacherous sensations.

The creature must make a Wisdom saving throw.

• Failure: The creature becomes Delirious for the duration.
• Success: The creature resists the effect and is unaffected.

Delirious Condition:
While Delirious, the creature’s perceptions fracture into intoxicating unreality:

• The creature has disadvantage on Intelligence, Wisdom, and Dexterity checks.
• The creature has disadvantage on Constitution saving throws made to maintain concentration.
• The creature’s perception of the environment is subtly distorted, manifesting as phantom lights, shifting colors, or illusory sensations.

In addition, at the start of each of the creature’s turns, it must make a Wisdom saving throw:

• Failure: The creature becomes Enthralled by Delusion until the start of its next turn.
• Success: No additional effect that turn.

Enthralled by Delusion:
While under this effect:

• The creature treats illusory stimuli, imagined comforts, or subjective perceptions as credible and compelling.
• The creature has disadvantage on Perception checks and cannot take reactions.
• The creature’s behavior may be influenced by hallucinated experiences at the DM’s discretion.

The creature is not charmed, frightened, or controlled. The distortion is perceptual, not emotional.

#### Chef's Keen Senses
*2nd-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

Your senses attune to sustenance. Flavor, rot, nourishment, and spoilage reveal themselves as unmistakable impressions upon your tongue and gut.

For the duration, you sense the presence of edible substances within 30 feet. This perception detects food, drink, ingredients, and consumable organic matter, regardless of whether they are fresh, spoiled, concealed, or disguised.

This awareness provides:

• The direction and approximate distance to each edible source
• The general nature of the substance (meat, grain, fruit, liquid, etc.)
• Its state of edibility (wholesome, stale, spoiled, toxic, inedible)

This sense does not penetrate solid barriers. Substances behind total cover are not detected.

Magical disguises, illusions, or transmutations do not conceal a substance’s edibility, though they may distort its apparent form.

This spell conveys no detailed visual information, only instinctive sensory impressions.

#### Clarity of the Mind
*2nd-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You gently realign the disordered currents of a willing creature’s thoughts, easing cognitive turbulence and restoring functional coherence.

Choose one willing creature within range. The spell soothes transient mental disturbances, steadying perception and emotional regulation without altering memory or personality.

The spell ends the following conditions affecting the target, provided they arise from mental strain, fear, psychic interference, or similar destabilizing influences:

• Paranoid
• Frightened
• Stunned
• Compelled
• Aroused (if imposed by a magical or supernatural effect)

This spell does not remove conditions caused by ongoing spells, magical domination, curses, or effects that explicitly resist lesser restorative magic, at the GM’s discretion.

The spell does not dispel enchantments or rewrite memory. It restores only the mind’s capacity to regulate itself.

#### Commoner's Glow-up
*2nd-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 500.0 feet
**Components:** S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You cloak a creature in a luminous, refined glamour that subtly alters how others perceive their bearing, attire, and presence. The target appears impeccably groomed, elegantly presented, and possessed of unmistakable social confidence. The transformation reflects culturally appropriate signs of wealth, prestige, or influence.

For the duration, the illusion affects only perception, not physical form.

• Creatures that see the target perceive them as unusually well-presented and socially elevated unless they succeed on an Intelligence (Investigation) check against your spell save DC.
• The target has advantage on Charisma (Persuasion, Performance, and Deception) checks made to impress, influence, or gain favor from creatures who value status, refinement, or hierarchy.
• Creatures predisposed to respect wealth, authority, or social standing may react more favorably to the target at the GM’s discretion.

This spell does not alter memories, compel obedience, or guarantee compliance. Suspicious creatures, close associates, or those with reason to doubt appearances may challenge the illusion normally.

#### Drowsing Embrace
*2nd-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You infuse a willing gesture of contact with a subtle soporific enchantment, transmitting unnatural lethargy through touch.

As part of casting this spell, you must touch a creature. The target must make a Wisdom saving throw.

• Failure: The creature falls Unconscious for the duration.
• Success: The creature resists the enchantment and is unaffected.

The sleep induced by this spell is unnaturally deep. The creature does not awaken from ordinary noise or movement, but awakens if it takes damage or if another creature uses an action to rouse it.

This spell has no effect on creatures immune to magical sleep.

⸻

Reversed Application

When cast upon a creature that is Unconscious due to a magical sleep effect, this spell may instead be used to immediately end one such effect, provided the original effect is of 2nd level or lower.

#### Duinir's Respite of Flames
*2nd-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

A pulse of gentle, heatless warmth flows from your hands, settling upon chosen allies like the memory of a sanctuary long extinguished.

Choose up to three creatures within range. Each target gains 2d4 temporary hit points and is immune to the Charmed condition for the duration.

While affected by this spell, a creature emits a faint, ember-like glow from its chest when subjected to magical influence or deliberate emotional manipulation. The glow sheds no light and is visible only in dim light or darkness.

#### Duinir’s Ember Aegis
*2nd-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You wreath a creature in a mantle of restrained embers that flare violently when its bearer is struck.

Choose one creature within range. For the duration, the target gains resistance to fire damage.

The first time the target takes damage from a creature’s attack while the spell persists, the embers erupt in retaliation. The attacker takes 2d6 fire damage.

The embers then subside, ending the retaliatory effect. The spell’s fire resistance remains for the duration.

#### Echo of the Hallowed Ground
*2nd-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

While this spell is active, your aura reflects the memory of sanctified or desecrated ground. For the duration:- Your Aura of Sanctity applies even if the terrain is not currently Holy or Unholy.- You gain a faint glowing aura (or a flickering shadow) that reveals your allegiance.- If you cast Consecrate or Corrupt during the duration, the effect becomes instantaneous and cannot be interrupted by damage.

Note: This spell allows you to “prime” a battlefield without needing the terrain benefit immediately, making it more tactical.

#### Eldritch Intoxication
*2nd-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You flood a creature’s senses with unnatural pleasure and destabilizing euphoria, severing discipline from perception.

Choose one creature within range. The target must make a Wisdom saving throw.

• Failure: The creature becomes Aroused for the duration. While Aroused by this spell:

• The creature’s speed is halved.
• The creature has disadvantage on Intelligence and Wisdom saving throws.
• The creature experiences vivid, distracting hallucinations. These manifestations are subjective, sensory, and chosen by the GM. They convey no reliable information and impose no additional mechanical effects beyond those described by the spell.
