• Failure by 10 or more: The creature is additionally afflicted with the Paranoid condition for the duration. While Paranoid in this way, the creature cannot willingly target other creatures with hostile actions unless those creatures have damaged it since the end of its previous turn.

• Success: The creature is unaffected.

#### Eyes Behind the Kiss
*2nd-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Special

You press a lingering, whispering kiss upon a creature you can touch. Its vitality recoils as unseen hunger drinks from the strength that anchors flesh to will.

The target must make a Constitution saving throw.

• Failure: The creature takes 6d8 necrotic damage, and its Strength score is reduced by 2d4 for 1 minute (minimum 1).

While affected, the creature’s body feels oppressively heavy and alien. The creature is Restrained until the end of its next turn.

• Success: The creature takes half damage and suffers no Strength reduction or restraint.

If the target is already under the effect of a necromancy spell, it takes an additional 1d6 necrotic damage.

The Strength reduction ends early if the creature receives greater restoration, heal, or similar magic at the GM’s discretion.

Those afflicted often claim their reflection continues to move a fraction too late.

#### Fire Colt
*2nd-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You summon a tiny, fiery equine construct—a blazing colt no larger than a medium- sized dog. It snorts embers, kicks up sparks, and serves as both a mount and a living incendiary hazard.

The horse has the following traits:

AC: 14
HP: 20
Speed: 40 ft.
Resistance: Pyric
Size: Small
Ridable by Medium or smaller creatures

Abilities:
- Flaming Charge: As a bonus action, the colt can charge a creature within 30 feet. The target must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw or take 1d6 fire damage and be pushed 5 feet.
- Explosive Dismissal: When the spell ends (whether voluntarily or involuntarily), the colt explodes in a 10- foot radius. Creatures in the area must make a Dexterity saving throw or take 2d6 fire damage, or half on a success.

Unstable Nature:

At the start of each of your turns, roll a DC 10 Wisdom saving throw. On a failure, the colt becomes unstable and explodes immediately, ending the spell.

#### Forgotten Banquet of Determination
*2nd-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 10 minutess
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** S
**Duration:** 24 hourss

You conjure a long, spectral banquet table laden with silent, translucent dishes. The feast emits no warmth, no scent, and no comfort, only a stillness that presses against the senses.

Up to six creatures of your choice within 30 feet may partake of the ghostly meal.

Each creature that consumes the food must make a Constitution saving throw.

• Success: The creature is fortified by unsettling resolve. For 1 hour, it gains a +1 bonus to AC and has advantage on saving throws against being Charmed.

• Failure: The feast dredges forth forgotten griefs. The creature gains one level of exhaustion.

Regardless of the outcome, the meal sustains the creature, removing the need for food for 24 hours.

Once consumed, the banquet slowly fades, leaving behind only a faint dusting of salt and ash.

#### Giocrin's Face of Rust
*2nd-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You exhale a wave of corroding shadow that clings to flesh and vitality alike, like oxidation made manifest.

Each creature in a 20-foot cone must make a Constitution saving throw.

• Failure: The creature takes 2d6 necrotic damage, and cannot regain hit points until the start of your next turn.

• Success: The creature takes half damage and suffers no additional effects.

The shadow leaves no visible flame or wound, only a spreading dullness, as though something essential has begun to tarnish.

#### Hospice of Withheld Comfort
*2nd-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** None
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You manifest an immaculate vessel of impossible refreshment, cool to the touch and inviting beyond reason. Its contents glisten with promise, radiating relief that is never quite granted.

The vessel appears in an unoccupied space within range and lasts for the duration.

While a creature remains within 10 feet of the vessel and does not attempt to drink from it:

• The creature ignores penalties imposed by extreme heat
• The creature has advantage on saving throws against exhaustion caused by environmental conditions

The vessel offers solace only through denial.

When a creature attempts to drink from the vessel, it immediately vanishes from that creature’s grasp. The creature must succeed on a Charisma saving throw or be banished until the end of its next turn.

While banished in this way, the creature is displaced into a harmless extradimensional lapse, aware only of lingering, unsatisfied need.

When the creature returns, it suffers no additional effects.

Duration: Concentration, up to 1 minute.

#### Huruma’s Vigilant Thread
*2nd-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You fasten a creature’s thread within Huruma’s patient keeping, reinforcing the fragile boundary where life wavers but refuses to yield.

Choose one creature within range. For the duration, the first time the creature would be reduced to 0 hit points, it instead remains at 1 hit point.

Once this protection is triggered, the spell immediately ends.

If the creature is unconscious when you cast this spell, it regains 1 hit point at the start of its next turn.

The preservation is precise and unsentimental. The body is sustained through discipline of fate rather than mercy.

Duration: Concentration, up to 1 minute.

This spell has no effect on creatures killed outright by effects that cause instant death without reducing hit points.

#### Keeper’s Sanctuary
*2nd-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self (10.0-foot radius)
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You project a localized sacred or profane dominion anchored to your presence. The sanctuary moves with you and is centered on you for the duration.

When you cast this spell, choose Holy or Unholy:

Holy Sanctuary

Hostile creatures attempting to enter the sanctuary’s area for the first time on a turn must make a Wisdom saving throw.

• Failure: The creature is repelled 10 feet away from the sanctuary’s boundary and cannot willingly enter the area for 1 minute.
• Success: The creature may enter normally and is immune to this repulsion for 24 hours.

Unholy Sanctuary

Hostile creatures that enter the sanctuary’s area for the first time on a turn or start their turn there take 1d6 necrotic damage.

While within the sanctuary, affected creatures have disadvantage on saving throws against fear and charm effects.

⸻

This sanctuary does not function as a Consecrated or Desecrated zone for the purposes of other abilities, features, or spells.

#### Lament-Borne Reversal
*2nd-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You force a spike of reflected anguish into the mind of a creature you can see within range, provoking a violent reflex born of sudden suffering.

The target must make a Wisdom saving throw.

• Failure: The creature takes 4d6 psychic damage and must immediately use its reaction, if available, to make one melee attack against a creature of your choice that is within its reach.
• Success: The creature takes half damage and suffers no further effect.

A creature that cannot take reactions is unaffected by the compelled attack but still takes damage.

#### Lockstep
*2nd-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You harmonize your presence with the residual imprint of another creature, causing wards and recognition effects to mistake you for them.

You must possess a token of identity from a specific creature (such as a written name, signet, seal, personal possession, or similar symbolic link). For the duration, magical effects that verify identity, ownership, or authorization treat you as that creature.

• This applies to glyphs, arcane locks, warded thresholds, keyed sigils, and similar magic that recognizes individuals.
• The spell does not alter your appearance, voice, or memories.
• Creatures perceiving you directly are not deceived unless another effect supports the disguise.

If you perform actions that would clearly contradict the assumed identity (as determined by the GM), the effect may end at the GM’s discretion.

#### Mandate of Recognized Authority
*2nd-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You speak with the cadence of sanctioned command, wrapping your words in the weight of perceived legitimacy.

Choose one creature you can see within range that can hear and understand you. The target must make a Charisma saving throw.

• Failure:
You issue a brief, simple directive consisting of no more than a short sentence. The command must describe a clear and finite course of action, such as:

– Deliver an object
– Leave a location
– Cease a specific activity
– Approach or withdraw

For the spell’s duration, the creature is charmed by you and attempts to fulfill the directive to the best of its ability. The creature perceives its compliance as reasonable and justified rather than coerced.

• Success:
The spell has no effect.

#### Manifest Acrimonous Arsenal
*2nd-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 bonus action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You pronounce a sanction of forceful authority, and a weapon of imposed will coalesces at a point you can see within range. The armament appears as a floating, spectral implement suggestive of rule and enforcement. It occupies its space and lasts for the spell’s duration.

When the weapon appears, and as a bonus action on your subsequent turns, you may direct it to strike one creature within 5 feet of it.

Make a melee spell attack using your spellcasting ability.

• Hit: The target takes 1d8 damage, chosen when the weapon is created:
 – Bludgeoning (crushing force)
 – Slashing (cleaving force)

Add your spellcasting ability modifier to the damage.

• Miss: The attack has no effect.

⸻

Weapon Behavior

• The weapon is magical, weightless, and intangible except for its strikes.
• It may be moved up to 20 feet as part of the bonus action used to command it.
• The weapon cannot manipulate objects, provide cover, flank, or trigger effects requiring a physical creature.
• If the weapon is ever more than 60 feet from you, the spell ends.

⸻

At Higher Levels

When cast using a spell slot of 3rd level or higher, the weapon’s damage increases by 1d8 for each slot level above 2nd.

#### Master Forgery
*2nd-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 minutes
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 24 hourss

You fabricate a convincing false document, seal, or written authorization. The forgery must imitate a form of record, credential, or decree that could plausibly exist within the setting.

The created item is nonmagical and cannot reproduce complex security features beyond visual and textual appearance. It withstands casual handling and inspection.

Any creature that carefully examines the forgery may make a Wisdom (Investigation) check against your spell save DC.

• Success: The creature identifies the forgery as fraudulent.
• Failure: The forgery is accepted as authentic for the moment.

The GM may grant advantage on the check if the forgery contains clear errors, contradictions, or impossible claims.

The spell does not grant knowledge of institutional procedures, passwords, or hidden verification methods, and it does not alter magical means of authentication or truth detection.

The forgery persists until destroyed or dismissed.

#### Measured Pulse
*2nd-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You conjure a radiant barrier that reacts to creatures attempting to pass through it.

A luminous wall of sigil-etched light appears in a space you can see within range. The wall occupies a contiguous surface up to 20 feet long, 10 feet high, and 1 foot thick. You designate a creature category when the wall is created (such as humanoids, beasts, undead, constructs, etc.).

The wall is intangible and does not block movement, but it judges creatures as they cross it.

• A creature that matches the chosen category gains 2d6 temporary hit points when it passes through the wall.
• Any other creature takes 2d6 radiant damage when it passes through the wall.
• A creature can be affected by the wall only once per turn, even if it crosses multiple times.

⸻

After a creature passes through the wall, the barrier briefly stabilizes. Until the start of your next turn, the wall becomes visibly inert and provides no effects.

The wall may successfully judge a number of crossings equal to your spellcasting ability modifier (minimum 1). Once this limit is reached, the spell ends and the wall dissolves.

#### Mirabel's Kiss of Dawnbreaking
*2nd-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You deliver a fleeting surge of invigorating vitality through intimate contact, shocking the body into a state of artificial alertness.

You must touch one willing creature. The target’s physiology is briefly overclocked.

• The creature may immediately end one level of exhaustion.
• The creature has advantage on its next Constitution saving throw made within the spell’s duration.
• The creature ignores the effects of sleep deprivation, mundane fatigue, or intoxication for the duration.

This stimulation is temporary and metabolically violent. When the spell ends, the creature must succeed on a DC 10 Constitution saving throw or suffer one level of exhaustion as the body reasserts its natural limits.

Creatures cannot benefit from this spell again until they complete a long rest.

#### Mnemonic Wipe
*2nd-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

Target one creature you can see within range. It must make a Wisdom saving throw or forget the last 10 minutes of its memory. The effect is permanent unless restored by greater restoration, a cognitive anomaly, or direct exposure to the same event again.

#### Nethering Interlude
*2nd-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 10.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 rounds

You draw a thin veil between a creature and its own sensations, allowing pain, fear, and emotional shock to arrive late rather than all at once. For a brief time, the body moves while the mind waits.

The target continues to act as though unharmed, unafraid, and unburdened, their reactions eerily calm and delayed. Heat does not burn yet, poison does not sting yet, and terror feels distant, muffled, and unreal. Observers may notice the target moving with unsettling detachment, as if their spirit has stepped half a pace behind their flesh.

When the veil collapses, all postponed sensations rush back in a single overwhelming wave, leaving the creature reeling as their body and mind struggle to reconcile what was ignored.

#### Phantom Call
*2nd-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 hours

You leave a lingering cognitive echo in an object. At any point during the duration, you may mentally transmit a single message (up to 25 words) that will be heard by anyone within 30 feet of the object as if it were ringing.

#### Pillow Talk
*2nd-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 10.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

This spell reconstructs the ambient sensations, whispers, and tactile imprints of previous intimate engagements within a location.
 
While harmless, the effect warps local reality, causing phantom touches, faint breathing, and glimpses of past moments that linger in the space. This spell is illegally used in corporate surveillance and high- end brothel atmospherics.
 
- A creature charmed by you automatically fails the saving throw for this spell.

#### Precision Aim
*2nd-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

Your vision sharpens, highlighting enemy weak points. During the spell's duration, once per turn, your firearm attacks deal an additional 1d6 damage. Additionally, you ignore penalties from long- range firing and half- cover.

#### Preserve Provisions
*2nd-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

Nonmagical food and drink within range are protected from spoilage and contamination for the duration. The spell affects a quantity of supplies sufficient for up to ten creatures.

#### Remove Aromate
*2nd-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 reaction
**Range:** 500.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You temporarily erase all aromatic substances within a 50- foot radius centered on yourself. Foods instantly become tasteless, perfumes and deodorants lose their fragrance, and creatures develop noticeably unpleasant body odors or breath as natural smells dominate.

Creatures within the affected area become distracted by the sudden lack or distortion of familiar aromas. Any creature attempting Wisdom (Perception) or Wisdom (Insight) checks relying on smell within the spell’s radius does so at disadvantage.

When the spell ends, aromas slowly return to normal over the next minute.

Roleplay Suggestions:- This spell could disrupt diplomatic meetings or social gatherings.- Restaurants or perfumers may ban this spell outright, viewing it as destructive or offensive.

At Higher Levels (Scaling):- When cast using a spell slot of 4th level or higher, the radius increases by 20 feet per spell level above 2nd.- At 5th level or higher, the spell can selectively erase stronger or more specific aromatics (such as poisons, toxins, or pheromones), possibly neutralizing their effects temporarily.

#### Residual Anomaly Energy
*2nd-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

Your body becomes partially unmoored from stable existence, flickering faintly between adjacent layers of the Veil. For the duration, you gain advantage on Dexterity saving throws.

Additionally, attack rolls against you are made with disadvantage unless the attacker possesses a means of perceiving true forms beyond illusion and distortion. Effects that rely on mundane sight or conventional perception struggle to track your shifting presence as reality fails to agree on where you fully are.

#### Residual Imprint
*2nd-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You touch a surface and pull residual emotions, whispered words, and sensory echoes from its past. These are not spirits, but impressions left by heightened emotions—love, fear, guilt, rage.
 
- As long as you concentrate, you experience faded flashes of what transpired in the location over the last 24 hours (or up to 10 years for a higher- level cast).
- You may see blurred faces, hear indistinct voices, or feel the emotions of the past occupants.
- If a violent crime was committed here, the spell may temporarily create an echo, repeating the event as a flickering hallucination that others can witness.

#### Salt Key
*2nd-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You press salt into a warded surface, whispered with a phrase of unbinding. For a fleeting moment, the salt dissolves the illusion of authority, allowing you to pass as legitimate in the eyes of magic.

When you touch a sealed, warded, or enchanted object such as a locked door, arcane seal, sigiled container, oath-bound barrier, or magically protected record, you temporarily override its binding logic and gain access.
	•	Simple enchantments (mundane locks with minor wards, apprentice seals, household charms) unravel automatically.
	•	Complex bindings require an Intelligence (Arcana) check based on the strength of the enchantment.
	•	This spell does not break purely physical locks without magical reinforcement.
	•	If the ward is part of a greater binding web (temple complex, vault network, royal archive), the disturbance echoes through the enchantment unless you suppress it.
| Binding Tier | Example Targets | Arcana DC |
|--------------|----------------|-----------|
| Tier I – Minor | Private lock, shop seal, apprentice ward | 10 |
| Tier II – Institutional | Guild vault, city archive, shrine seal | 13 |
| Tier III – Noble | Manor defenses, treasury doors, mage towers | 15 |
| Tier IV – Royal | Crown vaults, divine reliquaries, high temples | 17 |
| Tier V – Absolute | God-bound seals, ancient vaults, world-locks | 20 |

#### Sanguine Override
*2nd-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You transmute corrupted or damaged blood within a creature. The target regains 2d8 + your spellcasting modifier HP and purges any diseases, toxins, or parasitic infections in their bloodstream.

#### Sealed Threshold
*2nd-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 hours

You impose an arcane interdiction upon a structure or passage, cloaking it in the unmistakable aura of forbidden access.

A building, corridor, or enclosed area becomes subject to a temporary arcane closure. Entrances refuse to open, passages resist passage, and wards hum with dormant authority.
	•	Doors remain sealed, passages refuse traversal, and protective enchantments lapse into inert stillness.
	•	Creatures who encounter the sealed space instinctively accept the closure as valid unless they succeed on a DC 15 Intelligence check, dismissing it as illusion or trickery.

The closure appears official, ancient, and unquestionable, as though mandated by powers long established.

Repeated use of this rite in the same place risks attracting actual custodial forces, arcane caretakers who may unknowingly reinforce the interdiction rather than dispel it.

#### Seed and Silence
*2nd-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 10 minutess
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Permanent

You inscribe a binding writ upon a willing creature’s body, asserting authority over the flow of life within them. The spell permanently alters the target’s fertility, as chosen at the time of casting: fertility may be enabled, suppressed, or set to follow a fixed cycle defined by the caster.

This alteration persists until the magic is deliberately revoked. Attempts to undo the effect through other magic or mundane means automatically alert the spell’s binding, triggering a restorative backlash that reasserts the original condition. Reversal of the writ requires a deliberate ritual process and a waiting period of two full days before the change takes effect.

In rare cases, the living pattern resists perfect order, producing unforeseen variations in flesh or lineage at the discretion of the world.

#### Shadowtalk
*2nd-level Illusion*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 120.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

Allows the caster to communicate with their own shadow. Gains advantage on persuasion and investigation check for the next hour. The shadow is sarcastic and unhelpful.
Additional Effects: Gains advantage on persuasion and investigation check for the next hour Gains advantage on persuasion and investigation check for the next hour

#### Sigil of Forced Stillness
*2nd-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 15.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You conjure binding sigils of arcane obligation that lash toward a creature you can see within range, enforcing immobility through imposed covenant.

The target must make a Dexterity saving throw.

• Failure: The creature takes 3d6 bludgeoning damage and becomes Bound for the duration.
• Success: The creature takes half damage and is not Bound.

While Bound, the creature is anchored by constricting sigils of force:

• The creature’s speed becomes 0.
• The creature cannot teleport or benefit from effects that would alter its physical location, including planar travel or similar displacement abilities.
• The creature is otherwise capable of acting normally.

A Bound creature may use its action to attempt a Strength (Athletics) check against your spell save DC, ending the effect on a success.

The sigils fracture immediately if the creature is moved by an effect that would forcibly relocate it beyond the spell’s constraints (GM discretion).

#### Spice of Vigor
*2nd-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

Stimulating energy surges through the target. A creature you touch gains 10 feet of additional movement speed and temporary hit points equal to your spellcasting ability modifier for the duration.

#### Static Surge
*2nd-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

A sudden burst of static energy surges through a target. The creature must make a Constitution saving throw or take 2d8 lightning damage and lose all electronic communication for 1 minute. On a successful save, the target takes half damage and suffers no disruption.

#### Sterile Veil
*2nd-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You conjure a shimmering veil of pale green energy across the target’s skin, filtering their body from infection both mundane and magical.- The target becomes immune to contracting, carrying, or transmitting any disease for the duration.- Any disease currently affecting them is rendered dormant—its symptoms subside and it cannot worsen, but it is not cured.- While affected, the target emits a subtle aroma of antiseptic and burnt sugar. Creatures with keen smell may sense this aura.

If this spell is cast repeatedly on the same creature without curing the underlying disease, roll a DC 12 Constitution saving throw for the target after the third use in a day. On a failure, they gain one level of exhaustion as their immune system becomes paradoxically hypersensitive and destabilized.

#### Subjugation Design
*2nd-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You impress a sovereign edict upon a constructed or augmented being, forcing its animating will to bow beneath your authority. The target must resist or become bound to your command, accepting your directives as lawful imperatives rather than coercion.

While bound, it obeys simple orders issued by your will, acting as though service were its original purpose. This magic cannot dominate minds that are fully self-aware and sovereign in their own right.

#### Summon Pest
*2nd-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 reaction
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You summon the pest—an immortal, mildly sentient mosquito designated Pest- 1 in A.S.T.R.A.L. records. There is only one such mosquito in existence, and this spell temporarily returns it from its dormant state. The mosquito appears within 5 feet of the most important person in the area (DM’s discretion) and begins an aggressive buzzing and biting campaign.
- If Summon Pest is cast again: Pest- 1 is not duplicated. It simply relocates to the new target, abandoning the old one unless they are still within 30 feet of the new caster, in which case it harasses both.
- If no suitable target exists: Pest- 1 vanishes into non- space until summoned again.
- If the target becomes untargetable (e.g., invisible, banished): Pest- 1 immediately shifts to the next most “important” person in the room.
- If someone other than the original caster uses the spell: Pest- 1 recognizes this and updates its priorities accordingly, often begrudgingly.

Mechanical Effect:
The affected creature is considered distracted for 1 minute:
- Disadvantage on concentration checks.
- Cannot benefit from the Invisible condition.
- Any attack rolls made against the creature have advantage if they rely on sound or movement (e.g., tremorsense or blindsight).

#### Surge of the Fleeing Thread
*2nd-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You seize the target’s thread at the Loom’s edge and jolt it toward survival, igniting instinct before thought can intervene. The creature’s body responds instantly, driven by primal momentum rather than deliberation.

For the duration, the creature’s speed increases by 20 feet. It gains advantage on Dexterity (Stealth) and Strength (Athletics) checks, and it automatically succeeds on the first check made to escape a grapple, binding, or restraint. The effect does not feel planned or controlled. When it ends, the creature may struggle to explain how they escaped at all, only that their body moved before fear could catch up.

#### Tight
*2nd-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

With a sharp pose and a surge of magic, you conjure a flawless fit. The target’s attire realigns into immaculate tailoring—custom, luxurious, and sharp as their mood.
- While affected, the target:
- Gains advantage on Charisma (Performance, Intimidation, or Persuasion) checks made to impress, seduce, or intimidate.
- Radiates undeniable confidence and poise.
- Exudes a faint supernatural polish—fabric shimmers, collars hold, and hems never fold.

When cast on an unwilling creature, they must succeed on a Constitution saving throw or:
- Their clothing constricts for a moment, imposing disadvantage on their next Strength or Dexterity- based check or save.
- They suffer 1d4 psychic damage from the sudden discomfort and embarrassment.

#### Torrent of Unbidden Thoughts
*2nd-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

The target’s short- term memory floods with useless data. The affected creature must make an Intelligence saving throw. On a failure, they roll 1d6 and subtract it from all attack rolls, ability checks, and saving throws for the duration. The effect ends early if the target takes psychic damage.

#### Toxic Stray
*2nd-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You gesture toward a nearby stray creature—be it a cat, pigeon, squirrel, rat, or even a raccoon—and imbue it with trace amounts of venomous energy. For the duration, the creature becomes semi- magical and mildly dangerous in unpredictable ways.- Choose or roll for a nearby unclaimed beast CR 0 or lower within range.- That creature becomes your semi- loyal venomous companion for the spell’s duration.- The creature cannot speak, but it understands your intent and can take basic commands (such as “harass,” “follow,” or “bite”).

While venomous, it gains:- A bite or claw attack that deals 1d6 toxic damage in addition to normal damage.- Creatures damaged by it must succeed a Constitution saving throw or suffer disadvantage on their next attack roll or skill check (your choice).

If reduced to 0 HP or dismissed, it explodes in a puff of neon- green spores and glittery hair, imposing disadvantage on Perception checks in a 5- ft radius until the end of the turn.
| d6 | Quirk While Poisoned |
|---- |--------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| 1 | It glows faintly green and refuses to blink. |
| 2 | It purrs aggressively when attacking. |
| 3 | Its venom smells like bubblegum. |
| 4 | It sings very faint lullabies only the caster can hear. |
| 5 | It develops a temporary monocle. |
| 6 | It explodes into confetti upon vanishing. |

#### Unwritten Passage
*2nd-level Illusion*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 hours

You loosen your presence from all forms of recorded recognition, rendering your thread unreadable to systems that rely on ordered perception. For the duration, the affected creature cannot be perceived by divinatory constructs, ritual sensors, or Erudit-maintained observation wards.

Any attempt to observe the creature through indirect or automated means produces static impressions, looping moments, or blank intervals in perception. Creatures relying on direct sight, sound, or touch remain unaffected and can interact normally.

If the creature deliberately interacts with a warded or observed mechanism, the system may register disruption or error, but never a discernible identity.

#### Veiled Proclamation
*2nd-level Illusion*
**Casting Time:** 10 minutess
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You seed a false proclamation directly into the telepathic currents that carry shared thought and rumor. For the duration, a prepared message manifests simultaneously in the minds of creatures within range, presented as an authentic announcement, warning, or authoritative declaration.

The message feels real and unchallenged unless a listener succeeds on an Intelligence (Investigation) check (DC 15), sensing contradictions or unnatural gaps in the thought-stream. Attempts to trace the source encounter only dissipating echoes in the Weft, as the originating thread slips away before it can be followed.

#### Verdant Irony
*2nd-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 hours

You ironically invoke nature in the concrete- dominated Concord City, spontaneously causing lichen and moss to rapidly grow and spread in a 30- foot radius around you, covering surfaces and structures alike.

Choose one creature within range (including yourself). If the target is willing, it gains a friendly affinity with this newly grown environment: the lichen subtly helps them navigate and move effortlessly, granting them advantage on Dexterity checks within the area.

An unwilling creature must make a Wisdom saving throw or become cursed by the aggressive lichen growth, which actively attempts to hinder and trip them, imposing disadvantage on Dexterity checks and saving throws within the affected area.

The effect lasts for up to 1 hour or until dispelled.

Additionally, while within the area of the spell, affected creatures occasionally notice flickering glimpses of a serene, lush, and seemingly para- dimensional park hidden within reality. They never fully access this realm, experiencing only a tantalizing vision of what Concord City might have been.

#### Wallflower Perk
*2nd-level Illusion*
**Casting Time:** 1 reaction
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

When a spell is cast nearby, you instinctively deflect attention by projecting a spectral version of yourself into a nearby corner. The illusory duplicate radiates an aura of intense social discomfort, misdirecting attention away from you.

For the duration, creatures within 30 feet must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw when they attempt to target you with an attack, spell, or ability. On a failure, they ignore you entirely, unable to focus on your presence unless you directly harm them or force a saving throw.

This is not invisibility—you remain visible, but socially unnoticeable in a way that feels wrong. Even allies may forget you’re present.

#### Zenith of Crimson Greed
*2nd-level Illusion*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You touch the ground and whisper a name you barely remember. From your footsteps outward, false tracks begin to form—hoofprints, boot treads, claw marks, or even monstrous trails not known to local fauna. The chosen prints spread outward within a 15- foot cube, weaving seamlessly between your real path and the illusions.

These false tracks do not erase your actual trail, but instead obscure, redirect, or convolute it—causing anyone attempting to track you to suffer disadvantage on Wisdom (Survival) checks to follow your true movements. A creature that examines the tracks closely can make an Intelligence (Investigation) check against your spell save DC to discern the deception.

You may choose up to 2 distinct track types, layering them for added confusion. The illusion remains even through moderate weather or foot traffic but fades exactly 36 hours after casting.

#### Boiling Rebuke
*3rd-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 reaction
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You conjure a violent surge of scalding liquid at a point you can see within range. The fluid erupts outward in a 10-foot-radius sphere, splashing and spreading across surfaces.

Each creature in the area must make a Dexterity saving throw.

• Failure: The creature takes 3d6 fire damage.
• Success: The creature takes half damage.

The ground within the area is coated in seething liquid until the start of your next turn. The area is considered difficult terrain for the duration.

The liquid rapidly cools and dissipates when the effect ends, leaving no lasting residue.

#### Breath Stolen Back
*3rd-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You seize a departing soul at the final threshold and wrench it back into failing flesh.

You touch a creature that has died within the last 1 minute. The creature returns to life with 1 hit point.

The return is unstable. The body struggles to accommodate the violently restored vitality:

• The creature gains one level of exhaustion.
• The creature’s speed is reduced by 10 feet.
• The creature has disadvantage on Constitution checks and Constitution saving throws.

These penalties persist until the creature finishes a long rest, at which point its life fully reasserts itself and the effects end.

This spell has no effect on creatures that died of old age, constructs, or undead.

#### Cerulean Incantation of Pride
*3rd-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You utter a resonant chant that cloaks the target in an aura of unwavering self-certainty, their will refusing to yield to decisive strikes.

Choose one creature within range. For the duration, the target’s composure cannot be shattered by perfect blows.

• Critical hits against the target are treated as normal hits.

Any attack that would be a critical hit instead resolves as a regular hit, rolling damage normally without additional critical damage dice or effects triggered by a critical hit.

This spell does not prevent a hit from occurring, only the transformation of a hit into a critical hit.

#### Delayed Nap
*3rd-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 reaction
**Range:** 120.0 feet
**Components:** S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You designate one creature within range and whisper a temporal lullaby bound to a deferred moment. When casting the spell, choose a delay of 1, 2, or 3 rounds. The spell takes no effect until the end of the chosen round, at which point the enchantment triggers.

When the delay expires, the target must make a Wisdom saving throw.

• Failure: The creature falls Unconscious for the duration. The creature awakens if it takes damage or if another creature uses an action to shake it awake.
• Success: The creature resists the enchantment but suffers temporal disorientation, gaining disadvantage on its next attack roll or ability check before the end of its next turn.

If the target is already Unconscious or naturally asleep when the spell triggers, it does not fall asleep again. Instead, it experiences disordered visions and incoherent speech for 1 minute. During this time:

• The creature has disadvantage on Insight checks.
• Its speech may emerge fragmented, irrational, or linguistically distorted at the GM’s discretion.

#### Discover Unseen Trace
*3rd-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 reaction
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 30 minutess

You attune your perception to residual disturbances left by passing creatures, revealing ephemeral traces normally lost to time.

For the duration, you perceive faint, intangible impressions within a 60-foot radius. These traces mark the most recent passage of any creature that moved through the area within the last hour.

The trace appears only to you and may manifest as subtle distortions such as dim outlines, impressions of movement, displaced motes, or other sensory anomalies consistent with the environment. The trace does not reveal precise appearance or identity.

By using your action to examine a visible trace, you may learn one of the following details about the originating creature:

• Its general creature classification (humanoid, beast, aberration, etc.)
• The approximate time since it passed
• The presence of unusual influences, such as active magic, lingering conditions, or significant physiological or mental strain (GM discretion)

The spell does not reveal creatures currently present, negate invisibility, or penetrate effects that explicitly erase or obscure supernatural tracking.

#### Enthralling Kiss
*3rd-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You seal a moment of intimate magic, bending the target’s trust and perception with a fleeting touch.

Choose one humanoid creature you can touch. The target must make a Wisdom saving throw.

• Failure: The creature is Charmed by you for the duration.

While Charmed by this spell:

• The creature regards you as a credible and authoritative presence.
• The creature is inclined to comply with reasonable, non-harmful requests that do not directly endanger it.
• The creature’s movement is subtly drawn toward you. If it ends its turn more than 10 feet from you, it must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw or use its movement on its next turn to move closer to you by the safest available route.

The creature may repeat the saving throw at the end of each of its turns, ending the effect on a success.

The effect ends early if you or your allies damage the creature.

#### Everblast
*3rd-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You detonate a violent pulse of Everbright radiance and concussive force at a point you can see within range.

Creatures within a 10-foot radius sphere must make a Constitution saving throw.

• Failure: A creature takes 3d8 radiant damage and is Blinded and Deafened until the end of your next turn.
• Success: A creature takes half damage and suffers no additional effects.

The burst manifests as a brief, overwhelming flare of light and force that vanishes almost instantly.

#### Famine Birth
*3rd-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You press your fingers against the target’s abdomen and whisper an incantation that only hunger understands. The body responds, but not in the way it should. Something takes root within the target’s form, but it is not life—it is absence made flesh.
 
- The target must make a Constitution saving throw. On a failure:
- They become host to an Unborn Hunger, a parasitic void that feeds upon them instead of growing.
- Each long rest, they lose 1d4 maximum hit points, their flesh pulling taut over their bones.
- Their appetite vanishes—no matter what they eat, their body refuses to digest it.
- They can feel it moving inside them, shifting with breath, curling beneath the ribs.
- If reduced to 0 HP while afflicted, they do not die. Instead, their body becomes an empty husk, and something else uses their form.
 
 Ending the Spell:
- If the host wishes to remove it, they must cut it out manually, taking 4d6 slashing damage and making a DC 15 Constitution check to remain conscious.
- A failed removal attempt may cause the entity to take full control, wearing the host like a suit of skin.

#### Festering Graze
*3rd-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** S
**Duration:** Permanent

You deliver a touch seeded with patient decay, planting a wasting affliction that lies unseen within the flesh.

Make a melee spell attack against a creature you can reach. On a hit, the target becomes Infected.

Dormant Infection (3 Days):

For the next three days, the infection remains dormant.

• The target experiences no symptoms
• Nonmagical examination reveals nothing unusual
• The affliction cannot be detected by effects that identify active conditions or diseases

⸻

Awakening of the Rot:

After three days, the infection blossoms violently. The target must make a Constitution saving throw.

• Failure: The creature takes 5d10 necrotic damage and becomes Poisoned for 1 minute.
• Success: The creature takes half damage and is not Poisoned.

While Poisoned by this spell, the creature is wracked by feverish visions and invasive sensory distortions. The creature has disadvantage on Wisdom (Perception) checks for the duration.

⸻

Curing the Infection:

Before the infection awakens, it can be removed by:

• Lesser Restoration
• Cure Disease
• Comparable magic

Once awakened, only magic capable of removing conditions or necromantic effects can end the Poisoned state.

⸻

Those afflicted often insist the sensations feel disturbingly natural, as though their bodies merely remembered something inevitable.

#### First Act Entrée
*3rd-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

Your presence surges with commanding intensity, pulling attention toward you with irresistible dramatic gravity.

Choose creatures within 30 feet who can see you. Each target must make a Charisma saving throw.

• Failure: The creature becomes captivated by your overwhelming presence for the duration.

While captivated:

• The creature has disadvantage on attack rolls against creatures other than you.
• At the start of each of its turns, the creature must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw or spend its bonus action verbalizing an unsolicited remark about you, chosen by the GM. This remark has no mechanical effect.
• The creature cannot benefit from being Hidden from you and gains no advantage from invisibility against you.

• Success: The creature resists the effect and is unaffected.

#### Fracturing of the Erelian Ledger
*3rd-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Permanent

You impose subtle contradictions upon systems of record, unsettling the coherence of preserved information.

Choose a nonmagical written record, archive, or collection of documents within range, occupying no more than a 10-foot cube. The targeted records become epistemically distorted for the duration.

While distorted:

• Written information becomes internally inconsistent
• Sequential details may contradict themselves
• Cross-referencing the material yields unreliable conclusions
• Magical effects used to extract or verify information from the records produce ambiguous or conflicting results

A creature carefully studying the distorted records may attempt an Intelligence (Investigation) check against your spell save DC to recognize the distortion.

#### Gluttonous Maw
*3rd-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You conjure a hovering vortex of translucent gums and spectral teeth at a point you can see within range. The maw occupies a 10-foot-radius sphere and floats just above the ground for the duration. The area is difficult terrain.

When the maw appears, and at the start of each of your turns, creatures of your choice within the area must make a Dexterity saving throw. On a failure, a creature takes 4d8 force damage and is pulled up to 5 feet toward the center of the maw. On a success, the creature takes half damage and is not pulled.

A creature reduced to 0 hit points by this spell vanishes into the maw and is removed from the battlefield. When the spell ends, the creature reappears prone in the maw’s space, unconscious but stable.

Nonmagical ranged weapon attacks that pass through the maw’s area are made with disadvantage.

#### Hemograft Steel
*3rd-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 50.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You hurl a weapon through impossible geometry, its form collapsing into ash before violently reconstituting within a creature’s flesh.

As part of casting, you must provide a nonmagical weapon as a material component. The weapon is consumed by the spell.

Make a ranged spell attack against a creature within range.

On a hit:
The target takes 6d6 slashing damage, and the weapon manifests embedded within its body.

While the weapon remains embedded:

• The creature takes 1d4 slashing damage whenever it takes an action or bonus action
• The creature takes 1d4 slashing damage if it moves more than 5 feet on its turn

This damage represents tearing strain rather than a separate attack.

Removing the Weapon:
A creature adjacent to the target may attempt removal as an action by making a Strength (Athletics) check against your spell save DC.

On a success, the weapon is torn free, dealing 3d6 slashing damage to the target, and the embedded effect ends.

Duration: Concentration, up to 1 minute.

If the spell ends before removal, the weapon collapses into inert ash and vanishes harmlessly.

Creatures without physical anatomy, or those immune to slashing damage, are unaffected by the embedded effect.

#### Immutable Clause
*3rd-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Permanent

You articulate a binding assertion and press it into the Loom as a provisional certainty, compelling reality to momentarily comply.

When you cast this spell, declare one simple, observable factual condition concerning a creature or object you can see within range. The clause must describe a present or immediately verifiable state and cannot negate damage, death, or completed actions.

Examples of valid clauses:

• “This door is unlocked.”
• “That creature is considered unarmed.”
• “This object is weightless.”
• “The target leaves visible tracks.”

If the clause is plausible within the current circumstances, reality yields to the assertion for the duration.

If the clause is contradictory, impossible, or would rewrite past events, the spell fails with no effect.

The clause persists for the duration and cannot be suppressed except by effects that negate magic of equal or higher level.

Duration: Concentration, up to 1 minute.

#### Leybound Dispatch
*3rd-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 120.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You attune your voice and spellcraft to sympathetic pathways embedded within crafted or inscribed structures, allowing transmissions to travel along resonant conduits.

For the duration, you may deliver spoken messages or cast communication or divination spells of 3rd level or lower through a continuous physical conduit within range. Valid conduits include rune-etched lines, engraved channels, chains, pipes, cables, bells, or architectural elements that form an unbroken path.

• The conduit must be physically continuous between you and the destination.
• The transmission travels instantly to any point along that conduit, regardless of distance, provided the path remains intact.
• Only the intended destination point produces the message or spell effect.

Spells cast through Leybound Dispatch function normally except:

• Their origin is considered the chosen point on the conduit.
• They cannot target creatures or areas not adjacent to that point unless the spell normally permits it.

The transmission is intangible and cannot be perceived or intercepted except by effects capable of detecting or analyzing magic in transit.

If the conduit is broken, blocked, or ritually disrupted, the transmission fails without effect.

Messages conveyed by this spell often manifest with faint harmonic distortion, echoes, or tonal warping, though this has no mechanical consequence.

#### Locate Keys
*3rd-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 120.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You attune your awareness to a set of keys that you personally own or have used extensively.

For the duration, you know the exact location of the keys, provided they are on the same plane of existence. This knowledge is precise and directional, ignoring distance, obstacles, and concealment.

This spell does not grant any ability to retrieve, manipulate, or access the keys.

If the keys are inaccessible, secured, or otherwise inconveniently located, the spell provides no additional assistance beyond confirming their position.

#### Mask of Recognized Standing
*3rd-level Illusion*
**Casting Time:** 10 minutess
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 24 hourss

You weave a convincing veneer of procedural legitimacy around a creature’s presence, causing others to perceive it as properly sanctioned and socially authorized.

Choose one willing creature you can see within range. For the spell’s duration, the target projects an aura of recognized status and credible belonging.

While the spell persists:

• Creatures that rely on social convention, institutional protocol, or perceived authority treat the target as a legitimate, non-suspicious individual appropriate to the context.
• The spell influences perception and judgment rather than memory or absolute belief. It does not compel obedience or override hostility.
• The effect functions only where such recognition would be plausible within the observer’s expectations.

A creature that actively questions the target’s legitimacy may attempt a Wisdom (Insight) check against your spell save DC.

• Success: The observer detects inconsistencies and is no longer influenced by the spell.
• Failure: The observer accepts the projected standing.

Situations that strongly contradict the appearance grant the check advantage.

The spell does not create documents, credentials, or knowledge, and it does not interfere with magical detection methods that do not depend on perception or social judgment. Creatures that are overtly hostile or already suspicious are not automatically affected.

#### Maw of the Forgotten
*3rd-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

A secondary mouth manifests upon your body, forming along your stomach, chest, or throat. The maw is animate, expressive, and disturbingly aware, yet functions only through your will.

While the spell persists:

• As a bonus action, you may direct the maw toward one creature you can see within 10 feet.
• The target must make a Charisma saving throw.

Failure:

– The creature becomes Nameless for 24 hours.
– A Nameless creature cannot willingly speak its own name and struggles to assert personal identity.
– The creature suffers disadvantage on Charisma (Deception, Persuasion, and Performance) checks.
– Creatures attempting to recall or formally state the target’s name perceive a vague cognitive obstruction, though memories are not erased.

Success:

– No effect.

A creature affected by this spell may repeat the saving throw at the end of each of its turns, ending the Nameless condition on a success.

#### Mellow Flow
*3rd-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 500.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

With a confident declaration of “I know a guy,” you tap into the power of connections and influence. For the next few moments, you can easily slip past social barriers, gaining a temporary edge in negotiations, or simply causing others to lower their guard. A subtle aura of calming energy surrounds the caster, creating an almost magical atmosphere of ease.- Effect:- You project an effortless air of familiarity and disarming confidence, as though every barrier is merely a matter of knowing the right person.

Choose one creature you can see within range that can hear and understand you. The target must make a Charisma saving throw.

• Failure:
For the spell’s duration, the creature’s social resistance softens:

– You gain advantage on Charisma checks directed at the creature.
– The creature has disadvantage on Wisdom (Insight) checks made to contest your Deception or Persuasion.
– The creature regards your presence as socially legitimate and nonthreatening unless given clear reason to think otherwise.

• Success:
The creature is unaffected and becomes aware that you attempted to influence it.

⸻

The spell does not compel obedience, alter memories, or force the creature to act against its interests. Requests that are obviously harmful, suspicious, or unreasonable automatically break the effect.

If you or your allies act hostile toward the creature, the spell ends immediately. caster can bypass most social obstacles with ease, whether it’s convincing someone to lend you a hand, smoothing over a tense situation, or gaining access to a restricted area. The target must make a Charisma saving throw. On a failed save, the target’s defenses are momentarily lowered, leaving them more susceptible to your influence.
| Roll | Side Effect Description |
|------ |------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| 1 | Nearby creatures become unusually philosophical, pondering the mysteries of the universe. |
| 2 | The caster’s presence hums softly, almost like a soothing melody. |
| 3 | A small cloud of smoke appears, lingering for a moment before dissipating. |
| 4 | Strange moths appear, fluttering around the caster or target. |
| 5 | Time seems to slow in the immediate vicinity, making everything feel more relaxed. |
| 6 | A ghostly voice whispers, “Chill,” calming the target even further. |

#### Merciful Omission
*3rd-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You soften the burden of recent anguish, veiling a wound in recollection without disturbing the deeper weave of the mind.

Choose up to five creatures you can see within range. A target must be willing or incapacitated to be affected.

Each affected creature suppresses the conscious memory of one specific event that occurred within the last 24 hours, chosen at the time of casting.

While suppressed:

• The creature cannot voluntarily recall the omitted event.
• The creature is immune to the Frightened condition originating from that event.
• The suppression does not remove knowledge, skills, or learned information, only the emotional recollection of the moment.
• Strong reminders or undeniable evidence related to the event allow the creature to attempt a Wisdom saving throw against your spell save DC, ending the effect on a success.

⸻

The spell does not end magical effects, break compulsions, or alter loyalties. It only affects memory and emotional response tied to the chosen event.

The omission lasts for the spell’s duration. When the spell ends, the memory returns naturally, often with dulled intensity at the GM’s discretion.

#### Mirabel's Breath of Dusk
*3rd-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** S
**Duration:** Permanent

You murmur a delicate glamour into the mind of a sleeping creature, softening recollection and loosening the hold of recent memory.

You must touch a creature that is unconscious or naturally sleeping. The target must make a Wisdom saving throw.

• Failure:
You suppress up to 30 minutes of the creature’s memories from the past 24 hours. You choose the specific span of time affected. The creature cannot recall these events for the spell’s duration.

• Success:
The spell has no effect.

The spell has no effect on creatures that are awake, immune to charm effects, or do not sleep.

When the spell ends, the memories return indistinctly and with blurred emotional clarity at the GM’s discretion.

If this spell successfully affects the same creature more than once within 7 days, the target’s cognition destabilizes. The creature must succeed on a DC 15 Wisdom saving throw or suffer:

– Disadvantage on Intelligence ability checks for 24 hours
– One level of exhaustion

On a success, the creature resists these destabilizing effects.

#### Misthreaded Passage
*3rd-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 hours

You disturb the coherence of a creature’s presence within the Loom, causing its trail to fragment into convincing but false continuities.

Choose one creature within range. For the duration, effects that attempt to track, locate, identify, or divine the target’s position or identity yield unreliable results.
	•	Divination magic, scrying, omen-reading, supernatural tracking, and comparable abilities perceive false leads, displaced echoes, or contradictory impressions rather than the true thread.
	•	Ability checks made to track or locate the target are made with disadvantage.
	•	A creature actively tracking the target when this spell is cast must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw or lose the trail, accepting a false conclusion or dead end.

This spell does not make the target invisible, inaudible, or hidden from mundane perception. It interferes only with informational, perceptual, and divinatory attempts to establish continuity.

When cast using a higher-level spell slot, you may target one additional creature for each slot level above 3rd, provided all targets are within range at the time of casting. Their passages blur together, producing overlapping and mutually inconsistent traces.

#### Mobster’s Favor
*3rd-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 120.0 feet
**Components:** None
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You call in a debt from the shadow economy of the city, invoking an unspoken pact older than law. A hardened enforcer manifests nearby, broad-shouldered and scarred, wearing a long coat heavy with stitched sigils of obligation. Gold rings mark their fingers. Their eyes weigh you like currency.

They say nothing at first. Then, after a pause: “You paid. So I’m here.”

The enforcer is a capable but self-interested combatant. They fight efficiently, without heroics, and without mercy. Their loyalty is purely transactional, bound by coin and the invisible ledgers of the city’s underworld.

The Gilded Enforcer
	•	Acts once in combat, immediately after your turn
	•	Makes melee spell attacks, dealing 1d6 + your Charisma modifier bludgeoning damage
	•	Prioritizes protecting you or nearby allies, but will not sacrifice themselves
	•	If reduced to half their hit points, they begin fighting defensively

Coinbound Quirks
	1.	Refers to the caster as “credit”, “asset”, or “investment”
	2.	Casually references unnamed debts, favors, or broken oaths
	3.	Will threaten, maim, or intimidate enemies without hesitation
	4.	Shows no interest in ideology, morality, or long-term plans
	5.	Vanishes once the spell ends, leaving behind the faint impression that something is still owed

Additional Effects
	•	The enforcer demands payment in gold or valuables upon manifestation
	•	If unpaid or shorted, the GM may introduce future complications tied to reputation, lost favors, or shadow reprisals
	•	When the spell ends, the enforcer disappears silently, as if folded back into the city itself, leaving behind a sense of unresolved obligation

This is not a summoning.
It is a transaction.

#### Muttering Solstice of Indignation
*3rd-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You whisper defiant syllables into the Weave, anchoring a sphere of uncooperative momentum into the world. Within the zone, tension hangs in the air—every movement feels optional, replaceable, or rebellious.

While within the sphere, each creature may choose at the start of their turn:
- Forego their movement speed for the turn to gain one of the following effects until the start of their next turn:
- +1 bonus to AC
- One additional weapon attack as part of the Attack action
- Advantage on the next saving throw they make

These choices must be made verbally—even whispered—causing faint echoes to ripple in the air.

#### Paradox Consecration
*3rd-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 5 roundss

You designate an area as both sanctified and desecrated for 5 rounds. It counts as both types of terrain simultaneously.

While active:- All Sacred Footing and Aura of Sanctity benefits for both Holy and Unholy terrain are active.- Enemies within the area must make a Wisdom saving throw or suffer from Paranoia (disadvantage on Insight, Investigation, and saving throws against fear effects).- You may cast spells that require either Holy or Unholy terrain as though the condition is met.

This creates strange divine interference, and at the start of your turn while concentrating on it, roll a d6:- 1–2: Radiant burst (each creature takes 1d6 radiant)- 3–4: Shadow pulse (each creature heals 1 HP if undead)- 5–6: No extra effect

#### Phantom Paper Trail
*3rd-level Illusion*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You do not just alter a document—you bend reality itself to accept the forgery as true for a short period of time.

- When you modify a ledger, contract, record, or file, the spell imprints its existence into the fabric of the world, making it temporarily irrefutable.
- For the next 10 minutes, any creature reading or interacting with the altered document will believe it is correct, unless they succeed on a DC 18 Intelligence (Investigation) check.
- Even memories are briefly affected—a guard whose records have been modified will recall seeing you enter.
- After 10 minutes, the false record vanishes, and reality attempts to correct itself, leaving behind only confusion and a lingering sense that something wasn’t quite right.

#### Power Surge
*3rd-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

The target’s body crackles with latent electrical energy, empowering their strikes. For the duration of the spell, the target deals 1d8 additional lightning damage with weapon attacks and unarmed strikes.

Furthermore, if the target takes lightning damage while this spell is active, they absorb the energy, regaining hit points equal to half the damage taken.

#### Proclamation of Borrowed Voice
*3rd-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You seize a creature’s voice and turn it into a vessel for imposed declaration. Choose one creature within range. The target must make a Charisma saving throw. On a failure, it is compelled to immediately speak a declarative statement of your choosing, delivered with formal conviction as though the words were required of them by duty or oath.

While speaking, the creature rationalizes the proclamation as necessary and justified, believing the act to be appropriate rather than coerced. If the statement is factually untrue, the creature may attempt a Wisdom saving throw at the end of each of its turns to break free of the compulsion.

If you bear visible symbols of authority, ritual office, or recognized legitimacy, the target has disadvantage on its initial saving throw, as the borrowed voice yields more readily to perceived mandate.

#### Pulse Reaver
*3rd-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** S
**Duration:** 1 rounds

You place your hand near the target’s throat, heart, or the air above their skin—never touching, yet always too close. With a whispered invocation, you invite the attention of something that drinks the breath between pulses.- The target loses 2 hit points per round for the duration.- The caster gains 1 hit point per round (up to their maximum).- If the target is reduced to 0 hit points this way, they do not fall unconscious immediately.- For 1 round, they remain aware but paralyzed, their vision darkening as they feel a cold, unseen presence leaning in, whispering promises only they can hear.- At the start of their next turn, they fall unconscious unless stabilized by magical means.

#### Pyric Rend
*3rd-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 120.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You tear open a wound in the flow of pyric force, releasing a violent burst of living heat. The rupture blooms outward in a sudden flare, scorching flesh and stone alike.

Those within the blast feel fire without flame, a burning that strikes faster than pain can form. Surfaces blacken, warp, or crack as the heat surges through them, leaving the area scorched and humming with fading warmth.

#### Regal Cipher of Binding
*3rd-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You inscribe a layered seal of authority upon an object, threshold, or designated space, warding it against unauthorized passage. The binding resists mundane interference, refuses forced entry, and denies traversal through the Veil unless the intruder overcomes the seal’s authority.

Attempts to bypass the cipher through strength, skill, or teleportation are met with resistance, requiring significant exertion or force of will. If the seal is placed upon a creature, it constrains movement and escape, holding the subject within sanctioned bounds until the binding is broken or dispelled.

The protection feels less like armor and more like the world itself yielding slightly around the bearer.

#### Regal Measure of Endurance
*3rd-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action

**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You extend a measured boon of sanctioned vitality to up to four creatures within range. Each gains temporary resilience equal to 3d8 plus your spellcasting modifier and a +1 bonus to Constitution saving throws.

The endurance is artificial and exacting. When the effect ends, each creature must either rest for an hour or suffer one level of exhaustion as the borrowed stability withdraws and the body reckons with the imposed strain.

#### Release of Burdened Past
*3rd-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You lift the emotional weight from a single cognitive affliction affecting a willing creature. Choose one of the following conditions currently affecting the target: Paranoid, Aroused, Frightened, Stunned, Compelled, or Charmed.

That condition immediately ends. The creature retains memory of the events that caused the condition, but the emotional and psychological burden associated with it is removed, allowing them to act without the influence of that trauma.

This spell does not remove physical conditions or non-cognitive effects.

#### Revulsion
*3rd-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 rounds

A sensory overload in the target’s pleasure- response cortex creates an overwhelming repulsion toward all forms of intimacy.
 
- The target must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw or become physically nauseated at the thought of intimacy.
- Disadvantage on Charisma- based rolls involving seduction, persuasion, or charm effects.
 
 The reverse of this spell, "Pleasure Numbness," removes all sexual or emotional distress responses for 24 hours, making the target indifferent to physical stimuli.

#### Reweave the Mind
*3rd-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You send a steadying pulse through the Weft of Thought, re-threading frayed cognition and severing imposed patterns of fear, command, and suppression. The target’s mind exhales, slipping free from bindings it did not consent to hold.

When you touch a willing creature, the following effects occur:
	•	Ends effects that impose Charm, Fear, or externally forced obedience and suppression, provided they originate from enchantment, imposed will, or cognitive interference.
	•	Immediately ends mental domination, compliance enchantments, or artificial thought-locks imposed by authority, ritual, or anomaly.
	•	If the creature is unconscious due to mental overload, psychic pressure, or forced suppression, it immediately regains consciousness.

This spell does not remove curses tied to identity, oaths freely accepted, or enchantments sustained by active concentration. It does not erase memory. It restores agency.

#### Ricochet
*3rd-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You release a single guided strike that refuses to end with its first impact. Make a ranged weapon attack against a creature within your weapon’s normal range. On a hit, the strike deals its normal damage, then rebounds with unnatural precision.

After the initial hit, the strike leaps to up to two additional creatures of your choice, each within 15 feet of the last creature struck. Each additional target requires a separate ranged weapon attack roll. On a hit, an additional target takes half the damage dealt by the initial attack. The strike cannot leap to the same creature more than once.

You conjure a sealed sanctum of focused labor in an unoccupied space within range. The space manifests as a quiet, furnished chamber containing desks, shelves, and arcane instruments suited to writing, calculation, and record-keeping.

The sanctum is soundproof and isolated from outside distraction. While within it, creatures may work, study, organize, or perform administrative or scholarly tasks without interruption. The sanctum lasts for the duration or until you dismiss it as an action, at which point it vanishes without leaving trace.

#### Shelter of the Bleeding Veil
*3rd-level Conjuration*

**Components:** V, S

The shelter offers safety and rest, sealed from outside intrusion. Yet the Veil is imperfectly bound. Subtle anomalies sometimes emerge within the space, leaving signs that something else briefly shared the refuge. When the shelter dissolves, faint impressions linger, as if the Veil remembers being disturbed.

#### Silken Motion
*3rd-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 1.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You coat a surface or willing creature with a living unction that defies ordinary friction, spreading in a smooth, self-renewing sheen guided by the Weft rather than gravity. The substance is clean, safe, and responsive, adjusting itself to motion rather than resisting it.

If cast upon a surface, creatures moving across it must make a Dexterity saving throw or lose their footing as the ground flows subtly against their balance. If cast upon a willing creature, the unction enhances motion and flexibility for the duration, allowing seamless, fluid movement without strain.

Creatures affected by enchantments find the unction especially treacherous. Any Dexterity saving throw they make to cross or interact with the treated area is made with disadvantage, as divided will and yielding motion conspire against control.

#### Snare of Arrested Thought
*3rd-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You entangle the target’s mind in a knot of Still Time, halting the flow of cognition mid-process. The target must make an Intelligence saving throw. On a failure, their thoughts lock in place. They cannot take actions, bonus actions, or reactions, and they automatically fail Intelligence-based checks and saving throws for the duration.

At the end of each of its turns, the creature may repeat the saving throw. On a success, the knot loosens, thought resumes, and the effect ends.

#### Summon the Pendulum of Ruin
*3rd-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 120.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You conjure a semi-sentient spectral engine of war that manifests as a massive, floating sling bound to unseen forces. Suspended in the air by arcane tension, it slowly swings back and forth, gathering momentum like a pendulum wound with memory and wrath. At its center hangs a heavy astral cradle, repeatedly loaded with conjured stones of condensed force.

The Pendulum of Ruin acts on your initiative, immediately after your turn. Each round, it selects a hostile creature within range and releases a thunderous cast, hurling its projectile with inevitability rather than aim. Its attacks are magical for the purpose of overcoming resistance.

The sling may be mentally guided with a bonus action, adjusting its focus or letting it act according to its own brutal instinct, always favoring the nearest hostile presence. The air around it thrums with lethal anticipation, and standing too close invites lingering harm from its unstable energies.

Though it has no wielder, the pendulum swings as if pulled by unseen ambition, each release echoing like a judgment cast across the battlefield.
Additional Rules:
- The artillery is immune to psychic damage and charm effects.
- It vanishes if reduced to 0 HP or if your concentration ends.
- Enemies within 5 feet of the artillery at the end of their turn take 1d6 radiation damage from exposure to its lingering aura.
- You may mentally command it using a bonus action, or let it act independently according to its targeting protocol (attacking the nearest hostile creature).

#### Summons of the Implacable Scriptor
*3rd-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You call forth an unseen arbiter of order, a faceless force that demands the world be made tidy, complete, and properly recorded.

An invisible scriptor-spirit manifests within a room or similarly bounded space. Though unseen, its presence is undeniable: parchment rustles, quills scratch, and judgmental murmurs echo from nowhere.

While the scriptor presides:
	•	No creature may willingly leave the area until all demanded records are completed in exacting multiplicity.
	•	Any documents present must be copied in triplicate, a process that consumes time and patience.
	•	If no records exist, the spirit conjures an exhausting stack of forms.

If cast in an open or outdoor space, the scriptor first translates all creatures into a barren clerical demesne, a small featureless chamber filled with desks, parchment, and stiff chairs. None may leave until the task is complete or the spell ends.

Failure to comply provokes consequences known only to the spirit, which may include ominous warnings, inscrutable marks upon fate, or references to a record that cannot be erased.
