#### The Jester's Wild Gambit
*3rd-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

Chaos hangs in the air, swirling with possibilities. You embrace the whimsy of chance, drawing power from fate’s unpredictable nature.

When you cast The Jester’s Wild Gambit, you surrender yourself to fate’s hands. Every time you make an attack roll or ability check, you may roll twice, taking the higher result. On a natural 20, the effect is magnified—doubling the result of your roll. But on a natural 1, something chaotic occurs. The DM may choose an unpredictable effect, such as disadvantage on your next roll, an unintended event that causes a distraction, or a minor but inconvenient consequence.

**Components:** V, S

If the target is a creature, it must make a Wisdom saving throw or be compelled to speak truthfully for the duration, unable to withhold or disguise what the unsealed threads reveal. The whispers fade when the spell ends, but what was heard cannot be forgotten.

#### Urge Unerring
*3rd-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You align your body, mind, and bladder with an invisible thread of inevitability. For the duration, cosmic forces ensure your next strike is absurdly accurate—but only under strangely specific conditions.

Until the spell ends, your next attack roll automatically hits a target of your choice if any of the following are true at the time of the attack:
- You are actively urinating.
- You are within 5 feet of someone who is.
- You are standing inside a bathroom, restroom, washroom, or similarly designated facility—regardless of plumbing status.

If none of these conditions are true, you must spend an action miming the act of relieving yourself (DMs are encouraged to enforce social consequences) to activate the effect. Once the effect is used, the spell ends

#### Utallash's Pursuit of Ceramic
*3rd-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 bonus action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** None
**Duration:** Permanent

You invoke a forbidden remnant of ancient magic, drawing from the chilling legacy known as Utallash’s Pursuit of Ceramic. Choose one creature within range; 
it must make a Charisma saving throw. On a failed save, the target suffers the following effects:
- The target takes 4d8 force damage as their identity begins to fracture, leaving a hollow, ceramic
- like resonance within their being.- They become a “Husk”: For the next hour, the target struggles to remember their own name, imposing disadvantage on all Charisma- based checks and saving throws.

Marked by the Void (Caster’s Consequences):
Every time you cast this spell, you become subtly marked by the magic. The mark grows stronger with repeated uses. You experience minor, unsettling phenomena:
- Your reflection occasionally blinks or moves independently.
- Your shadow periodically misaligns or lags behind your physical form.

After you cast this spell 3 or more times, you gain disadvantage on Charisma saving throws until you complete a long rest, as the magic slowly erodes your own identity.

These effects are cumulative but subtle enough to be hidden from casual observers—though those familiar with the Void’s whispers will recognize your affliction immediately.

Removing the Mark:
A Greater Restoration or similarly potent cleansing magic removes all accumulated marks from you, resetting the count.

#### Veil-Slip of Unrecorded Passage
*3rd-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 reaction
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You momentarily slip your thread beneath the Veil of recognition, causing the Loom to lose sight of your movement. For the duration, divination magic, scrying effects, and tracking rites cannot perceive you.

If you were already being observed or followed, the last recorded position of your thread remains fixed, as though you never moved beyond that point. Any attempt to reestablish your trail through magical tracking fails unless the caster succeeds on an Intelligence saving throw against your spell save DC, as the Erudits’ registries refuse to update your position.

#### Veil-Tread of Uncertain Thread
*3rd-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You loosen your thread from the Loom and allow it to drift unpredictably across the Veil. At the start of each of your turns, roll a d6 as the Veil resettles around you:
	•	On a 1–2, the Veil thickens defensively, granting you resistance to all damage.
	•	On a 3–4, your thread snaps sideways through the Veil, teleporting you 30 feet in a random direction.
	•	On a 5–6, the Veil obscures your presence entirely, rendering you invisible until the start of your next turn.

Each shift feels uncontrolled, as though the Veil itself is deciding how best to accommodate your unstable presence.

#### Veil-Walk of the Unnoticed Thread
*3rd-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You partially displace your body across the Veil, causing your presence to blur between states of recognition. For the duration, you move through crowds without drawing notice unless actively sought, slipping past attention as though your thread refuses to catch the eye.

You may pass through fragile barriers such as glass, light fencing, or unreinforced doors, and you leave no trace upon pressure-sensitive wards, ritual scans, or motion-detecting enchantments. To the world, you are not invisible, but unregistered, and therefore unseen.

#### Veiled Thread Dispatch
*3rd-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

By touching a prepared focus, you weave a brief message of up to twenty-five words directly into the Loom and guide it along hidden telepathic channels toward a specific recipient. The message arrives instantly as a clear thought in the recipient’s mind, spoken in your mental voice.

The transmission leaves no physical trace, no record within Erudit registries, and no lingering signature once delivered. If the recipient is fully severed from telepathic or planar connectivity, the dispatch fails harmlessly, the thread dissolving before it can reach its destination.

#### Veins of the Forgotten
*3rd-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You allow your veins to forget their purpose, turning your circulatory system into something liquid, shifting, and unknowable.
 

- For the duration of the spell, your blood is no longer entirely inside you—it slithers beneath your skin, forming moving patterns, and drips onto the floor in places you haven't stepped.
- You gain the following benefits and consequences:
- Your body is semi- fluid, allowing you to squeeze through gaps no wider than 1 inch.
- You are immune to poison and diseases, as your blood is no longer organic.
- You take half damage from slashing attacks, but piercing attacks deal double damage as your body cannot hold shape properly.
- Each time you cast a spell, your blood reacts violently, causing you to lose 1d6 HP per spell level.
- If you reach 0 HP while this spell is active, you do not die—instead, your blood scatters across the room, and your body must be reassembled manually.
 

 Anomaly Effect:
- If used too frequently, your blood refuses to return to your body, forming an independent entity that watches you, waiting for an opportunity to replace you.

#### Velvet Undress
*3rd-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 10.0 feet
**Components:** S
**Duration:** Special

With a deliberate and hypnotic performance, you begin a sensual dance designed to captivate a single creature of your choice within range. As part of the performance, you must remove one article of clothing per round. Each round the dance continues:
- The target must make a Wisdom saving throw, suffering a 
– 1 penalty for each round you’ve maintained the dance.
- On a failed save, the target becomes Charmed and fully fixated on your every movement, unable to willingly look away or take hostile actions against you for the duration.
- If the target is already Charmed by you when this spell is cast, the duration extends by 1 additional minute.

The spell ends early if the caster is interrupted, breaks concentration, or voluntarily stops dancing.

#### Weftbound Renewal
*3rd-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You bind up to three creatures to a shared pattern of restoration within the Tesserac Weft. At the start of each of their turns, each bound creature regains 1d8 hit points as vitality is redistributed through the weave.

If any affected creature is missing a limb, the Weft initiates slow regrowth. Over the course of 1d4 days, the lost limb reforms gradually, knitting itself back into place as the pattern completes. The process is steady and unmistakably unnatural, as though the body is remembering a shape it was never meant to forget.

#### Writ of Arrested Will
*3rd-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You invoke a binding writ drawn from the unseen authority of higher dominion, fixing a creature in a state of sanctioned inaction. The target must make a Charisma saving throw. On a failure, an overwhelming pressure settles upon them, as though reality itself has denied their right to act. While affected, the creature cannot move, attack, or take actions.

At the end of each of its turns, the creature may attempt a Wisdom saving throw, straining to assert its own intent against the writ’s authority. On a success, the effect ends.

If the creature attempts to force movement or action through sheer physical effort, it must make a Strength saving throw against your spell save DC. On a failure, an unseen barrier repels them 5 feet, accompanied by a fleeting manifestation of sigils that signify denial and refusal.

When cast at higher levels, the writ expands its reach, binding multiple creatures under the same arrest of will.

#### Aether Surge
*4th-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You release a violent surge of warped aetheric resonance, filling the area with shrieking vibrations that shatter concentration and bodily control.

The surge erupts in a 10-foot-radius sphere centered on a point within range. Each creature in the area must make a Constitution saving throw.

• Failure: The creature takes 5d8 thunder damage and is Stunned until the start of its next turn.
• Success: The creature takes half damage and suffers no additional effect.

Unattended objects composed primarily of glass, crystal, or ceramic within the sphere may fracture or shatter at the GM’s discretion. This effect typically damages fragile items such as vessels, panes, and ornaments, but does not automatically destroy larger structures or reinforced objects.

The surge manifests as overwhelming vibrational force rather than audible sound, a disorienting pressure that rattles both matter and mind.

#### Architect’s Collapse
*4th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 10 minutess
**Range:** 10.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Permanent

You touch a crafted object or man-made structure and command it to forget its shape. The target must be a nonmagical, unattended object or structure composed of mundane materials such as wood, stone, or metal.

If the target is a Small or smaller object, it immediately separates into its constituent components. Wood, stone, and metal divide cleanly along functional boundaries: a blade into hilt and edge, a lock into springs and casing, a shield into fittings and plates.

If the target is a Large or larger structure, you affect a 10-foot cube of the structure’s material at the point of contact. That portion collapses into beams, fastenings, panels, and raw elements. The collapse is controlled and nonviolent, producing no damage beyond what the loss of support naturally causes.

Creatures occupying or supported by the affected area must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw or fall prone and be displaced to the nearest unoccupied space outside the collapsed components.

The separated materials remain intact and retain the memory of their former arrangement:

• The components may be reassembled into their original form if reconstruction is completed within 48 hours.
• Reassembly requires appropriate tools and a successful Intelligence (relevant tool) check, DC determined by complexity.
• No material loss occurs during proper restoration.

If a creature attempts to rebuild the object or structure incorrectly, the components resist the flawed design:

• The reconstruction automatically fails.
• The creature must succeed on a Strength check or the unstable components shift, wasting the effort.
• Repeated attempts continue to fail unless the original configuration is followed.

Magical objects, creatures, and structures animated by magic are unaffected.

#### Blasphemer’s Undoing
*4th-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 reaction
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

Sanctified Terrain retains a residual antipathy toward creatures marked by necrotic influence.

When a creature that has dealt necrotic damage within the past 24 hours enters Sanctified Terrain, you may invoke the consecrated field as a reaction. The terrain violently rejects the intrusion.

The creature must make a Constitution saving throw.

• Failure: The creature takes 6d6 fire damage as sanctified energies scour its presence.
• Failure by 5 or more: The creature is Incapacitated until the end of its next turn, its body overwhelmed by the force of the rejection.
• Success: The creature takes half damage and suffers no additional effect.

This effect only triggers upon entry into the terrain. A creature that remains within the area is not subjected to repeated saving throws unless it exits and re-enters.

Creatures immune to fire damage are still subject to the incapacitation effect.

#### Canticle of the Built World
*4th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 minutes
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 hours

Canticle of the Built World — Mechanics-Clarified Version

You lay your hand upon stone, concrete, or reinforced architecture, attuning your awareness to the slow, burdened presence of the structure.

For the duration, while you remain in contact with the same surface, you gain a muted perception of disturbances within the structure out to 60 feet. You sense movement, impacts, and significant shifts in weight or stress, though not precise identities or locations.

This awareness allows you to discern:

• Whether creatures are moving within range
• The general size or intensity of recent disturbances
• Areas of unusual strain or structural damage

The communion also permits limited inquiry. You may mentally pose simple questions regarding the structure’s recent experiences, such as:

• What type of force last stressed or damaged it
• Whether living creatures currently occupy it
• Whether significant motion recently occurred within

The structure’s responses manifest as impressions rather than language, and may be vague or incomplete at the DM’s discretion.

⸻

Once before the spell ends, you may exert direct influence over a 10-foot cube of the structure within range:

• Mend: Restore up to 30 hit points to the targeted section.
• Fracture: Deal 6d6 force damage to the targeted section.

Damage caused by this effect ignores resistance to nonmagical damage if the structure is nonmagical.

This command cannot collapse a structure outright unless the affected section’s destruction would logically cause such a failure.

⸻

The spell ends early if:

• You break physical contact with the structure
• The contacted surface is destroyed
• You cast this spell again

#### Deferral to Higher Writ
*4th-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 hours

You impose a compulsion of misplaced authority upon a humanoid within range. The target must make a Wisdom saving throw.

• Failure: The creature becomes convinced that the matter before it lies beyond its standing. For the duration, it gains the Paranoid condition and refuses to engage with the current conflict or task, insisting the situation requires intervention from a superior authority.

While affected:

• The creature is unwilling to take hostile actions related to the triggering circumstance.
• In combat, the creature takes the Dodge action on its turns unless it has been directly attacked since the end of its previous turn.
• The creature may still move, speak, and take non-hostile actions, typically expressing agitation, doubt, or procedural fixation.

The creature may repeat the Wisdom saving throw at the end of each hour, ending the effect on a success. The creature also repeats the saving throw immediately if confronted by an entity it genuinely recognizes as possessing legitimate higher authority.

• Success: The creature resists the compulsion but has disadvantage on its next ability check or attack roll before the end of its next turn.

#### Dissonant Gestation
*4th-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 hours
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Permanent

You implore the dark corners of the far realms to place an unseen burden within a creature’s body—not a pregnancy, but an unnatural gestation, a thing that grows, waits, and feeds.
 
The target must make a Constitution saving throw.

• Failure: The creature becomes Infected. An unseen gestation begins within its body, producing progressive and deeply unsettling symptoms over time.
• Success: The creature resists the intrusion and is unaffected.

⸻

Progression of the Infection

At the end of each week, roll a d6 to determine the dominant manifestation of the corruption. The effects are intentionally disturbing and primarily narrative in nature, though the GM may assign mechanical consequences consistent with the transformation.

The precise presentation and severity of symptoms are determined by the GM.

⸻

Termination of the Gestation

If the infection persists for three months, the corruption reaches culmination. The resulting transformation, emergence, or catastrophic failure is entirely determined by the GM and may be lethal.

The gestation may be ended prematurely by:

• Significant surgical intervention
• Effects that cure curses or magical diseases (GM discretion)
• More powerful magic capable of removing profound bodily corruption
d6
Manifestation
1
Bone Nesting – Skeletal structures distort, producing pain, rigidity, or unnatural growth.
2
Chitinous Sheathing – Flesh hardens in places, forming shell-like patches beneath the skin.
3
Hollowing – The creature experiences the sensation of internal absence or shifting voids.
4
Corrupted Blood – Circulatory behavior becomes erratic, accompanied by visible or sensory anomalies.
5
Divided Thought – The creature perceives intrusive impulses, alien instincts, or internal voices.
6
Aberrant Bloom – Temporary protrusions, distortions, or impossible physiological irregularities emerge.

#### Dyrnar’s Tormentous Wail
*4th-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You release a scream that does not originate from your body, but from a depth of existence older than breath. The wail floods the minds of those before you with echoes of nameless dread.

Each creature in a 30-foot cone must make a Wisdom saving throw.

• Failure: The creature is Frightened of you for 1 minute.
• Failure by 5 or more: The creature is Frightened and takes 5d6 psychic damage.

A Frightened creature may repeat the saving throw at the end of each of its turns, ending the effect on a success.

#### Fold Space
*4th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 10 minutess
**Range:** 100.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 hours

You bend spatial continuity along existing architectural boundaries, stitching together two points of passage.

Choose two visible thresholds within 100 feet of you.

A threshold is defined as:

• A doorway
• An archway
• A tunnel entrance
• A window large enough for a creature
• Any comparable opening that connects two distinct spaces

Each threshold must be unoccupied and capable of physically admitting a creature of the intended size.

For the duration, the thresholds become spatially linked:

• A creature passing through one immediately exits through the other
• The fold functions bidirectionally
• Traversal requires movement as normal
• The linked thresholds remain fixed in space

The fold manifests as a faint distortion lining each opening. A creature inspecting a threshold may attempt an Intelligence (Arcana) check against your spell save DC to recognize the effect.

The spell ends immediately if either threshold is:

• Destroyed
• Fully blocked
• Subject to an effect that suppresses conjuration magic

When the spell ends, the connection collapses silently.

#### Giocrin's Hunt
*4th-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 10.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 hours

You unleash a pulse of predatory awareness, exposing the subtle disturbances creatures impress upon the world simply by existing within it.

Choose a point you can see within range. Creatures of your choice within a 30-foot-radius sphere must make a Wisdom saving throw.

⸻

Failure

For the duration, you perceive the creature’s presence as a shifting distortion in space:

• The creature gains no benefit from invisibility against you
• The creature gains no benefit from being hidden from you
• You have advantage on Wisdom (Perception) and Wisdom (Survival) checks made to detect or track it

⸻

Success

The creature resists the intrusive awareness.

However, until the end of the spell’s duration:

• The creature leaves behind a faint perceptual trace visible only to you
• You have advantage on Wisdom (Survival) checks made to track it
• This trace does not reveal precise location, only direction and movement

| Effect | Description |
|---------------- |------------- |
| Marked | The creature emits a visible, flickering aura only you can see. You have advantage on attack rolls, ability checks to track, locate, or affect them. |
| Haunted | The creature is Under Surveillance: has disadvantage on Stealth checks and cannot benefit from invisibility. |
| Overloaded | If the creature is already being observed by magical or technological surveillance, it takes 4d6 psychic damage from conflicting signals. |

#### Imperatum Reassertion of the Veil
*4th-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You pronounce a sovereign correction, compelling unstable phenomena to yield before sanctioned reality.

Choose a point you can see within range. A 20-foot-radius sphere centered on that point is subjected to Veil reassertion.

Within the sphere, the following effects apply for the duration:

• Magical anomalies, conjured effects, and summoned manifestations of 4th level or lower are immediately suppressed
• Ongoing spell effects of 4th level or lower are suppressed while within the area
• Creatures sustained by magic of 4th level or lower must succeed on a Charisma saving throw or be banished until the start of your next turn

Effects created by magic of 5th level or higher are not dispelled but are visibly strained. Affected creatures have disadvantage on the first saving throw they make within the area.

Veil distortions recoil under the pressure of the decree, causing illusory or extradimensional effects to flicker and destabilize at the DM’s discretion.

Duration: Concentration, up to 1 minute.

#### Imperial Recall Rite
*4th-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You invoke sovereign claim over a recently departed soul, compelling its thread to reverse course and reoccupy its abandoned form.

Choose one creature that has died within the last minute whose body remains largely intact and within range.

The soul is marked for recall. After 1d6 rounds, the creature returns to life at a space occupied by its body or the nearest unoccupied space.

Upon return:

• The creature regains hit points equal to half its hit point maximum
• The creature is Prone
• Until the end of its next turn, the creature cannot take reactions

If the creature’s soul is unwilling, or if the body is destroyed, missing vital components, or under the effect of magic that prevents resurrection, the spell fails.

A creature restored by this rite bears faint, imperceptible sigils of recall visible only to effects that detect necromancy or divine magic.

This spell cannot restore creatures that died of old age, nor those whose souls have been claimed or bound by another effect.

#### Lance of Dreadmere Scour
*4th-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You release a concentrated lance of corrupted flame that tears through creatures in a straight line, leaving a lingering wound in space.

Choose a line 60 feet long and 5 feet wide originating from a point you can see within range. Each creature in the line must make a Dexterity saving throw.

• Failure: The creature takes 6d8 fire damage.
• Success: The creature takes half damage.

The line becomes a Dreadmere Scar for the duration while you maintain concentration. The scar is visible as a faint, sickened distortion etched along the beam’s path.

While the scar persists:

• A creature that starts its turn within 10 feet of the scar takes 1d4 necrotic damage.
• Once a creature regains hit points, it becomes temporarily resistant to this lingering damage until it leaves the area.
• A creature that exits and later re-enters the affected radius is harmed normally.

The scar is an environmental effect, not a creature or object, and cannot be attacked. When concentration ends, the distortion fades harmlessly.

The lance does not simply burn. It stains the space it crosses with residual dread.

#### Nonlinear Travel
*4th-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 hours

You exist in two places simultaneously, shifting between locations each round. You can take actions from either location, but your form is flickering and unpredictable. Any attempt to track, capture, or observe you results in incomplete or contradictory reports.

#### Pulse of Still-Time Displacement
*4th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self (30.0-foot sphere)
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You release a surge of distorted Still Time that fractures the instant of impact. Creatures caught in the area suffer 6d10 psychic damage as their perception and motion fall out of alignment. Each creature must make a Constitution saving throw. On a failure, its thread slips slightly out of phase with the present moment, becoming Displaced and suffering disadvantage on attack rolls and Dexterity saving throws until the end of its next turn.

When invoked at higher power, the Still Time distortion deepens, increasing the damage as the moment is forced further out of sync.

#### Redlight in a Pocket
*4th-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 5 hourss

You conjure a sealed, unearthly chamber, where indulgence flows like silk and no outside force may intrude.

- The 15- foot- diameter space is soundproof, protected from weather, and forbiddingly private.
- The caster can shape the interior at will, conjuring cushions, incense, and music that hums from the walls themselves.
- Those who rest inside awaken feeling like time itself curled around them, leaving them untouched.

#### Refraction of Self
*4th-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 bonus action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

Your form fractures slightly from this world, your outline flickering and bending at unnatural angles. When injured, reality itself offers you an escape—but not always a reliable one.

While this spell is active, each time you take damage, you may immediately teleport up to 20 feet to an unoccupied space you can see. This reaction does not cost an action or reaction.

You must have line of sight to teleport intentionally. If no valid space exists, the teleportation fails.

While this spell is active, you cast no reflection on reflective surfaces

#### Refusal Writ of the Crown
*4th-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 reaction
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

When an external force attempts to bind your will, you invoke a writ of refusal anchored in Regal authority. You immediately reroll the saving throw against any effect that would impose charm, compulsion, or enforced obedience.

On a successful save, all such effects upon you end instantly, and you become immune to further attempts of that nature for 1 minute. If the source of the coercion is within 30 feet, the backlash tears through their mind, dealing 4d6 psychic damage as the Veins of Lament echo their overreach.

This writ stands in defiance of magical contracts, psychic domination, and any force that claims the right to command without rightful standing.

#### Regal Seal of Arrested Passage
*4th-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You inscribe a concealed seal of Regal authority into the environment, binding the surrounding space beneath sanctioned stillness. The seal is invisible to ordinary senses and can only be perceived through specialized divination or Erudit scrutiny.

When a creature first enters the warded area, it must make a Wisdom saving throw. On a failure, its thread is halted and diverted into a suspended state of recognition, aware of its surroundings but unable to move, act, or communicate. The creature remains contained until presented with a valid sigil of release, bound at the time of casting to you or a designated bearer.

Creatures that succeed on the saving throw pass through unhindered, though the seal remains dormant until triggered. Once activated, the seal cannot detain additional creatures.

Repeated use of such seals within the same region risks attracting higher Regal scrutiny, which may cause the seal to misapply its authority, detaining an unintended subject or manifesting a bureaucratic anomaly of Still Time.

#### Rejection of False Authority
*4th-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 reaction
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You assert the primacy of your own will against imposed dominion. When an external force attempts to bind, command, or observe you, this spell fractures the authority behind it.

Lesser bindings unravel instantly, their claims rendered void. Stronger compulsions find no easy hold, as your resolve hardens against them, granting you heightened resistance to all attempts to dominate or surveil your actions for a short time.

#### Residual Presence
*4th-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 hours

You reach beyond the veil and call forth a flickering echo of a recently deceased creature. Instead of communicating directly, you witness fractured memories or emotional imprints they left behind.

When cast on a space where a humanoid died within the last 7 days, choose one of the following effects:

- Residual Vision. You and up to 5 willing creatures see a ghostly reenactment of the creature’s final moments, projected like a spectral recording. The scene is silent and incomplete, but may reveal useful visual details such as a killer's face, a hidden object, or a symbol drawn in blood.
 
- Lingering Instinct. You gain a skill or tool proficiency the deceased possessed (your choice, if known) for 10 minutes. You also gain advantage on Intelligence checks related to the creature's past profession or knowledge.

- Emotional Imprint. The space is saturated with the creature's strongest emotion at the time of death. For 10 minutes, anyone entering the space must succeed on a DC 13 Charisma saving throw or experience that emotion intensely (e.g., rage, fear, sorrow), which may affect social interactions, Insight, or Intimidation checks.

The echo fades once the chosen effect ends, or if dismissed early.

#### Restoration of Borrowed Breath
*4th-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You draw lingering strain out of the target’s body and return it to the Weft, allowing the creature to stand renewed. The spell removes one level of exhaustion from the target, or two levels if cast at greater power.

If the target is unconscious or severely overworked, the sudden restoration also restores 4d8 hit points as breath, strength, and will are forcibly returned. The relief is immediate but not gentle, as vitality reclaimed too quickly always leaves a faint echo of strain behind.

#### Rite of Flesh Alignment
*4th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You realign the living patterns of up to six creatures, restoring harmony between form, function, and vitality. Each target regains 5d8 hit points and ends one condition affecting it: blinded, deafened, paralyzed, or poisoned. When used on constructs or augmented beings, the rite also resolves internal malfunctions as their systems are forced back into functional coherence.

#### Rotating Opus of Indignation
*4th-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 reaction
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** S
**Duration:** 1 rounds

As your mind cracks under pressure, you unleash an anomalous pulse of rhythm and defiance—a stuttering cosmic melody that replays itself, over and over, across the battlefield. The air pulses in time with an unseen waltz. Reality blinks.

When you fail a saving throw, you may cast this spell to release a psychic backlash in a 20- foot radius centered on a point you choose within range.

Each creature in the area must make a Charisma saving throw. On a failure, they take 4d8 fire damage, and are staggered, unable to take reactions until the start of their next turn. On a success, they take half damage and suffer no additional effect.

Once per round for the duration (1 round), the melody echoes faintly again at initiative count 0. Creatures that failed their original save feel a tremor of déjà vu and take 1 psychic damage as the rhythm loops.

#### Royal Claim of Provision
*4th-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 10 minutess
**Range:** Self (10.0-foot radius)
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You assert a Regal claim upon sanctioned stores maintained beyond the Veil. An item is drawn forth and manifested in an unoccupied space within range, bearing sigils of recognition from the Erelian Erudits.

The claimed provision may be a weapon, armor, or tool of notable value, a short-lived prototype bearing minor tesseral enhancement, or a sealed record such as plans, codes, or restricted writs. The item persists for a brief time before its claim expires and it is withdrawn from the Veil’s edge.

If the provision is squandered, destroyed, or unlawfully seized, the claim is marked as dishonored, and your standing suffers accordingly among those who track Regal obligation.

#### Scourge of Rewound Hours
*4th-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You unleash a brutal surge of temporal violence, wrenching time forward and backward in a single breath. Each creature affected must make a Constitution saving throw. On a failure, the creature takes 6d8 temporal damage as its body is forced to relive moments of extreme strain in rapid succession, flesh and essence tearing under contradictory timelines. On a success, the creature takes half damage.

If a creature is reduced to 0 hit points by this effect, its body becomes locked in a frozen instant for one round. During this suspension, time refuses to advance for it. The creature cannot be healed, stabilized, or revived until the moment resumes and the frozen second is finally allowed to pass.

#### Seal of Tempered Flesh
*4th-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 5.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 roundss

You impose a suppressive seal upon the target’s flesh and spirit, stilling impulses of desire and severing the feedback between appetite, emotion, and will. Passion dulls, confidence falters, and the body resists engagement beyond necessity.

The afflicted creature struggles to project charm or allure, their resolve frayed by inner dissonance. If the target is held under enchantment born of desire or fascination, this seal shatters that influence outright, restoring clarity through enforced restraint rather than consent.
 
- The target must make a Wisdom saving throw or suffer from:
- Disadvantage on Charisma checks involving seduction or persuasion.
-- 2 penalty to attack rolls and morale checks as a side effect of psychological distress.
- Temporary reductions in Wisdom, Constitution, and Charisma by 1d3 points for the duration.

#### Sever Anomaly
*4th-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You attempt to forcibly disconnect a supernatural entity from the material world. The target must make a Charisma saving throw. On a failure, it loses its ethereal, invisible, or extraplanar traits for the duration. If it was bound to this plane via an anomaly, it must roll a d6 each round—on a 1, it is banished permanently.

#### Sever Link
*4th-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You disrupt a telepathic bond, magical connection, or mental influence. The target must make a Wisdom saving throw. On a failure, they lose any telepathic abilities or magic item attunements for the duration.

#### Shades of the Unnamed
*4th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 8 hourss

You sever a creature’s presence from bindings that rely on name, identity, or recognition. For the duration, the target gains the following effects:

• The target is immune to the Under-Contract condition.
• The target’s name cannot be magically spoken, written, recorded, or recalled.
• All attempts to bind, compel, or track the target through contractual, bureaucratic, or identity-based magic automatically fail.
• Any creature attempting to recall or reference the target experiences hesitation and cognitive interference.
• Ongoing effects that rely on legal, contractual, or imposed identity are suppressed.

The spell immediately ends if the target willingly identifies themselves, signs a binding agreement, or submits identifying information.

#### Sleep Theft
*4th-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 special
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** S
**Duration:** Special

In the intimacy of flesh and fevered breath, the caster siphons the essence of slumber from their partner.

- After a shared act of passion, the target falls into an unnatural sleep for 1 hour per caster level.
- The caster awakens fully refreshed, as if they had slept those stolen hours.
- If the spell is cast repeatedly on the same victim, their dreams begin to fray, unraveling into visions of things best left unseen.
- If the target is asleep or unconscious, they automatically fail the saving throw against this spell.
- Some say the most powerful users of this spell never sleep at all, stealing rest from a hundred lovers.

#### Sphere of Sensory Oblivion
*4th-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You create a 20-foot-radius sphere in which light, sound, and distant perception are smothered. Creatures within the sphere are blinded and deafened, and magical means of communication fail unless a creature succeeds on a Wisdom saving throw. The space feels hollowed out, as if sensation itself has been removed.

#### Step Between Forms
*4th-level Illusion*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You blur at the edges, your body slipping into the seams of unreality. Shadows cling to you unnaturally, muting your presence, your weight, your warmth. You become a half- whisper in the world of form.

While the spell is active:- You gain resistance to all damage except fire and cognitive.- You cannot physically interact with creatures or objects (you pass through doors but cannot open them; you cannot attack or cast spells requiring material components).- You are considered heavily obscured to creatures relying on normal sight and invisible in dim light or darkness.- You can move through non- magical objects and walls as if they were difficult terrain, but you take 1d10 psychic damage if you end your turn inside a solid object.

#### Still-Time Antechamber
*4th-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 10.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You carve out a pocket of Still Time, a suspended antechamber where motion halts but awareness remains sharp. Up to six creatures within range are drawn into an echoed copy of the location, existing slightly apart from the Loom’s forward weave.

Outside the chamber, time flows normally. Within it, no external force may intrude, and no action taken can affect the world beyond. Through a silent veil, you may observe reality as it unfolds, gathering knowledge while remaining untouched.

Lingering too long risks thinning your thread. When you return, reality may hesitate to recognize you, causing subtle distortions as the Loom struggles to reweave your presence.

#### Still-Time Overclock
*4th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 hours

You draw the target into a heightened alignment with Still Time, compressing effort and intention into a narrow, relentless focus. For the duration, the creature’s movements sharpen and reactions tighten, granting a +2 bonus to AC, advantage on attack rolls, and resistance to exhaustion effects as their body functions beyond its natural cadence.

When the effect ends, the compressed moment releases all at once. For 1 hour, the creature suffers disadvantage on all ability checks as their thread struggles to resettle into the Loom’s ordinary rhythm, leaving them drained and unfocused.

#### Summon the Bound Retinue
*4th-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 10.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 hours

You call forth a retinue of spectral servants bound to authority rather than flesh. These figures resemble robed scribes, stone-faced attendants, and faceless functionaries of the Imperatum, each moving with practiced efficiency and unquestioning purpose.

For the duration, the retinue can perform non-combat labor such as assembly, repair, organization, transcription, or logistical processing at a rate equivalent to ten skilled workers. They do not tire, complain, or improvise, acting only within the scope of their summoned mandate.

If threatened or forced into combat, the retinue dissolves instantly, their purpose complete or revoked, leaving behind only the faint sense that order briefly passed through the space.

#### Suspension of Disbelief
*4th-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V
**Duration:** 1 hours

You briefly attune to the narrative fabric of reality, gaining an uncanny sensitivity to dramatic structure, clichés, and meta- patterns. For the duration, you can sense the presence of common story tropes in characters, environments, and events within range.

You can detect things like:
- When a villain is about to monologue
- If a side character radiates “tragic backstory energy”
- Whether a room feels “too conveniently empty”
- If an ancient prophecy is about to become relevant
- When someone is definitely about to betray the party

This insight is incredibly annoying to others. NPCs may roll Insight to feel disturbed by your overly convenient genre awareness.

Meta Mechanic (once per casting):

If the DM becomes visibly annoyed by your observations—subtly or overtly—you may “break the fourth wall.” When this happens:
- You may ask the DM one question about the current narrative, twist, or character.
- The DM must answer, but may do so cryptically.
- Your character forgets the answer consciously, but retains it subconsciously.
- The player gains one “narrative gut feeling” that can be invoked at any time for advantage on a single Insight, Perception, or Investigation check.

This ability can only be triggered once per casting.
Roleplay Guidance:- You might instinctively distrust someone because they “look like a redemption arc.”- You might refuse to read scrolls because “reading aloud always triggers curses.”- You might whisper “he’s the real villain” the moment you meet the king.

#### Thallan's Flecks of Repugnant Soap
*4th-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You cast a handful of impossibly dry, crumbling soap into the air. It dissolves mid- flight, releasing microscopic flecks of cleansing hatred that scour body, soul, and shame alike.

Each creature in a 20- foot- radius sphere centered on you must make a Constitution saving throw. On a failed save, a creature takes 11d4 poison damage as the soap sears away impurities—real or imagined—with unrelenting force. On a successful save, they take half damage.
- Affected creatures are coated in a stinging residue for 1 minute. During this time, they emit a foul, antiseptic stench, suffer disadvantage on Charisma checks, and cannot benefit from healing spells unless they succeed on a Constitution saving throw at the start of their turn.
- Creatures without skin (undead, constructs, oozes) are immune to this spell.

#### Thallan's Hand of Craven Opal
*4th-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You call upon the maddening echoes of the Craven Opal, forcing the minds of your enemies to grasp fragments of truths too vast to bear. Choose up to three creatures within range. Each must make an Intelligence saving throw.
- On a failure, a creature takes 5d8 psychic damage and has(disadvantage on Intelligence and Wisdom saving throws) until the end of its next turn.
- On a success, it takes half damage and suffers no other effect.

While concentrating on this spell, you may use your action on subsequent turns to target the same or different creatures within range (up to three again). Each new wave of insight echoes the original effect—forcing a new save, new damage.

#### The Crawling Hunger
*4th-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Permanent

You place a consuming need inside a creature, but it is not hunger for food—it is for something worse.
 
- The target must make a Wisdom saving throw. On a failure, they develop an insatiable hunger for a specific, forbidden thing, chosen randomly from the list below:
 
- The hunger cannot be resisted forever—every 24 hours without consuming the object, they take 2d6 psychic damage.
- If they give in, they feel no satisfaction, only greater hunger.
| Roll | Side Effect Description |
|------ |--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| 1 | Flesh of the Living – The target craves human flesh. They can resist, but only barely. |
| 2 | Dead Voices – The target wants to chew on books, scrolls, and paper, consuming knowledge instead of food. |
| 3 | Their Own Body – The target begins biting and gnawing at their own hands, arms, and lips when no one is looking. |
| 4 | Glass and Metal – They find themselves chewing on shards of glass and rusted nails, feeling neither pain nor damage—but never satisfaction. |
| 5 | Forgotten Names – The target whispers the names of those who have been erased from history, consuming their legacies with each repetition. |
| 6 | Shadows – They try to eat lightless spaces, their mouth opening wider than it should when they stand in darkness. |

#### The Infinite Stare
*4th-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

Your eyes become vessels of an unknowable force—an unblinking, paradoxical void that reflects nothing and sees everything. You focus this unnatural stare on a single creature within range.

The target must succeed on a Charisma saving throw or become Obsessed with your gaze. While obsessed, the creature:
- Cannot avert its eyes from you and cannot willingly move more than 30 feet away.
- Suffers disadvantage on Wisdom and Intelligence checks and saving throws as its thoughts loop in recursive terror.
- Takes 2d6 psychic damage at the start of each of its turns as your gaze frays its mental barriers.

The creature may attempt another saving throw at the end of each of its turns. On a success, the effect ends.

#### The Ticking Man’s Favor
*4th-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 minutes
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 24 hourss

You grant a creature the blessing of the Ticking Man, a timeless entity whose debts must always be paid.
 

- The target gains +1 to AC and saving throws while the spell is active.
- At any time within 24 hours, the Ticking Man may call in the favor, forcing the target to perform one action or request, no matter the cost.
- If the request is refused, the target immediately ages 2d20 years and loses the benefits of the spell.

#### Threadbound Recall
*4th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 10 minutess
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You bind a willing creature’s thread to a prepared point of safety within range. At any moment while the binding persists, the creature may sever its current position and snap instantly along the Loom to the designated location.

The recall may be invoked only once per casting. The passage leaves a faint disturbance in the surrounding Weft, making repeated use increasingly noticeable to those who watch for sudden absences and returns.

#### Unwitnessed Deeds
*4th-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You conjure a shroud of arcane interference that fouls the act of observation itself. Sightlines blur, divinatory senses slip, and memory refuses to hold what should have been seen.

For the duration, the following effects apply within the area:
	•	Divination magic used to observe or record the area suffers disadvantage, as visions fracture into static impressions, echoes, or false overlays.
	•	Magical sensors, scrying eyes, familiars used as observers, and similar effects fail to relay clear information, instead looping old images, fading to darkness, or presenting distorted scenes.
	•	Any creature attempting to observe the area remotely through magic must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw or be unable to recall what they perceived, retaining only vague impressions or missing time.

This spell does not render creatures invisible. Direct, unaided sight functions normally, but any attempt to watch, record, or verify events through supernatural means becomes deeply unreliable, as though reality itself refuses to be properly witnessed.

#### Verdant Reclamation
*4th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You awaken the buried will of nature beneath stone and ruin, commanding life to reclaim what was taken from it.

Twisting vines, iron-hard moss, and thorned growth burst from cracked stone and worked ground, spreading across the area.
	•	The terrain becomes choked with overgrowth, hindering movement.
	•	Creatures caught within must struggle against binding plants that seize limbs and armor alike.
	•	You may will the growth to crawl across walls or floors, extending its grasp.
	•	Constructs and creatures of purely inorganic nature are especially vulnerable, as the living world rejects their presence.

The spell transforms ruin into a battlefield where stone remembers it was once soil.

#### Withering Works
*4th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 120.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You call decay into being, drawing corrosive influence through the Weft and into the ground. A spreading sphere of rust, oil, and structural fatigue blooms outward, gnawing at matter and mechanism alike.

Each creature that begins its turn within the area must make a Constitution saving throw or suffer corrosive harm as materials weaken and forms degrade. Weapons dull and seize, surfaces crumble, and constructs find their bodies especially vulnerable to the imposed entropy.

As a bonus action, you may urge the blight to creep onward, dragging the zone of decay across the terrain like a slow, deliberate rot, leaving warped ground and failing structures in its wake.

#### Yarol's Veil
*4th-level Illusion*
**Casting Time:** 1 minutes
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You wrap yourself in the forgotten script of Yarol, creating a mobile sphere of veiled perception. For the duration, all creatures of your choice within a 30- foot radius of you become invisible. The area of effect moves with you, but the spell ends early if you move faster than half your speed, cast a spell, or make an attack.

Objects not held or worn remain visible, even if within the veil. Items carried by invisible creatures vanish along with them. Light, sound, and scent still pass through the veil—this is not silence, only obfuscation.

Creatures under this effect become heavily obscured to others, but not to one another—those within can still see each other clearly, as if the veil exists only to conceal them from the outside world.

#### Barb of Living Ruin
*5th-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You drive a needle of unstable ruin into the target, an invisible barb that seeds their body with volatile decay. On contact, the target takes 6d10 radiant damage and becomes contaminated for the duration. A faint, glowing scar shaped like a hooked barb marks the point of impact.

While contaminated, the target bleeds destructive energy in a 5-foot radius. Any creature that starts its turn within that radius, excluding you, takes 1d6 radiation damage. At the start of each of the target’s turns, it takes 1d4 radiation damage as its body struggles to contain the ruin. The contamination spreads to any creature that ends its turn grappling or touching the target.

If the target receives magical healing, the contamination ends for that creature, though the scar remains unless removed by Arcane Sterilization or Sigil of Restoration.

#### Covenant of Deferred Morena
*5th-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 24 hourss

You bind a creature beneath a covenant that delays Morena’s claim, securing its thread against immediate severance by the Loom.

Choose one creature within range. For the next 24 hours, the first time the target would die, the Loom forcibly reasserts its fading thread. The creature immediately returns to life at the location of its body with hit points equal to half its maximum hit points.

This covenant is fulfilled only once. After it triggers, the spell ends.

The body must remain sufficiently intact for the Loom to reclaim it. The covenant fails if the creature’s death results from disintegration, total bodily destruction, or effects that explicitly prevent revival.

The return does not remove conditions, afflictions, or ongoing effects present at the time of death unless explicitly stated otherwise.

Such deferrals are understood to incur consequence. The Loom does not forget intervention, and Morena’s claim is never nullified, only postponed.

#### Echoes of the Forgotten
*5th-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You disturb the sediment of memory, stirring impressions that should have faded. Within the affected space, unseen voices press against the mind with suffocating intimacy.

A 20-foot-radius sphere forms at a point you can see within range. The area fills with intangible murmurs perceptible only to those caught within.

Each creature in the sphere must make a Wisdom saving throw.

• Failure: The creature is Frightened and Deafened for the duration.
• Success: The creature is unaffected.

A creature Frightened by this spell perceives intrusive whispers shaped by its own recollections and anxieties. These manifestations are subjective, disjointed, and may evoke regret, loss, or unrealized possibility at the GM’s discretion.

A creature that ends its turn within the sphere must repeat the Wisdom saving throw, ending the effect on a success.

#### Edict of the Stilled Moment
*5th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You pronounce an Imperatum mandate that arrests an unfolding instant, forcing reality to defer its consequence.

When a creature you can see within 60 feet makes an attack roll or casts a spell, you may use your reaction to impose the edict. The creature must make a Wisdom saving throw.

• Failure: The triggering action is suspended and produces no immediate effects. The action resolves at the start of the creature’s next turn, using the original roll, spell slot, and declared parameters. No new decisions may be made when the effect resumes.

• Success: The action resolves normally.

A suspended spell is considered active for the purpose of concentration. If concentration is broken before the delayed resolution, the spell fails harmlessly.

You may affect only one moment with this spell at a time.

#### Faint Heartbeat
*5th-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You extend your perception beyond sight and sound, attuning to the fundamental cadence of living bodies.

For the duration, you sense the presence and precise location of all living creatures within range that possess a beating heart.

This perception:

• Ignores invisibility
• Ignores darkness
• Ignores mundane and magical concealment
• Penetrates cover and solid obstacles
• Functions regardless of Stealth or hiding

You perceive creatures as pulsing points of awareness, each marked by the unmistakable rhythm of life. This sense provides no insight into identity, thoughts, or condition, only location and movement.

This detection fails against:

• Undead
• Constructs
• Creatures without a biological pulse
• Creatures shielded by effects that explicitly block divination magic

#### Fleshsmith’s Alloy
*5th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 hours
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Permanent

You permanently fuse worked metal or bone with living tissue, creating an object that remembers sensation.

Choose a nonmagical weapon, suit of armor, or suitable metal/bone object within range. Over the casting, the material binds with living flesh, transforming into a permanent Fleshsmith’s Alloy.

The object becomes magical.

⸻

Permanent Cost

The casting exacts a biological toll.

The caster suffers:

• 2d10 necrotic damage that cannot be reduced or prevented
• Maximum hit points reduced by an amount equal to the necrotic damage taken

This reduction lasts until the caster completes a long rest.

If this reduction would drop the caster’s maximum hit points to 0, the spell fails.

⸻

Weapon Infusion

If the target is a weapon:

• Gains +1 bonus to attack and damage rolls
• Remains unnaturally pristine
• Exhibits faint organic movement when held

⸻

Armor Infusion

If the target is armor:

• Grants resistance to nonmagical bludgeoning damage
• Flexes and twitches subtly on impact

⸻

Destruction

If destroyed, the alloy releases a psychic death-shriek.

• Creatures within 10 feet must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw or be Frightened until the end of their next turn

#### Grand Provision
*5th-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You conjure a plentiful banquet of wholesome food and drink, enough to sustain a gathering of creatures. The feast appears at a point you can see within range and remains for the duration.

Up to twelve creatures may partake of the provision. A creature that spends at least 10 minutes eating gains the following benefits:

• The creature regains 4d8 hit points

• For 1 hour, the creature has advantage on Constitution saving throws made to resist poison or disease

A creature can benefit from this spell only once per long rest.

The conjured food spoils and vanishes when the spell ends.

Duration: 1 hour.

#### Gravity Bubble
*5th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You conjure a 10-foot-radius sphere of unstable gravitational force centered on a point you can see within range. The area is heavily distorted for the duration.

When the sphere appears, creatures of your choice within it must make a Dexterity saving throw.

On a failure, a creature is lifted up to 20 feet upward. If the creature cannot remain aloft, it falls at the end of the movement, taking 2d6 bludgeoning damage from the impact.

On a success, the creature maintains footing but moves with difficulty, having disadvantage on Strength and Dexterity checks while inside the sphere.

While you maintain concentration, the sphere’s gravity shifts unpredictably. At the start of each of your turns, roll a d4:

• 1: Gravity inverts. Creatures currently in contact with a surface must make a Dexterity saving throw or be lifted up to 20 feet.

• 2: Gravity pulls laterally in a random horizontal direction. Creatures must make a Dexterity saving throw or be moved up to 10 feet in that direction.

• 3: Gravity intensifies. Movement speeds inside the sphere are halved until the start of your next turn. Unsecured objects are forced downward.

• 4: Gravity weakens. Creatures inside the sphere cannot take reactions until the start of your next turn.

Creatures inside the sphere have disadvantage on ranged attack rolls.
| d4 Roll | Gravity Surge Effect |
|--------- |--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| 1 | Upward – Creatures must make a Dexterity save or be lifted again. |
| 2 | Sideways (caster’s left) – Creatures are thrown 10 feet to the side, potentially colliding with surfaces. |
| 3 | Downward Surge – Gravity doubles briefly; all movement is halved and unsecured objects slam to the ground (1d6 damage). |
| 4 | Zero- G Lull – Creatures float freely, unable to take reactions until the start of their next turn. |

#### Hollow of Lingering Thread
*5th-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 hours

You seize a departing soul at the instant of death, denying its passage and binding its fading thread to a fragile echo of memory.

Choose one creature that has died within the last round. The creature’s soul is bound as a Hollowed remnant for the duration. The body remains lifeless and cannot be restored while the Hollow persists.

The Hollow manifests as a disembodied, intangible presence anchored to a point you can see within range.

While the Hollow endures:

• It can speak and be heard within 30 feet
• It retains the creature’s memories and personality, though its perceptions are unstable
• It can manipulate unattended objects within 10 feet as if using a spectral hand (no more than 10 pounds)
• It has no physical form, cannot attack, and cannot cast spells
• It is immune to all damage and conditions except those that specifically affect undead or spirits

The Hollow’s cognition is imperfect. At the start of each of its turns, roll a d6:

1–2 → The Hollow is disoriented and cannot act that turn
3–6 → The Hollow acts normally

If the spell ends, the soul immediately passes on and the creature may be restored by normal means if its body remains viable.

Duration: Concentration, up to 1 minute.

#### Imperial Rite of Erasure
*5th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 10 minutess
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Permanent

You invoke the Imperatum’s censoring authority, severing a creature from the mechanisms by which the world acknowledges standing, identity, and claim.

Choose one creature you can see within range. For the duration, the target’s presence is metaphysically deemphasized.

While affected:

• Creatures have disadvantage on Intelligence checks made to recall information about the target
• The first time a creature attempts to identify, remember, or meaningfully reference the target, it must succeed on an Intelligence saving throw (DC 18) or recall only vague or distorted impressions
• The target has advantage on Charisma (Deception) checks made to pass unnoticed in formal or institutional interactions
• Hostile creatures are not prevented from perceiving the target, but their recognition lacks certainty unless directly engaged

This spell does not render the creature invisible, inaudible, or hidden, nor does it alter physical records. Instead, it subtly destabilizes the cognitive and social anchors that sustain recognition.

Creatures immune to being charmed are unaffected.

Duration: Concentration, up to 1 hour.

#### Imprint of the Permanence
*5th-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Permanent

You draw forth the distilled metaphysical pattern of a creature, manifesting its defining essence as a fragile Imprint of memory, identity, and consequence.

Choose one creature within range. The target must be willing, incapacitated, or restrained for the spell to succeed.

The creature’s Imprint appears in an unoccupied space you can see within 10 feet of you. The Imprint is a Tiny, intangible magical construct visible only to you, representing the creature’s existential signature.

While the Imprint persists, you may manipulate it using one of the following options:

Alter Imprint.
You introduce subtle distortions into the creature’s metaphysical pattern. For the duration, the creature has disadvantage on saving throws against effects that rely upon true names, identity recognition, or attunement.

Obscure Imprint.
The creature becomes difficult to isolate through supernatural means. For the duration, divination spells that attempt to locate or identify the creature must succeed on a spellcasting ability check against your spell save DC or fail.

Seal Imprint.
You temporarily stabilize the creature’s existential pattern. For the duration, the creature has advantage on saving throws against charm, possession, and effects that alter memory or identity.

Only one Imprint effect may be active at a time.

The Imprint lasts for the duration or until dismissed as an action.

Duration: Concentration, up to 10 minutes.

A creature affected by this spell is considered Altered for the duration of any Imprint manipulation.

#### Ledger of Justified Existence
*5th-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You invoke the Loom’s unseen calculus, forcing a creature to answer for its claim to substance.

Choose one creature you can see within range. The target must make a Charisma saving throw.

• Failure: The creature becomes immaterial for 1 minute. While immaterial, it is conscious and aware but is treated as though it does not exist for the purpose of interacting with the world:

– It cannot move or take actions
– It cannot affect or be affected by creatures, objects, or effects
– It is immune to all damage and conditions
– It cannot be targeted or perceived by any means

When the effect ends, the creature reappears in the space it last occupied, or the nearest unoccupied space if that location is no longer valid.

• Success: The creature is unaffected.

Creatures native to the current plane make this saving throw with advantage.

#### Lien upon the Nought
*5th-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 hours

You impose a binding claim upon a creature’s existence, marking its thread as owing consequence. The target must make a Charisma saving throw. On a failure, it becomes bound to fulfill a single command issued by you, provided the command does not directly lead to its death.

If the creature resists the obligation, its thread tightens painfully, dealing 2d10 psychic damage at the start of each of its turns. Should the creature die while the lien persists, its soul does not pass on to Morena, instead held in suspended claim until the debt is resolved or transferred through ritual accord.

#### Midnight Admirer
*5th-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You conjure an idealized romantic apparition bound to a creature’s longing, vanity, and unattended desire.

Choose one creature you can see within range. An intangible admirer manifests, perceptible only to the target. The figure speaks, gestures, and behaves as an impossibly charming suitor shaped by the creature’s subconscious preferences.

When the admirer appears, the target must make a Charisma saving throw.

• Failure:
For 1 minute, the creature is emotionally disoriented:

– Disadvantage on Wisdom (Insight) checks
– Disadvantage on Concentration checks
– The admirer occupies the creature’s attention

• Success:
The spell has no effect.

The admirer cannot physically interact with the world.

If the creature willingly reciprocates the admirer’s attention, the spell ends.

If the creature consciously rejects or refuses the admirer, the apparition marks the slight. The magic does not immediately punish the refusal.

Instead, the admirer may return during the creature’s next long rest.

When the admirer returns in this manner, the creature must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw.

• Failure:
The long rest provides no benefit and the creature gains one level of exhaustion. The refusal count increases by one.

• Success:
The admirer fails to manifest that night.

A creature that accumulates six failed manifestations becomes fatally drained. At the end of the sixth disruption, the admirer siphons the creature’s vitality.

The creature immediately drops to 0 hit points and must make death saving throws as its life force is consumed by the curse.

If the creature dies in this way, its death is considered a curse-induced death.

The recurring manifestations end if the spell is dispelled or removed by magic capable of breaking powerful curses, such as Remove Curse, Greater Restoration, or similar effects at the GM’s discretion.

#### Rapid Reload
*5th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 bonus action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 9 roundss

You briefly unshackle motion from hesitation. For the duration, you ignore the loading property of ranged weapons you wield, as your hands reset bows, mechanisms, or thrown implements with impossible speed. While this spell persists, you also gain advantage on initiative rolls, as your body reacts before thought can slow it.

#### Regency Intercession
*5th-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 reaction
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 rounds

You invoke a regent’s authority to halt the immediate unfolding of events. When a creature within range attempts an action, its execution is deferred by one full round as the moment is seized for review. The target must make a Wisdom saving throw. On a failure, the action does not occur until the start of its next turn.

If the creature attempts to force the action through, it must expend both its bonus action and reaction struggling against the imposed intercession, accomplishing nothing in the process. Creatures accustomed to rigid hierarchies of command and obedience find the delay especially difficult to resist.

#### Rend of the Veil
*5th-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

The area is difficult terrain. At the start of each creature’s turn while inside the zone, it must make a Constitution saving throw, taking 4d10 bludgeoning damage on a failure. Teleportation and planar movement automatically fail within the fractured space.

#### Revelation That Breaks the Mind
*5th-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You tear open a sealed truth never meant to be carried by mortal thought and force it into the awareness of a creature within range. The target must make an Intelligence saving throw. On a failure, it takes 6d10 psychic damage as forbidden understanding floods its mind and fractures its sense of self. For 1 minute, the creature suffers disadvantage on Intelligence and Charisma checks while its thoughts spiral around the implications of what it has learned.
On a successful save, the creature takes half damage and suffers no further effect. Some knowledge does not enlighten. It overwhelms.

#### Rite of Royal Absolution
*5th-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You perform a cleansing rite that strips away imposed influence and coerced obedience, restoring a creature’s sovereign will. The spell removes all poison, disease, and dependency effects, and breaks long-term mental domination, conditioning, and subliminal control. Effects born of indoctrination, enforced loyalty, or imposed identity unravel and lose their hold.

At higher power, the rite can also sever cursed implants, binding artifacts, or devices that exert control over thought or behavior, restoring clarity and autonomy to the afflicted.

#### Rite of Twin Accord
*5th-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You bind the life rhythms of two willing creatures into perfect concord, forging a shared cadence of motion, thought, and pain. While within 10 feet of each other, the bonded creatures gain advantage on attack rolls, resistance to psychic damage, and the ability to communicate telepathically. When one creature takes damage, the other may use its reaction to absorb half of that damage, splitting the harm between them. The bond manifests as a steady, unseen pulse felt by both participants. If either creature becomes unwilling or unconscious, the accord immediately dissolves.

#### Sigil Missive
*5th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 10 minutess
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You weave a concealed lattice of sigils into a mundane readable surface, embedding a hidden message within an existing object such as a signpost, message board, inscription, mural, carving, or written notice.

Choose a creature known to you. Only the designated recipient can perceive the message’s true content. To all other creatures, the surface appears entirely normal or contains only harmless, context-appropriate text or markings.

The message must be inscribed upon a nonmagical object or surface capable of bearing visible information. The writing or symbols do not appear overtly magical and withstand casual inspection.

A creature other than the recipient may attempt to detect irregularities by making an Intelligence (Investigation) check against your spell save DC. On a success, the creature recognizes that the surface contains hidden meaning but cannot decipher it without magic or extraordinary means.

If the message is not perceived by the intended recipient within 7 days, the sigils degrade and the hidden content is lost.

#### Spectral Retraction
*5th-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 90.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You invoke an invisible tether of force that violently pulls a creature backward through the path it came.

Choose one creature within range. That target must succeed on a Strength saving throw or be dragged up to 30 feet in a straight line toward the space it occupied at the start of its previous turn.

- If the target collides with a solid object or creature during this forced movement, it takes 6d12 psychic damage, and the object or creature it struck takes half as much.
- On a successful save, the target is not moved, but still takes half damage from the forceful retraction.

#### Sundering Gate
*5th-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You invoke forbidden authority and rend open a violent passage between two points of the world that should never touch.

A vast, unstable rift opens between your position and another location you can see within range. The tear yawns wide, its edges writhing with warped light and fractured space, and remains open for the duration so long as your focus holds.
	•	Any creature may step through the rift as a movement, arriving instantly at the far side.
	•	All who pass must return through the same gate before it closes.

Those who fail to return are cast into the Between, a collapsing lattice of half-formed dimensions.

While lost between worlds:
	•	The creature cannot be targeted, perceived, contacted, or located by any means.
	•	After 1d6 hours, the world violently rejects them, expelling them into the nearest safe, unoccupied space near the destination.
	•	Upon return, they suffer 3d10 force damage, their bodies and minds wrenched by temporal and spatial dissonance.

If you willingly end the spell or lose consciousness, the gate snaps shut instantly, severing all remaining paths.

#### Thallan's Suppurating Lance
*5th-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 120.0 feet
**Components:** S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You tear open a festering seam in the air and expel a spear of starving, ulcerous light in a straight line. The lance does not illuminate. It infects space as it passes, like a wound dragged across reality.

Each creature in the line must make a Constitution saving throw.

• Failure: The creature is Cursed by the Lance and suffers 2d8 fire damage as blistering fissures crawl beneath its skin, leaking heat and sickly radiance.
• Success: The creature takes half damage and resists the curse.

While Cursed by the Lance:

• The body of a slain creature ruptures violently, collapsing inward before bursting in a spray of incandescent rot. Creatures within 10 feet take 2d6 fire damage.
• Any creature killed by this detonation tears open in the same manner, allowing the corruption to propagate in a chain of meat-splitting flashes.
• Cursed creatures twitch subtly. Their shadows lag behind them. A faint, wet crackling accompanies their movement.
