*5th-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

- Any creature attempting to teleport, phase shift, or enter the area via extradimensional travel must succeed on a Charisma saving throw.
- On a failed save, they are forcibly bounced back to their point of origin and take 4d6 psychic damage as the firewall briefly stabilizes their reality—violently.
- Creatures that attempt to cross into the firewall without magical travel feel a pressure in the air but suffer no immediate effect unless the area is layered with other wards.
- The firewall emits a low- frequency pulse only detectable to those attuned to arcane signals. To most, it appears as empty space.

#### The Price of Names
*5th-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 minutes
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You strip power from a target’s true name, making them vulnerable.

- The target has disadvantage on all saving throws against effects that explicitly name them in their casting, inscription, or invocation (such as through a name spoken aloud, signed in a document, or used in a ritual).
- Any creature who speaks the target’s name aloud can sense the direction (not exact location) of the target within 1 mile, provided the target is on the same plane.
- This effect ends if the name is burned, rewritten, legally nullified, or exchanged through sanctioned rites (as negotiated through an A.S.T.R.A.L. broker or similar agent).

#### Truth of Gizy ao zrfzm

You project a metaphysical failsafe that prevents involuntary memory alteration and data corruption within a 10- foot radius sphere.

- Any attempt to erase, fragment, or overwrite memories in this area automatically fails.
- Spells like Memory Fragmentation, Compliance Protocol, and A.S.T.R.A.L. Redaction are nullified within the field.
- Digital and paper records within the field are temporarily immune to deletion by magical or technological means.

#### Unbound Stone
*5th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You rewrite the obedience of matter itself, compelling solid substance to part and flow aside like water under command.
	•	Choose a solid, nonmagical wall, vault, or reinforced surface no more than 5 feet thick. You open a 10-foot-long, 5-foot-wide passage, the material folding away in rippling bands of pale, unstable light.
	•	The passage shimmers faintly, semi-translucent, as though reality itself is uncertain it should exist.
	•	The opening seals itself after 1 round unless you maintain concentration, in which case it remains for the spell’s duration.
	•	The passage cannot be formed through living creatures or organic matter.

Warded or Enchanted Surfaces:
If the surface is protected by magic, make an Arcana check (DC = 10 + the level of the ward). On a failure, the spell collapses harmlessly, leaving the surface untouched.

#### Weft Saturation
*5th-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self (30.0-foot radius)
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You flood a localized area with an excess of arcane weave, forcing incompatible strands of reality to occupy the same space. Within this zone, magic does not fail because it is suppressed, but because it is overwritten by too many simultaneous truths.

Spells unravel before they can fully resolve, ongoing enchantments flicker and lose coherence, and beings whose existence relies on bindings, artifacts, or sustained arcane structures experience severe disorientation as the Loom pulls them in conflicting directions.

The air hums with invisible tension, as if reality itself is struggling to decide which version of the world should apply here.

The effect ends early if the target passes three consecutive Wisdom saves or if a a restoration spell is cast.

|------- |------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ |

#### Womb of the Unwritten
*5th-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 10 minutess
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Permanent

You whisper an incantation not meant for mortal tongues, invoking the presence of something that waits between fate and flesh. The spell rewrites the biological continuity of the target’s reproductive essence, severing it from natural law and entangling it with the unknown.

- The change is not immediately noticed—it takes effect subtly, like a whisper embedded in the fabric of their being.

| Roll | Side Effect Description |
|------- |---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| 1–2 | Fertility Erasure – The target is forgotten by the lineage of time; they can no longer conceive, and records of their ancestry begin to fade from existence. |

#### Conjure Seducers
*6th-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 minutes
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Special

You utter forbidden words of beckoning, calling forth a presence drawn not by allegiance, but by desire, fascination, or emotional resonance.

Choose an unoccupied space within range. An alluring extraplanar entity materializes and remains for the duration. The entity is bound to your service but retains its own will, temperament, and interpretation of your commands.

The creature is neither mindless nor fully obedient. It cooperates selectively, expresses preferences, and pursues subtle interests of its own.

Each time a creature engages in a meaningful interaction with the entity, that creature must make a Constitution saving throw. Meaningful interaction includes extended conversation, physical contact, or willingly accepting favors, bargains, or assistance.

• Failure: The creature suffers a draining backlash, taking 3d6 psychic damage and having disadvantage on Constitution checks until it finishes a long rest.
• Failure by 5 or more: The creature also gains one level of exhaustion.

A creature can only be subjected to this saving throw once per turn.

The entity remains until dismissed, destroyed, or the spell ends. When it departs, it invariably extracts some narrative or situational concession determined by the GM.

Creatures immune to charm effects have advantage on the saving throw.

#### Echo of the Forgotten
*6th-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You call forth a fractured specter of residual existence, an entity shaped from discarded impressions and incomplete memory.

The Echo manifests in an unoccupied space you can see within range and persists for the duration.

⸻

Echo of the Forgotten

• Armor Class: 16
• Hit Points: 60
• Speed: 0 ft., Fly 40 ft. (hover)

• Resistances: Bludgeoning, Piercing, and Slashing from nonmagical attacks
• Condition Immunities: Grappled, Prone, Restrained

⸻

Phantom Passage

The Echo can move through creatures and solid objects as if they were difficult terrain. If it ends its turn inside an object, it is harmlessly shunted to the nearest unoccupied space.

⸻

Actions

Cognitive Tendrils. Melee Spell Attack: your spell attack modifier to hit, reach 10 ft., one target.

• Hit: 2d10 psychic damage.

The Echo acts on your initiative and requires your bonus action to take the Cognitive Tendrils action. If you issue no commands, it takes no actions.

⸻

Behavior

The Echo obeys only deliberate commands you provide. If you are Incapacitated, the Echo vanishes at the end of your next turn.

#### Erudit Mind Fracture
*6th-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You rupture the disciplined architecture of a creature’s mind, splintering the ordered structures that sustain thought and perception.

Choose one creature within range. The target must make an Intelligence saving throw.

• Failure: The creature takes 8d8 psychic damage and is Incapacitated until the end of its next turn.

• Failure by 5 or more: The creature is additionally Blinded for 1 minute. The creature may repeat the Intelligence saving throw at the end of each of its turns, ending the blindness on a success.

• Success: The creature takes half damage and suffers no additional effects.

⸻

Scaling

When cast using a spell slot of 7th level or higher, the fracture deepens, tearing through more resilient strata of cognition. The psychic damage increases by 1d8 for each slot level above 6th, as progressively deeper layers of ordered thought collapse under the strain.

#### Everbright Cascade
*6th-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You unleash a torrent of Everbright radiance interwoven with striations of shadow, scouring the space before you with blinding intensity.

A 30-foot cone of refracted brilliance erupts from you. Creatures within the area must make a Constitution saving throw.

• Failure: A creature takes 8d8 fire damage and is Blinded until the end of its next turn.
• Success: A creature takes half damage and is not Blinded.

The radiance leaves behind a fleeting instability. Until the start of your next turn, the affected area is considered difficult terrain as light-distorted space resists movement.

The flare fades almost immediately, though afterimages and shimmering distortions may briefly linger.

#### Forced Alignment
*6th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 hours

You impose a momentary perfection upon a creature’s vital thread, coercing the Loom into an idealized configuration.

Choose one creature within range that you can see. The target must make a Charisma saving throw.

• Failure: Select one of the creature’s ability scores. That score increases by 4, to a maximum of 24, for the duration.

The imposed perfection destabilizes the creature’s weave. Roll a d6 to determine which other ability score is reduced:

1 Strength
2 Dexterity
3 Constitution
4 Intelligence
5 Wisdom
6 Charisma

The rolled ability score (excluding the enhanced score; reroll if necessary) is reduced by 4 for the duration.

• Success: The creature resists the effect and is unaffected.

When the spell ends, all modified ability scores return to their original values.

#### Imperial Shroud of Denial
*6th-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self (30.0-foot radius)
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You impose the Imperatum’s censoring veil upon a region, asserting sovereign control over perception, detection, and distant inquiry.

Choose a point you can see within range. A 30-foot-radius sphere centered on that point is shrouded for the duration.

Within the sphere:

• Divination spells of 6th level or lower cannot perceive into or within the area
• Magical sensors, scrying effects, and clairvoyant manifestations are suppressed while overlapping the veil
• Creatures attempting supernatural perception treat the area as heavily obscured
• Illusory distortions and false impressions subtly manifest at the boundary of perception

Effects created by divination magic of 7th level or higher are not automatically suppressed but require a successful spellcasting ability check against your spell save DC to function within the area.

The veil blocks extraplanar observation only for effects of 6th level or lower.

Duration: Concentration, up to 10 minutes.

#### Loop of the Stolen Moment
*6th-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 minutes
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You seize a creature’s immediate past and bind it into a closed temporal loop.

Choose one creature you can see within range. The target must make a Wisdom saving throw. On a failure, the creature becomes trapped in a repeating fragment of time for the spell’s duration.

While trapped in the loop:

• The creature cannot choose new actions, movement, or reactions.
• On each of its turns, it must repeat the same actions, movement, and attacks it performed on its previous turn, following the same targets, paths, and decisions where possible.
• If a repeated action is no longer possible (for example, the target has moved, a path is blocked, or a condition prevents the action), that portion of the turn is lost with no substitute behavior.
• The creature’s awareness remains intact, but it cannot alter the looped behavior.

At the end of each of its turns, the creature may repeat the Wisdom saving throw, ending the effect on a success.

#### Mannequin's Lament
*6th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 hours

You impose a rigid stillness upon a creature’s living form, compelling flesh to yield to lifeless substance.

Choose one creature you can see within range. The target must make a Constitution saving throw against your spell save DC.

• Failure:
The creature’s body hardens into an inert, sculptural state resembling wood, glass, or porcelain (chosen at casting).

While transformed:

– The creature is Paralyzed.
– It remains conscious and aware of its surroundings.
– It cannot speak, move, or take actions.
– It gains resistance to nonmagical damage.
– It is considered an object for the purpose of forced movement.

• Success:
The spell has no effect.

⸻

Concentration & Duration

The transformation lasts for the spell’s duration while you maintain concentration.

If your concentration ends, the creature immediately returns to its normal state with no additional harm.

⸻

Shattering Risk

If the transformed creature takes damage, the rigid form may fracture:

• Whenever the creature takes damage, it must make a Constitution saving throw.

– Failure: The creature takes additional damage equal to the triggering damage type, representing structural cracking.
– Success: No additional effect.

⸻

Permanent Lament

If the creature remains transformed for the full duration, the effect becomes permanent.

A permanently transformed creature:

– Does not age or decay
– Requires magic capable of reversing major transmutations, such as Greater Restoration, Remove Curse, True Resurrection, or equivalent magic at the GM’s discretion

Time limits on restorative magic are ignored, as the creature’s state is preserved without biological decay.

You trigger a violent psychic surge that collapses thought into searing static.

– The creature takes 8d6 psychic damage.

– The creature takes half damage.

#### Paradox Echo
*6th-level Illusion*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S

You leave behind a temporal echo of yourself, a fractured imprint repeating your most recent motion as if caught between moments. #### Power Word: Unravel
*6th-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You speak a single, forbidden syllable: A sonic anomaly that cuts beneath thought, identity, and social constraint. The moment it leaves your lips, the word spreads like an invisible shockwave, slipping past armor, modesty, and mental fortitude.

Every creature within 60 feet of you who can hear the word, including yourself, must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw or be compelled to immediately strip all worn items, including clothing, armor, uniforms, accessories, magical attire, and identity- linked gear.

Affected creatures drop whatever they are holding and use their next movement and action (if able) to completely disrobe, regardless of current danger, weather, or social context. The compulsion lasts until the creature has removed all items or is incapacitated.

- The caster is not immune.
- Creatures immune to being charmed are unaffected.
- Deafened creatures or those in soundproof areas are unaffected.
- Constructs or creatures that do not wear gear are unaffected.
- If a creature removes magical protective gear, their AC may drop, and spell effects tied to those items end as usual.

Additional Effects
In addition to its physical effect, the power word unravels falsehoods.
- All illusions, glamers, disguises, and non- permanent magical concealments affecting creatures in range are immediately dispelled, as if targeted by dispel magic.
- Creatures under effects such as disguise self, invisibility, or illusion- based shapeshifting are revealed in their true forms for 1 minute.

#### Prism Shear 
*6th-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 hours

You unleash a pulse of pure polarity—light and shadow intertwined and tearing at each other with violent intensity. This unstable radiance converges on a creature within range, attempting to shear their essence between illumination and oblivion.

The target must make a Constitution saving throw. On a failure, they take 12d10 fire damage, pulled between the blinding burn of light and the consuming void of shadow. On a success, they take half damage.

If the target is reduced to 0 hit points by this spell, their form is torn into two halves—one vanishing in a beam of searing light, the other collapsing into inky residue.

#### Rimefold Exsanguination
*6th-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You tear the warmth from a creature’s flesh as if unthreading heat from blood, forcing it to spill outward into the world in a violent frostbound surge.

Choose one creature within range. The target must make a Constitution saving throw.
	•	On a failure, the creature is ravaged by unnatural cold as its body’s heat is ripped away, dealing severe cold damage. Its muscles stiffen and numb, leaving it unsteady and sluggish in its next strike.
	•	On a success, the creature resists the worst of the rimefold, suffering reduced cold damage and no lingering impairment.

If the target is in contact with metal, stone, or another heat-binding surface, the stolen warmth lashes outward. Creatures nearby are scorched by sudden frost as the displaced heat collapses into biting cold around them.

The air cracks and fogs instantly where the spell takes hold, and those who witness it swear they can see heat fleeing like pale ghosts from the victim’s skin.

**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You channel a precise surge of arcane force through a creature’s body, stilling thought, purging distortion, and re-aligning the spirit with its natural rhythm.
	•	All mind-affecting conditions are removed, including fear, confusion, domination, and mental overload.

	•	If the spell is forced upon an unwilling creature, it must succeed on a Constitution saving throw or be stunned for 1 minute, its senses briefly drowned in silence.

The rite is taxing and invasive, briefly stripping the mind to its foundations before allowing it to rebuild cleanly.

#### Slip Between Timelines
*6th-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You step sideways into a neighboring thread of time, a reflection of the world where moments were never chosen and events never fully occurred. In this half-real passage, the world appears hollow and distant, as though carved from memory rather than matter.

While veiled within this untaken timeline, you may move freely and unseen, untouched by sight, sound, or magic rooted in the waking world. Walls offer no welcome, voices carry no meaning, and nothing you do leaves a mark. You are a passing thought, not a presence.

When the spell ends, the abandoned timeline releases you, and you return to the world of consequence exactly where you began, as though you had never left at all. Some who use this magic swear they feel another version of themselves hesitate just out of reach, wondering why it was left behind.

#### Stone Ship
*6th-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 120.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You conjure a magically reinforced stone ship at a point you can see within range. The ship appears instantly and gently settles without causing damage, regardless of its immense weight.- If summoned onto water:
The ship immediately sinks to the bottom without damage and remains indefinitely as a stable underwater structure.- If summoned onto land or any solid surface:
The ship appears safely resting on the ground, remaining for 1 minute before vanishing harmlessly. It can serve as temporary cover, shelter, or a temporary barricade during this time.

Creatures or objects caught underneath when the ship is conjured are gently pushed aside and take no damage.
- The ship cannot cause physical harm due to its magical weightlessness when conjured.
- Provides half- cover (+2 AC) to creatures aboard or behind it.
- Once summoned, the ship cannot be moved or manipulated by normal physical means due to its immense (though magically nullified) weight.
| Spell Slot Level | Ship Size | Capacity |
|------------------ |----------------- |----------------------------------- |
| 1st | Tiny (5 ft.) | Fits 1 Small creature comfortably |
| 2nd | Small (10 ft.) | Fits up to 2 Medium creatures |
| 3rd | Medium (20 ft.) | Fits up to 6 Medium creatures |
| 4th | Large (40 ft.) | Fits up to 12 Medium creatures |
| 5th | Huge (60 ft.) | Fits up to 30 Medium creatures |

#### Summon the Saint
*6th-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 hours
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Permanent

You invoke the Assassins of the Saint, a hidden order of executioners bound by ancient contracts. This spell marks a target for death, ensuring that they will never know peace again.

- At dawn the next day, the target awakens with a blood- red rose placed on their chest.
- From this moment, Assassins of the Saint will begin hunting them.
- The first assassin arrives within 1d6 days, with each subsequent hunter increasing in lethality.

 Counterplay & Removal:
- The mark cannot be dispelled through normal means.
- Only by making an offering of equal or greater worth (to the Saint’s order) can the mark be transferred to another soul.

#### The Backdoor
*6th-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You target a door, wall, or secure entryway within range that you or an ally has previously passed through. For the duration, you and up to five willing creatures can step through a flickering illusion of that entrance, appearing on the other side as if you’d bypassed its barriers.
- The entrance must be non- magical, or you must succeed on a DC 20 Arcana check to bypass magical locks.
- The illusionary gateway remains open for 10 seconds after the first creature steps through, then vanishes.
- Any creature attempting to follow after that must make a DC 16 Dexterity saving throw or be displaced—emerging up to 30 feet away in a random nearby location.
- Surveillance systems or magical wards detect your passage as a security anomaly, triggering local alerts unless suppressed beforehand.

#### The Bleeding Contract
*6th-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 hours
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Permanent

You draft a supernatural contract, binding the signee to a deal they cannot escape—either willingly or through legal loopholes within reality itself.
 
- The contract must specify clear, finite terms (e.g., “deliver the encrypted drive,” “never disclose my presence,” “report back monthly”). 
- A creature may willingly sign the contract or be coerced through a failed Wisdom saving throw.
- If the signee violates the terms, they begin to hemorrhage lifeforce, suffering 1d6 bleeding damage per hour until the contract is honored or the caster dissolves it.
- The contract cannot be undone by mundane means. It can only be nullified through a corporate tribunal, anomaly override, or higher- order reality arbitration.
If the contract is poorly worded or vague, it will self- interpret using its own logic, often to the caster’s detriment. Corporate legal departments recommend all terms be double- verified before casting.

#### The Maw That Hungers
*6th-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self (30.0-foot radius)
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You conjure a vast, spectral maw beneath you—its jagged teeth grinding the threads of reality. The air trembles with a silent hunger, and all creatures of your choice within a 30- foot radius must succeed on a Constitution saving throw or suffer the following effects:

- Their maximum hit points are reduced by 2d10. This reduction lasts until they complete a long rest. 
- They become Frightened of you until the end of your next turn. 
- Their healing is halved for the duration of the spell.

A creature that fails this save by 10 or more is also afflicted with the Altered condition for 1 minute, their features subtly reshaped by the hunger of the void.

While the spell is active, the ground pulses like a throat, and creatures who begin their turn within the area take 1d6 fire damage as spectral teeth snap at their soul.

#### Theorem of the Broken Weft
*6th-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 minutes
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You draw corrupted strands of the Tesserac Weft together, weaving them into a semi-sentient construct of scrap, forgotten designs, and abandoned intent. The construct hauls itself into being as a towering assemblage of warped metal, bound memories, and tesseral tension. It obeys your spoken commands without hesitation, sharing your initiative and acting immediately after your turn.

The construct’s blows land with crushing tesseral force, and its unstable core occasionally vents Everbright energy in violent arcs. Though formidable, its mind is flawed. At the start of each of its turns, the Weft strains against its form, and on a moment of instability it lashes inward, wracking the construct with cognitive backlash and erratic behavior.

At higher invocations, you reinforce the weave, granting the construct greater endurance and deadlier precision as more strands of the Weft are forced into alignment.

 Mech Stats 
Medium or Large Construct, AC 17, HP 85 
Speed 30 ft., Climb 15 ft. 
STR 18, DEX 10, CON 16, INT 3, WIS 10, CHA 3 
Saving Throws: Con +6 
Damage Immunities: Poison, Psychic 
Condition Immunities: Charmed, Frightened, Poisoned 
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft., Passive Perception 10 
Languages: Understands the caster's commands, but cannot speak 

 Actions

Force Slam. *Melee Weapon Attack:* +8 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. 
Hit: 3d10 force damage.

Wrist Cannon (Recharge 5–6). 
The mech fires an unstable arcane round in a 30- foot line that is 5 feet wide. 
Each creature in the line must make a Dexterity saving throw (DC 16), taking 4d8 radiant damage on a failed save, or half as much on a success.

Interpose Shield (1/turn). 
When a creature within 5 feet is hit by an attack, the mech can intercept the blow, reducing the damage by 2d10 + its Constitution modifier.

#### Usurpation of Will
*6th-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You intrude upon a creature’s decision-making, threading foreign intent through its thoughts until choice and command become indistinguishable. The target must make an Intelligence saving throw or be compelled to follow your spoken orders as if they were its own decisions.

While affected, the creature genuinely believes its actions are self-directed. A creature already under another compulsion effect automatically fails its initial saving throw. At the end of each of its turns, the creature may attempt a new Intelligence saving throw to reclaim control.

#### Veilward Bastion
*6th-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 10 minutess
**Range:** Self (30.0-foot radius)
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 hours

You raise a bastion of folded Veil in a 30-foot radius centered on yourself. For the duration, the area becomes warded against external interference.

Forced teleportation, extradimensional travel, scrying, and mind-altering effects originating from outside the area automatically fail. Attempts to manipulate reality within the ward also fail unless the source of the effect originates from a creature of higher level than you.

#### Verdict of the Forgotten
*6th-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You invoke a judgment long forgotten, compelling reality itself to erase the target. The target must make a Charisma saving throw. On a failure, they take 10d10 fire damage, and all creatures within 30 feet must make a Wisdom saving throw or be frightened for 1 minute.

If the target is reduced to 0 HP by this spell, their body disintegrates into nothing, and their existence is stricken from minor recorded history (casual memories fade, but deep records remain).

#### Viral Purge
*6th-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 10.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

All creatures in range are cured of diseases, infections, and parasitic infestations. If a creature is actively suffering from a necrotic or viral- based curse, this spell grants advantage on saving throws against it for the next 24 hours.

#### Wogar's Harvest of Haunting Onyx
*6th-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You call forth shards of haunting onyx, manifested through the parasitic agony of something older than time. Choose up to three creatures within range. Each target must make a Constitution saving throw.

On a failed save, the creature:
- Takes 5d10 fire damage, their essence siphoned and crystallized into flickering slivers of shadowy gemstone.
- Suffers disadvantage on death saving throws until the end of your next turn, as remnants of their soul splinter and drift.
- You regain hit points equal to half the total damage dealt across all targets.

On a successful save, the creature takes half damage and you gain no healing from them.
The Elders of the Concord Spire refuse to acknowledge The Spear of Forgotten Kings, calling it 'a mistake in the fabric of the world.' Yet, the forbidden archives tell another story.

#### Alerrim's Solitude
*7th-level Illusion*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 10.0 feet
**Components:** S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You overwhelm the senses of up to six creatures within range with a hallucinated scent so vivid and strange that it threatens their grip on reality. The scent can be chosen by you upon casting and changes the spell’s effect. You may also choose whether the scent feels directional or all- consuming. Affected creatures must make a Constitution saving throw or suffer the selected effect.

At the end of each of their turns, affected creatures must repeat the saving throw. On two failed saves, the target becomes Stunned until the end of their next turn as the olfactory hallucination overwhelms their nervous system.

Choose one scent effect upon casting:

Rot and Filth: Targets that fail their save are Poisoned and suffer disadvantage on saving throws against charm and fear effects for the duration .

Sweet Perfume: Targets must succeed on a Wisdom save or be Charmed by you until the end of that turn.

Burnt Ozone: On a failed save, targets cannot take reactions until the start of their next turn and The creature has disadvantage on Perception and Insight checks.

You may use a bonus action on your turn to change the scent’s directionality (e.g., from everywhere to a specific direction).

The illusion lingers for 1 minute, and affected creatures must repeat the saving throw at the end of each of their turns. On a success, the effect ends for them.

Condition Synergy: If a target is already Frightened, Charmed, or Poisoned when affected, it has disadvantage on the initial saving throw.

Obscured Battlefield: While under the spell’s effect, affected creatures are considered heavily obscured to others—they constantly shift position in reaction to the scent, creating a surreal mirage- like presence. This effect ends if the scent illusion ends.

Additionally, while the spell is active, you may use an action to cause the scent to mimic a recognizable compound—such as smoke, fuel, or blood—potentially triggering scent- based detection systems or distracting creatures with scent- based senses.

#### Dyrnar's Doom of Despair
*7th-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 10.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 4 hourss

You utter a word of terminal condemnation, binding a creature’s fate to a slow and inescapable unraveling.

Choose one creature within range. The target must make a Wisdom saving throw.

• Failure: The creature is Marked by Doom. Shadowed sigils manifest upon its flesh, and it becomes aware of the curse and the time remaining.

The creature will die in 4d8 + 12 hours. This death cannot be prevented by damage resistance, temporary hit points, or similar effects.

While Marked by Doom:

• The creature knows the remaining time with unsettling clarity.
• Dark sigils slowly spread across its body as the deadline approaches.

The doom may be postponed or ended only by one of the following:

• Curse Rejection: At the end of each long rest, the creature may repeat the Wisdom saving throw, ending the effect on a success.
• Deferral by Blood: If the creature kills a humanoid before the doom expires, the remaining duration is extended by 24 hours. This extension may occur only once.

If the doom is not ended or deferred, the creature dies when the duration expires.

• Success: The creature is unaffected.

#### Echoing Pulse of Time
*7th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You dislodge yourself from the stable flow of time, your form splitting into fleeting afterimages of paths taken and paths abandoned. Reality struggles to reconcile your presence as moments misalign around you.

For the duration, you are surrounded by shifting temporal echoes.

• Attack rolls against you are made with disadvantage, as your position flickers between instants.
• You may take one additional reaction each round.
• The first time each round that a creature misses you with an attack, it takes 3d8 force damage as the failed moment violently corrects itself.

Your movement leaves faint afterimages that vanish immediately and produce no additional effects.

When the spell ends, temporal inertia reasserts itself. Until the end of your next turn, your speed becomes 0, and you cannot take reactions.
| d6 Roll | Temporal Effect |
|--------- |------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ |
| 1–2 | Slowed Flow – Enemies within range have disadvantage on attack rolls against you until the start of your next turn. |
| 3–4 | Accelerated Momentum – You may take a second bonus action this turn. |
| 5 | Echo Step – You teleport up to 15 feet to a location you occupied on your last turn. |
| 6 | Temporal Mirror – A flickering afterimage of yourself performs the same action you just did (repeating your action once, targeting a different creature if possible; no additional cost). |

#### Edict of Imperial Suspension
*7th-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 reaction
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You invoke the Imperatum’s authority to stay the rise of hostile magic, halting a spell before it can fully manifest.

When a creature you can see within 60 feet begins casting a spell, you may use your reaction to impose an Imperial Suspension. The caster must make a Wisdom saving throw.

• Failure: The spell is suspended and does not take effect. Roll 1d4. After that many rounds, the suspended spell collapses harmlessly, and the spell slot or resources used to cast it are expended.

While suspended:

• The spell is considered active for the purpose of concentration.
• The caster may maintain concentration as normal.
• The caster is aware that the spell has been stayed.

• Success: The spell is cast normally.

You may have only one suspended spell at a time. If you suspend another spell, the previous suspension immediately ends and the stored spell collapses.

#### Edict of Obliterated Claim
*7th-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 10 minutess
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Permanent

You pronounce an Imperatum mandate that severs a creature from the frameworks of recognition that govern obligation, pursuit, and authority.

Choose one creature you can see within range. The target must make a Wisdom saving throw.

• Failure: For the duration, the creature becomes Unacknowledged.

While Unacknowledged:

• Creatures cannot willingly target the affected creature with attacks, spells, or abilities unless they first succeed on a Wisdom (Perception) check against your spell save DC. On a success, the effect is ignored for that interaction only.
• Effects that rely on designation, identification, or authority (such as marking, scrying, or compelled recognition) automatically fail against the target.
• The creature leaves no memorable impression in casual observation. Creatures that are not actively focusing on it may behave as though its presence is insignificant or easily forgotten.

This effect does not render the creature invisible, inaudible, or physically undetectable. It instead disrupts the mind’s capacity to assign significance or claim.

• Success: The target is unaffected.

A creature that successfully interacts with the Unacknowledged target is immune to this effect for the remainder of the spell’s duration.

#### Erasure of Pain
*7th-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 hours

You sever the mind’s ability to register suffering, drowning agony beneath unnatural resolve and impossible clarity.

Choose up to six creatures within range. For the duration:

• The creatures are immune to the Frightened condition.
• The creatures ignore the effects of exhaustion.

While under this spell, affected creatures no longer perceive pain, discomfort, or physical distress in a meaningful way. Wounds still bleed, bones may still break, and bodies may still fail, yet the mind registers no suffering. Crippling injuries feel distant, muted, or entirely unreal.

This altered state often produces unsettling behavior. Creatures may continue fighting through grievous harm, fail to recognize mortal danger, or react to injury with inappropriate calm, detachment, or euphoria. The spell does not compel such behavior, but it removes the natural sensory barriers that would normally discourage it.

• Creatures do not suffer disadvantage imposed by exhaustion levels.
• Exhaustion levels are not removed and resume their effects when the spell ends.

This spell does not restore hit points, remove conditions, or prevent damage.

When the spell ends, the body violently reconciles with deferred suffering. Each affected creature must succeed on a Constitution saving throw or gain one level of exhaustion.

#### Fire Meltdown
*7th-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self (90.0-foot radius)
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You rupture the containment of pyric forces, releasing a cataclysmic surge of annihilating heat that engulfs the area.

Each creature in the affected area must make a Dexterity saving throw.

• Failure: The creature takes 10d10 fire damage.
• Success: The creature takes half damage.

The heat destabilizes magical protections. Non-artifact magical effects of 6th level or lower within the area are suppressed until the start of your next turn. Magical objects are unaffected.

Creatures that fail the saving throw must also make a Constitution saving throw.

• Failure: The creature gains one level of exhaustion as searing exposure drains vitality.
• Success: No additional effect.

For 1 minute, the ground in the area is warped by residual heat and collapsing air currents. The area becomes difficult terrain, and creatures that end their turn there take 2d6 fire damage.

#### Flawless Diamond of Dread
*7th-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 bonus action
**Range:** 20.0 feet
**Components:** S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You raise a simple token between your fingers. For a breath it gleams with impossible perfection, refracting light like a flawless diamond. Then it fractures without sound, and dread answers the break.

A prismatic spike of psychic force lashes toward one creature within range. The target must make a Wisdom saving throw.

• Failure: The creature takes 9d8 psychic damage.
• Success: The creature takes half damage.

For 1 minute, the creature becomes internally fractured by refractive dread.

While affected:

• The creature cannot regain hit points until the start of your next turn.
• The creature emits faint distortions of light and sound. It gains no benefit from being Invisible.
• When the creature takes psychic, fire, or radiant damage, roll a d4. On a 1, half of that damage is reflected to a random creature within 10 feet (excluding the original source).

If this spell reduces the creature to 0 hit points, its body disintegrates into dust-fine crystalline fragments. In its place remains a single flawed diamond worth 100 gp.

Those who survive often describe a lingering dissonance: their shadow hesitates a fraction too long.

#### Formula of Unraveling
*7th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 120.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You inscribe a destabilizing axiom into a creature’s vital pattern, compelling its structure to turn against itself.

Choose one creature within range that you can see. The target must make a Constitution saving throw.

• Failure: The creature takes 12d12 psychic damage, becomes Altered for the duration, and gains vulnerability to one damage type of your choice (chosen when the spell is cast).

• Success: The creature takes half damage and suffers no additional effects.

⸻

Altered State

While Altered:

• The creature’s form flickers with subtle distortions
• It has disadvantage on Constitution saving throws
• It gains vulnerability to the chosen damage type

The creature may repeat the saving throw at the end of each of its turns, ending the Altered state on a success.

⸻

What fractures is not merely flesh, but the unseen logic that once held the creature whole.

#### Giocrin's Incantation of Bitterness
*7th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You whisper a fractured syllable of corrosive significance, branding a creature with a metaphysical wound that reshapes how it suffers harm.

Choose one creature within range. The target must make a Charisma saving throw.

⸻

Failure

The creature is cursed for the duration.

• Choose bludgeoning or slashing damage when the spell is cast. The creature gains vulnerability to the chosen damage type.

• Whenever the creature takes damage of that type, it must succeed on a Constitution saving throw or gain one level of exhaustion.

• If the creature gains three levels of exhaustion from this spell, the wound deepens:

 – The creature loses any resistance it possesses to the chosen damage type
 – Attack rolls dealing the chosen damage type have advantage against it

These deepened effects last for the spell’s duration.

⸻

Success

The creature resists the incantation and is unaffected.

⸻

Duration: Until dispelled.

The curse ends only when removed by greater restoration, remove curse cast at 5th level or higher, or comparable magic at the GM’s discretion.

⸻

The wound is rarely visible. Flesh yields too easily. Impacts linger too long. The body learns, unwillingly, the shape of its new fragility.
At the start of each of your turns, roll a d6 to determine the temporal echo:
1–2. Slowed Flow – Enemies within range have disadvantage on attack rolls against you until the start of your next turn.
3–4. Accelerated Momentum – You may take a second bonus action this turn.
5. Echo Step – You teleport up to 15 feet to a location you occupied on your last turn.
6. Temporal Mirror – A flickering afterimage of yourself performs the same action you just did (repeating your action once, targeting a different creature if possible; no additional cost).

#### Incantation of Viridian Determination
*7th-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You invoke a forgotten rite of relentless vitality, binding a creature’s thread into a defiant knot of endurance. A faint viridian shimmer haunts the edges of perception, glimpsed only in reflections and peripheral vision.

Choose yourself or one creature you can see within range. For the duration, the target is sustained by unnatural resolve.

• The first time the creature would be reduced to 0 hit points, it instead regains 3d10 + your spellcasting ability modifier hit points. The creature immediately stands if it was prone, without expending movement.

• Until the end of the creature’s next turn after this restoration, it cannot be reduced below 1 hit point by damage.

• Until the restoration is triggered, the creature has advantage on saving throws against effects that would impose the Unconscious or Paralyzed conditions.

• Allies within 10 feet of the target have advantage on saving throws against being Frightened, Paralyzed, or Charmed.

Once the restoration effect is triggered, the spell immediately ends.

If the spell ends without the restoration being triggered, the viridian energies dissipate harmlessly, leaving only a subtle afterimage within reflective surfaces.

Duration: Concentration, up to 1 minute.

#### Litany of Flesh
*7th-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You recite a forceful litany that purges strain, affliction, and decay from a creature’s body, violently restoring physiological balance.

Choose one creature you can see within range. The target gains the following benefits:

• All levels of exhaustion are removed
• The creature regains 50 hit points
• One curse, disease, or madness affecting the creature ends (your choice)

The restoration disrupts recent cognition. The target forgets the last hour of its experiences, including events, conversations, and perceptions. This memory loss cannot be prevented by immunity to charm, fear, or similar effects.

This spell has no effect on constructs or undead.

#### Looming Obsidian of Anarchy
*7th-level Illusion*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You conjure a towering shard of dark obsidian that hovers at a point you can see within range. The shard occupies no space, emits no light, and is intangible, yet it is clearly visible. Its presence weighs upon the mind rather than the world.

Choose up to five creatures you can see within range when the shard appears. A chosen creature is affected for the spell’s duration.

Oppressive Vision
At the start of each affected creature’s turn, it must make an Intelligence saving throw:

• Failure:
– The creature takes 6d6 psychic damage.
– It has disadvantage on Intelligence, Wisdom, and Charisma ability checks until the end of its turn.
– If the save fails by 5 or more, the creature gains the Paranoid condition until the spell ends.

• Success:
– The creature takes half damage.
– No additional effects apply that turn.

A creature that cannot see the shard is unaffected for as long as it lacks sight of it.

Fracturing Pulse
At the end of each of your turns, the shard violently intrudes upon one affected creature of your choice that failed its saving throw since the end of your last turn:

• The creature takes 3d6 psychic damage.
• It must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw or become Frightened of the shard until the end of its next turn.

#### Mnemonic Fortress
*7th-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 minutes
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 24 hourss

You fortify the mind of a creature against forced memory alterations, cognitive tampering, and external data manipulation.
 
- The target becomes immune to Memory Fragmentation, A.S.T.R.A.L. Redaction, and similar effects.
- Any attempt to modify their memory fails outright, and the caster of the effect must make a Wisdom saving throw or suffer 5d8 psychic damage.
- The target also remembers everything perfectly for 24 hours, with a near- photographic recall of events.

#### Obsolescence
*7th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You mark a creature as obsolete, and reality enforces the correction. The target must make a Constitution saving throw. On a failure, it takes 10d10 bludgeoning damage and suffers disadvantage on all attack rolls and ability checks for 1 minute. If the creature has legendary resistances, it must expend one to automatically succeed.

#### Perfect Restoration
*7th-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You rewrite the body’s present state to match its intended form. The target regains all hit points and has all lost limbs and organs fully restored.

If the creature is suffering from mutation, deformity, or anomalous alteration, the spell attempts to return the body to its original, uncorrupted state, ending such effects where possible. This restoration does not resurrect the dead but fully repairs the living.

#### Reality Sidestep
*7th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You exist half inside reality, half outside of it. While active:
- You can pass through walls and barriers as long as they are not magical.
- You gain resistance to all physical damage.
- You leave behind a blurred, static afterimage that lingers for 6 seconds before catching up.

#### Rebuild Reality
*7th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You restore a destroyed or corrupted location (up to 1,000 square feet) to a prior state. This includes buildings, roads, and technological structures—but not living creatures. The restored state must have existed within the last 100 years, and anomalies within the area may resist reconstruction.

#### Restored Order
*7th-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You impose absolute order upon a creature whose existence has been bent, corrupted, or overridden. All effects that compel allegiance, dominate will, distort reality, or impose external control upon the target immediately end.

This spell removes all forms of magical mind control, possession, forced devotion, and imposed identity. Madness, paranoia, and supernatural trauma affecting the creature are fully cured. If the creature is possessed, overwritten, or controlled by another entity, that entity must succeed on a Charisma saving throw or be violently expelled from the target at once.

When cast using a 9th-level spell slot, this effect instead applies to all willing creatures of your choice within a 30-foot radius.

#### Reweaving of the False Thread
*7th-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 hours
**Range:** 10.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Permanent

You seize a creature’s thread and forcibly pass it back through the Loom, overwriting identity, memory, and purpose. The target must make a Wisdom saving throw. On a failure, its former self is erased from conscious recall, replaced with a fully formed false identity sanctioned by higher recognition.

The creature believes this new life to be authentic and continuous, accepting fabricated history and status as truth. Attempts to restore the original thread fail, unless magic of the highest order is used to unravel and reweave what has been imposed.

#### Skin Unwoven
*7th-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You weave an invisible suture in the air, connecting it to the target’s flesh and nerves. The thread does not cut, it unravels, pulling the skin away in delicate layers.

- The target must make a Constitution saving throw. On a failure, their flesh begins to separate from their body, piece by piece.
- Round 1: Their fingertips and lips begin to curl and peel, exposing raw flesh.
- Round 2: The skin along their arms and jaw pulls loose, hanging like discarded parchment.
- Round 3: Their entire face and chest are stripped, leaving only muscle and exposed nerves.

- The target takes 4d10 fire damage per round and suffers disadvantage on all Dexterity- based actions due to agony.
- If the spell lasts the full minute, the target is left entirely skinless, a raw, quivering thing, forced to exist in constant, unbearable sensation.

Skinless Condition: 
- The creature has disadvantage on all saving throws against pain, stun, or fear effects. 
- They are vulnerable to pyric and radiation damage. 
- They cannot benefit from healing spells other than *Reconstructive Audit* or *First Responder Algorithm* until ritually treated. 
- They are permanently disfigured, unless magically or surgically restored. 

End of the Spell: 
- The target may repeat the Constitution save at the end of each of their turns. On a success, the unweaving halts but does not reverse—what has been lost remains lost. 
- If the spell is cast multiple times on the same target, their skin may begin to regrow incorrectly, forming anomalous grafts that twitch and whisper in forgotten tongues.

#### Struck from the Loom
*7th-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Permanent

You sever a creature’s thread from the Loom of recognition, unweaving their presence from all sanctioned records and registries maintained by the Erelian Erudits. Names, credentials, holdings, and proofs of standing dissolve as though they were never woven.

The target must make an Intelligence saving throw. On a failure, they are treated as a non-entity by all institutions, authorities, and systems of recognition. Doors do not open for them, claims do not acknowledge them, and obligations cannot be formally applied, as their thread no longer appears in the Loom’s accounted weave.

#### Thallan's Septic Mandala
*7th-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes


You conjure an arcane seal of forgotten syllables—a 15- foot- radius circle inscribed with runes that shimmer like powdered saffron. The circle centers on you and moves with you. For the duration:

- Allied creatures within the circle gain a +5 bonus to damage on all weapon and spell attacks targeting enemies outside the circle. This damage is impact type and manifests as reverberating glyphs striking in tandem with the blow. 
- If this spell was cast using your final remaining spell slot, this bonus increases to +10, and the runes emit a low harmonic tone audible only to allies. 
- Enemies who enter or begin their turn within the circle must succeed on a Charisma saving throw or suffer disadvantage on all melee attacks until the start of their next turn. 
- Any creature affected by a Condition (such as Paranoid, Compelled, or Frightened) takes an additional 1d6 psychic damage when hit by attacks made from within the circle.

#### The Spear of Forgotten Kings
*7th-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You conjure a colossal spectral spear—a jagged relic made from the reigns of long- erased monarchs and the regrets that bound them. The spear surges forward in a straight line up to 120 feet long and 5 feet wide.

All creatures in the area must make a Constitution saving throw. On a failure, a creature takes 6d10 fire damage. A creature reduced to 0 hit points by this spell has its soul torn from memory and imprisoned within a spectral throne—unable to be resurrected or contacted by any means short of a *Wish* or *Sovereign Accord*.

Success: A creature takes half damage and is not affected by the soul imprisonment effect.

While affected by this spell:
- The area traversed by the spear echoes faintly with overlapping royal decrees in unknown tongues. 
- Any creature standing within 10 feet of the line for the next minute suffers disadvantage on Charisma checks, as their voice seems small and forgotten. 
- You may sense the presence of monarchic or noble bloodlines within range for 1 round, as they resonate with the spear’s memory.
The Veil Market traders whisper of an artifact that contains The Spear of Forgotten Kings—a single black page that cannot be burned, torn, or marked. Those who read it vanish, leaving behind only the scent of ink and decay.

#### Tortak's Siphon of Haunting Moss
*7th-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** None
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You release a parasitic curse woven from the hunger of haunted moss. Choose a point within range. Any number of creatures within a 15- foot- radius sphere centered on that point must make a Constitution saving throw.

On a failed save:
- For the duration, the next 45 hit points of healing the target would receive are stolen. Instead of regaining hit points, you regain that amount instead, and the target receives nothing.
- Each time this transfer occurs, spectral moss visibly spreads along the target’s skin or clothing.
- While affected, targets have disadvantage on Constitution saving throws to maintain concentration on spells.

On a success:
- The creature is unaffected, but faint lichen- like patterns momentarily crawl across their skin before vanishing.

The spell ends early for a creature when it has had 45 HP of healing siphoned, when it drops to 0 hit points, or if you lose concentration.

#### Yarol's Solitude
*7th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 reaction
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V
**Duration:** 1 rounds

As poison takes hold of a creature, you interject a fragment of forgotten transmutation—an ancient algorithm embedded in the bones of the world. The poison twists, sharpens, and magnifies into something far more insidious.

When a creature within range becomes poisoned, you may use your reaction to invoke Yarol’s Solitude. That creature must make a Constitution saving throw.

- On a failure, the poison mutates into a paralytic toxin. The creature becomes paralyzed for 1d3 rounds, instead of poisoned. Their body stiffens in place, overwhelmed by the sudden chemical transformation.
- On a success, the creature resists paralysis, but the altered poison still takes hold. They are slowed for 1d3 rounds, and remain poisoned. While slowed, they cannot take reactions and their movement speed is halved.

#### Bloom Canker
*8th-level Necromancy*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 120.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You trigger a catastrophic surge of malignant growth within a 20-foot-radius sphere centered on a point you can see within range. Flesh destabilizes, tissues proliferate uncontrollably, and the ground erupts with cancerous masses.

Each creature in the area must make a Constitution saving throw.

• Failure: The creature takes 8d10 poison damage and becomes Mutated for 1 minute.
• Success: The creature takes half damage and is not Mutated.

The affected area becomes difficult terrain for the duration as tumorous growths, fibrous protrusions, and pulsating tissue choke movement. The terrain remains for 1 minute.

While Mutated, a creature’s form is violently distorted by uncontrolled outgrowths:

• The creature’s speed is reduced by 10 feet.
• The creature has disadvantage on Dexterity checks and Dexterity saving throws.
• At the start of each of its turns, the creature takes 1d10 poison damage as its body strains under the instability.

A Mutated creature may repeat the Constitution saving throw at the end of each of its turns, ending the condition on a success.

If this spell is cast in an area of dense construction or reinforced infrastructure, lingering organic masses partially fuse with surfaces. These alterations are cosmetic and environmental unless the GM rules otherwise.

#### Chronoseal
*8th-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 hours

You inscribe a sigil of absolute temporal authority, binding a creature, object, or discrete structure within a suspension of arrested moments.

Choose one creature, object, or non-magical structure or object of Large size or smaller within range. The target is placed in perfect stasis for the duration.

While under the seal:

• The target is Incapacitated and its speed becomes 0.
• The target does not age, decay, or undergo any physical change.
• The target is immune to all damage.
• The target cannot be moved, manipulated, or affected by external effects.
• The target cannot take actions, reactions, or perceive the passage of time.

The sealed target remains visibly present and occupies its space normally. Effects that would interact with it automatically fail.

When the spell ends, the target resumes its state exactly as it was at the moment of sealing, with no awareness that time has passed.

Sealing sentient beings imposes severe metaphysical strain. Repeated or reckless use of such magic may invite unintended consequences at the GM’s discretion.

#### Concord of Dissonant Hearts
*8th-level Enchantment*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You impose a fleeting concord upon conflicting wills, forcing discordant minds into a moment of shared understanding. Creatures of your choice within range must make a Charisma saving throw.

• Failure: The creature is overcome by enforced empathy for the duration.
• Success: The creature is unaffected.

While affected, a creature is bound by the concord:

• The creature cannot make attacks, cast spells that deal damage, or take actions with the intent to directly harm another creature.
• The creature may still move, speak, take non-harmful actions, and flee normally.
• If the creature takes damage from a source other than itself, it may repeat the Charisma saving throw at the end of its turn, ending the effect on a success.

Creatures affected by the concord experience involuntary flashes of shared memory and emotional context from those around them, chosen by the GM. These impressions are fleeting and carry no mechanical effect, but may influence behavior or dialogue during the spell’s duration.

The spell ends early for a creature if it succeeds on a subsequent saving throw.

#### Conflagration of Unbound Force
*8th-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Instantaneous

You trigger a violent release of raw, unshaped power at a point you can see within range. The detonation collapses outward in a 20-foot-radius sphere, battering creatures with overwhelming kinetic violence. Each creature in the area must make a Dexterity saving throw.

• Failure: The creature takes 12d10 bludgeoning damage and is hurled up to 30 feet directly away from the center of the blast.
• Success: The creature takes half damage and is not moved.

A creature hurled by this spell stops early if it collides with a solid surface. If it strikes an obstacle, it takes an additional 1d6 bludgeoning damage for every 10 feet of movement prevented.

For 1 minute, the affected area remains visibly distorted. Colors refract unnaturally, spatial relations appear subtly misaligned, and weight distribution behaves erratically. The area is considered difficult terrain for the duration as creatures struggle to navigate the unstable environment.

#### Crown Weighing of Merit
*8th-level Divination*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You invoke a sovereign reckoning that does not condemn, but measures. Up to six creatures of your choice within range are subjected to the unseen scales of the Crown and found worthy.

For the duration, each affected creature’s resolve is fortified by recognition:

• The creature has advantage on saving throws against being Charmed or Frightened.
• Once per round, when the creature misses with an attack roll or fails an ability check, it may roll 1d10 and add the result to the roll, potentially turning failure into success.
• If the creature would be reduced to 0 hit points, it instead drops to 1 hit point and cannot die until the start of its next turn.

This preservation reflects suspended finality rather than protection. It does not prevent damage, unconsciousness, or subsequent harm.

A creature may benefit from the 1d10 adjustment only once per round.

#### Edict of Absolute Finality
*8th-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Self (60.0-foot sphere)
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You invoke the Imperatum’s supreme mandate, projecting an aura of sovereign authority that reality itself hesitates to defy.

An aura of decree radiates from you in a 30-foot radius for the duration.

Creatures of your choice within the aura must make a Wisdom saving throw.

• Failure: The creature becomes a non-actor for the duration. A non-actor  cannot take hostile actions, including making attacks, casting harmful spells, or using abilities that directly inflict damage.
• Success: The creature is unaffected.

Within the aura:

• Suppression of Manifestations: Summoned creatures, conjured entities, and extraplanar manifestations must succeed on a Charisma saving throw at the start of their turn or be dismissed to their point of origin.
• Dulled Supernatural Effects: Magical effects of 6th level or lower originating within the aura are suppressed while inside it. Such effects resume when they leave the area.

This edict does not dispel magic, but imposes temporary compliance.

#### Final Seal of Denial
*8th-level Abjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You impose a sovereign interdiction upon a creature’s vital thread, barring all ordinary paths of recovery.

Choose one creature within range that you can see. The target must make a Charisma saving throw.

• Failure: For the duration, the creature cannot regain hit points by any means, including magic, regeneration, or restorative effects. Temporary hit points function normally.

The creature is immune to effects that would remove conditions, restore ability scores, or end diseases or curses.

If the creature dies while under this seal:

• The body and all physical remains immediately vanish
• The creature cannot be restored to life by resurrection or revival magic
• Only reality-altering magic of the highest order can reverse this fate

• Success: The spell fails and has no effect.

#### Flesh to Paper
*8th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** Touch
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Permanent

Forbidden alterations cling to this spell, as though its structure remembers hands that no longer exist.

Choose one creature within range. The target must make a Constitution saving throw.

• Failure: The creature is transformed into a lifeless parchment scroll for the duration.

While transformed:

• The creature becomes an object and is Incapacitated.
• The scroll has AC 12 and hit points equal to the creature’s current hit points.
• The scroll is immune to poison and psychic damage.
• The creature is unaware of its surroundings and cannot act.
• The scroll is Tiny and weighs almost nothing.

If the scroll is reduced to 0 hit points, the creature dies.

• Success: The creature resists the transformation and is unaffected.

Duration: Concentration, up to 1 minute.

When the spell ends, the creature returns to its normal form in the space the scroll occupied, retaining its previous hit points.

#### Fleshbound Chronicle
*8th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

You bind a creature’s lived experience into its own flesh, forcing memory, sensation, and identity to rewrite themselves as a suffering ledger.

Choose one creature within range that you can see. The target must make a Wisdom saving throw.

• Failure: The creature becomes Incapacitated for the duration as its mind and senses are overwhelmed by the transcription.

While affected:

• The creature mutters fractured recollections, speaking distorted fragments of its own memories.
• You may ask up to three questions. The creature must answer truthfully to the best of its knowledge, though responses may be incomplete or impressionistic.
• The creature has no awareness of its surroundings beyond vague sensation.

At the end of each of its turns, the creature may repeat the saving throw, ending the effect on a success.

⸻

Death of the Subject

If the creature dies while under this spell, its body transforms into a Fleshbound Codex.

The codex:

• Is a Medium object
• Has AC 13 and 40 hit points
• Is immune to poison and psychic damage
• Contains impressions of the creature’s memories

A creature studying the codex for at least 10 minutes may attempt an Intelligence (Investigation) check against your spell save DC to extract a coherent memory, fact, or emotional truth from the archive.

Creatures that remain within 10 feet of the codex for more than 1 minute experience faint emotional echoes but suffer no mechanical effects.

#### Fragmentation Rift
*8th-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 150.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You tear open a violent dimensional discontinuity at a point in space.

Choose an unoccupied point you can see within range. A thrashing rift of fractured force manifests there, distorting nearby space for the duration.

When the rift appears, and whenever a creature enters the area for the first time on a turn or starts its turn there, each creature within a 20-foot-radius sphere centered on the rift must make a Dexterity saving throw.

• Failure: The creature takes 14d10 force damage as spatial fractures shear through its body.

• Success: The creature takes half damage.

Any creature reduced to 0 hit points by this damage is torn into the rift and removed from the battlefield, leaving behind no physical remains. Only magic capable of interplanar retrieval or equivalent intervention can restore such a creature, at the GM’s discretion.

The rift is violently unstable and collapses at the end of your next turn.

#### Fraying of the Loom
*8th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 60.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

You destabilize a creature’s existential thread, pulling it partially free from the Loom that anchors reality.

Choose one creature within range. The target must make a Charisma saving throw.

On a failure, the creature flickers between incompatible states of being for the duration.

While affected:

• Attack rolls against the creature are made with advantage
• The creature’s attack rolls are made with disadvantage
• The creature has disadvantage on ability checks and saving throws

The creature’s form wavers visibly, its presence uncertain and misaligned with the world.

On a success, the creature resists the fraying and suffers no effect.

#### Man ↔ Cock
*8th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 10 minutess

Man ↔ Cock
8th-level Transmutation

You impose a highly specific transformation upon the boundary between humanoid and fowl.

Choose one humanoid creature or one Tiny beast of the bird family that you can see within range.

Unwilling Target

An unwilling humanoid must make a Constitution saving throw.

• Failure: The creature is transformed for the duration.
• Success: The spell has no effect.

A transformed creature may repeat the saving throw at the end of each of its turns, ending the effect on a success.

Willing Target

A willing creature is transformed without a saving throw.

A bird targeted by this spell is always considered willing.

⸻

Forms

• Humanoid to Rooster
The creature transforms into a Tiny beast (rooster) with:

– 1 hit point
– Speed 10 ft
– Peck attack (1 damage, no proficiency)
– No ability to speak or cast spells

The creature retains its alignment, personality, and awareness, but its mental ability scores are replaced by those of the beast. It behaves as a normal, notably aggressive rooster at the GM’s discretion.

• Rooster to Humanoid
The creature transforms into a Medium humanoid of a general appearance chosen by the caster.

The humanoid:

– Possesses basic clothing
– Cannot recall its time as a bird
– Has no equipment or class features

⸻

Duration & Reversal

The caster may end the spell early as an action.

Casting this spell on a creature already transformed by it immediately reverts the target.

⸻

Blood Pact Amplification

If the spell is cast using a Vitality + Unique Offering blood pact, the transformation becomes permanent.

A permanent transformation may only be reversed by effects capable of undoing major transmutations, such as Greater Restoration, Remove Curse, or Wish, subject to GM adjudication.
Rooster Traits:

- Crowing: Emits a deafening *COCK- A- DOODLE- DOO!* once per hour.
- Aggressive: Will charge anything larger than it.
- Peck: Melee Weapon Attack, +3 to hit, 1 slashing damage.

#### Paradox of Endless Petition
*8th-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 minutes
**Range:** 30.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** Permanent

You consign a creature to an infinite cycle of royal petition and review, trapping their mind in an unresolvable appeal before unseen authority. The target must make a Wisdom saving throw. On a failure, they are unable to act for 1d10 days, convinced they are endlessly submitting requests, attending hearings, and awaiting judgments that never arrive. To the victim, time appears to pass normally, yet every attempt to act is deferred to a higher review that is always pending.

*8th-level Evocation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action

You invoke a catastrophic descent of raw pyric power, calling down Ragna’s fury in an uncontrolled discharge that ruptures the world’s tolerance for heat and force.

The eruption scours everything within its reach, overwhelming defenses and unraveling protective workings as blazing energy floods the area. When the light fades, the ground remains hostile and poisoned with lingering heat, a scar upon the land that warns all who approach that the fire has not finished remembering.

#### Seal of Severed Passage
*8th-level Conjuration*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 120.0 feet
**Components:** V, S

You impose a sovereign seal upon an area within a 60-foot radius, isolating it from the rest of reality. For the duration, no creature can enter or leave the area by teleportation, portals, or extradimensional movement.

The boundary is invisible and cannot be perceived or interacted with from outside. Creatures of overwhelming presence may attempt to destabilize the seal, testing its authority through sheer force of will.

#### Seam Ripper of the Living World
*8th-level Transmutation*
**Casting Time:** 1 action
**Range:** 120.0 feet
**Components:** V, S
**Duration:** 1 minutes

Reality was stitched together for convenience. You simply choose to pull at the thread.
You target a location within range and unravel the physical rules governing that terrain. For the duration, the area becomes Sutured Terrain:

- Matter Becomes Pliable – Stone flows like fabric. Walls bulge and flex. Ground can ripple like water underfoot. All movement is halved unless the creature succeeds a Strength saving throw at the start of its turn.
- Gravity Buckles – Gravity shifts every round. Roll 1d4:

Objects Drift Apart – Doors fall off frames. Windows become free- floating. Anchored structures must pass a DC 18 Constitution saving throw each round or begin to unravel into ambient material.
- Creatures Warped by Terrain – At the end of each round, any creature in the area must succeed a Constitution saving throw or gain a random minor mutation (DM’s discretion). Mutations last until the end of their next long rest.
| d4 | Gravity Effect |
|---- |--------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| 1 | Gravity reverses. Non- anchored creatures fall upward. |
| 2 | Gravity pulls sideways. Creatures are dragged 10 feet to the left. |
| 3 | Gravity flattens. Jumping is impossible, all creatures feel compressed. |
| 4 | Gravity vanishes. Creatures float, gaining a flying speed equal to half their walking speed. |
